Language: Amazigh Translator: Ramdane At Mansour - At Mensur
سُوۡرَةُ الۡفَاتِحَةِ S yisem n Öebbi, Aênin Ipêunun, Ccekôan i Öebbi, Mass imavalen, Aênin Ipêunun, Agellid n wass iqeîîiyen. D Keçç ay naâbed, d Keçç ay nepper d Amâ²iwen; Awi ya$ d ubrid iweqmen, Abrid n wid i T$atev; ur n wid i K isserfayen, ne$ n im$eôôqen.
سُوۡرَةُ البَقَرَةِ Alm. Appan Tezmamt, ur degs ccekk, d nnhaya i wid ipêezziben; wid iumnen s tbavnit, ipéallan, ipseddiqen seg wayen iten N$at; wid iumnen s wayen i k d irsen, akked wayen id irsen, uqbel ik, u, $ef laxeôt, nitni, pputebbten. Widak, di nnhaya n Mass nnsen, widak, d isaâdiyen. Wid ijehlen, s tidep, iâuva fellasen ma tnubav ten, ne$ ur ten tnubav. Ur ppamnen. Isle$ Öebbi ulawen nnsen, akked imeééu$en nnsen. Irs le$yaô $ef allen nnsen. Fellasen aâaqeb abarar. Ger yimdanen, llan wid iqqaôen: "numen s Öebbi akked wass aneggaru”; nitni, ur llin d lmumnin. La xedâen Öebbi akked wid iumnen. Ur xedâen siwa iman nnsen, ur faqen. Aîan deg ulawen nnsen; Irna yasen Öebbi aîan. Fellasen aâaqeb aqeôêan, ilmend n wayen skiddiben. Ma nnan asen: "ur ssefsadet di tmurt"! A d inin: "nekwni d wid, kan, ipleqqimen". Day maççi d nitni, s tidep, ay d ifessaden, maca ur faqen? Ma nnan asen: "amnet, akken umnen medden"! A d inin: "day a namen, akken umnen ije$lufen"? Day maççi d nitni, s tidep, ay d ije$lufen, maca ur éôin. Ma mmugren d wid iumnen, ad inin: "numen". Mara yilin weêêedsen, ar ccwaîen nnsen, ad inin: "nekwni yidwen! Nekwni la nettihi kan". Öebbi ad Ittihi fellasen. Isnerna yasen lbwe$v nnsen; ddebdeben. Widak, d wid iu$en ttelfan s nnhaya; ur d issasay ssuq nnsen, ur pwanhan. Tevôa yidsen am win issa$en times. Mi tnewweô ayen i s d izzin, Öebbi Iddem tafat nnsen, Iooa ten di tillas, ur pwalin. Âaégen, gugmen, dre$len; ihi, nitni ur d ppu$alen s abrid. Ne$ am usigna igenni, degs tillas, tirmegt, lebôaq. Pparran ivudan nnsen deg imeééu$en nnsen, mgal ssiâqat; ad nnestaôen si tmeppant. Öebbi Izzi i ijehliyen. Qôib i sen iêwi lebôaq, iéôi. Yal tikelt ideg i sen icâal, ad ddun syis. Mi sen ixsi, ad êebsen. Ma ihwa yaS i Öebbi, ad asen Ikkes timesliwt akked yiéôi nnsen. Öebbi, s tidep, Izmer i yal cci. A yimdanen! Âabdet Mass nnwen ikwen Ixelqen, kunwi, akked wid i kwen id izwaren, amar a pêezzbem; i wen Irran tamurt d usu, igenni d lebni; id Isse$li d aman seg igenni, Issuffe$ ed yissen ppemôa, d ôôeéq i kunwi. Ihi, ur pparrat tanudda i Öebbi, u kunwi teéôam. Ma tellam di ccekk, $ef wayen id Nessers ar umdan nne£, awit ed tasuôep i p icban. Neccdet ed inagan nnwen, war Öebbi, ma tessawalem tidep. Ma ur tessawvem, u, war ccekk, ur tessawavem, êezzbet i tmes isseô$an imdanen, id$a$en, ippuheggan i ijehliyen. Becceô wid iumnen, u xeddmen ayen ilhan, ar i nitni, leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen. Yal tikelt ara ppuôeéqen, si ppemôa nnsen, ad inin: "d aya is neppuôeéq, uqbel". Ippunefk asen i ten icban. Din, jjwao nnsen d ayen iûfan. Degsen ad wekkôen. Ih, ur Ikukra ara Öebbi, a d Ifk amedya n tizip, ne$ ip i$elben. Wid iumnen éôan neppa d tidep, s$uô Mass nnsen. Wanag wid ijehlen qqaôen: "acu Ib$a Öebbi s umedya agi"? Yis, Itellif aîas; yis, Inehhu aîas. Ur Itellif yis, siwa iballa$en; wid ipôuéun lemâahda n Öebbi, deffir lmitaq iS, issemfaôaqen ayen id Iumeô Öebbi ad imlil, issefsaden di tmurt. Widak d imexsuôen. Amek ara tnekôem Öebbi? Tellam temmuten, Issader kwen id. Sinna, a kwen Ine$, sinna, a kwen id Issider, sinna, $uôeS a ppu$alem. D Neppa i wen Ixelqen ayen akw illan di tmurt; sinna, Izzi ar igenni, Iwqem it d ûa igenwan. Neppa, Issen yal cci. Mi Inna Mass ik, i lmalayek: "Nek ad Rre$ aneûûaf di tmurt". Nnant aS: "day a Pperrev, degs, win ara isfesden degs, ara izzizlen idamen? Wanag, nekwenti nesbuccuâ K s ccekôan, u Neôôequ yaK". Inna: "Nek, èôi$ ayen ur teéôimt". Isseêfev akw ismawen i Adem. Sinna, Issken iten i lmalayek, Inna: "efkemt iyI d ismawen n wigi, ma kunemti d sut tidep". Nnant: "gedha s yisseK! Ur nessin, siwa i a$ Teslemdev. Keçç, s tidep, d Amusnaw, d Bab n ûûwab". Inna: "a Adem, efk asent ismawen nnsen". Mi sent imla ismawen nnsen, Inna: "day ur a kwent Nni$ ara: Nek Ssne$ tabavnit n tmurt akked igenwan, u èôi$ ayen d teqqaôem, akked wayen teppeffrem"? Mi Nenna i lmalayek: "knumt i Adem"! Knant, siwa Iblis. Iugi, u isme$weô iman is. Illa seg ijehliyen. Nenna: "a Adem, ezde$ keçç akked tmeîîut ik, di Loennet, eççet segs, s tawant, ayen i wen ihwan. Ur ppaéet ar ttejôa yagi, mulac a ppilim d imednas". Ikellex iten Cciîan fellas. Issuffe$ iten id seg wanda llan. Nenna: "ûûubbet, d icenga bbwaygarawen. I kunwi, di tmurt, i$imi akked zzhu, siwa tallit". Adem iîîef awalen n Mass is. Issuref as. Neppa, s tidep, Issuruf, Ipêunu. Nenna: "ûûubbet segs, akken ma tellam. War ccekk, a kwen id tas nnhaya s$uôI". Wid iddan d nnhaya, ur ppagwaden, ur $weblen. Wid ijehlen u skaddben issekniyen nne£, widak d at tmes, degs ad wekkôen. A yAt Isôail! Mmektit ed l$it iW, is ikwen Öeéqe$. Eîîfet di lemâahda W, ad Ïîfe$ di lemâahda nnwen. D nek iwumi ara têezzbem. Amnet s wayen id Sserse$, itebbten ayen illan $uôwen. Ur ppilit d imezwura ara t iagwin. Ur ppa$et, s issekniyen iW, ayen ôxisen. D nek iwumi ara têezzbem. Ur slusut, i tidep, tikerkas. Ur teffret tidep, u kunwi teéôam. èéallet, zekkit, îîinzet akked wid iîîinizen. Day a ppamôem ise$ i medden, a ppeppum iman nnwen? U kunwi teqqaôem Tazmamt. Day ur tefhimem ara? Ssutret lemâawna n ûûbeô akked téallit. Ih, dayen iwaâôen, siwa i imeéluven, wid iêûan ar ad mlilen akked Mass nnsen, u $uôeS, nitni, war ccekk, ad u$alen. A yAt Isôail! Mmektit ed l$it iW, is ikwen Öeéqe$. Nek, Smenyafe$ kwen i imavalen. Ëezzbet i wass ideg ur ippuoazi yiwen deg umkan n wayev, s wacemma. Ur tepwaqbal ccafuâa segs, ur tepwaîîaf, segs, le$ôama, ur ten ppaâwanen. Mi kwen Nsellek seg ugdud n Ferâun, sâaddayen fellawen aâaqeb adiran. Zellun arrac nnwen, ssidiren tilawin nnwen. Ayagi d taluft tabarart, s$uô Mass nnwen. Mi, yiswen, Nessemfaôeq ill, Nsellek ikwen, Ne$meq agdud n Ferâun, kunwi la tepwalim. Mi Nga lemâahda i Musa, kuéet wavan; sinna, deffir es, teddam d uâajmi. Kunwi d imednas. Sinna, deffir waya, Nsemmeê awen, amar a ppesnemmrem. Mi Nefka, i Musa, Tazmamt akked ufraz, amar a ppeppwanhum. Mi inna Musa i ugdud is: "a yagdud iw! Kunwi, s tidep, tdensem iman nnwen, mi teddam d uâajmi. Ssutret ssmaê i Uxellaq nnwen; mmin$et, ppif i kunwi ar Uxellaq nnwen. Issuref awen. Neppa, s tidep, Issuruf, Ipêunu". Mi tennam: "a Musa! Ur neppamen yisek, d awez$i, alamma nwala Öebbi, âinani". Tewwet ikwen id ssiâqa, kunwi tepwalim. Sinna, Nerra kwen id, deffir tmeppant nnwen, amar a ppesnemmrem. S usigna, Nerra yawen tili. Nessers awen d lmenna, ifeôôuoen: "eççet si téidanin is ikwen N$at". Ur a£ dnisen, maca densen iman nnsen. Mi Nenna: "kecmet tamdint agi, eççet degs, s tawant, ayen i wen ihwan; kecmet si tebburt, s lekni; init: nendem. Ad awen Nsemmeê tuccva nnwen, a Nernu i iâaôviyen". Wid idensen bedlen awal, ur d win i sen nnan. Nessers ed, i wid idensen, tawa$it seg igenni, ilmend n tucmitin nnsen. Mi issuter Musa aman i ugdud is, Nenna: "ewwet aéôu, s uâkkwaz ik". Feggvent ed, segs, mrawsnat tliwa. Yal wa iéôa anda ara issew. "Eççet, esswet, si ôôeéq n Öebbi. Ur ssefsadet di tmurt am imjaêen". Mi tennam: "a Musa! Ur nesteqnaâ bippa s yiwen n lqut. Nuj a$ Mass ik, ad a$ d Issuffe$ ayen d teggar tmurt: tizzegzewt is, axyaô is, ticcert is, laâds is, lebûel is". Inna: "teb$am a pbedlem ayen ilhan s wayen ixuûen? Üûubbet ar Maûeô, a n tafem, war ccekk, ayen tessutrem". I$li d fellasen ddell akked ééelt. Sebbeben d urrif n Öebbi. Ayagi, acku llan ugin issekniyen n Öebbi, neqqen lambiyya, war ssebba. Ayagi, imi âuûan, u zgaren tilas. Ih, wid iumnen, udayen, imasiêiyen, iûabiyen, kra iumnen s Öebbi akked wass aneggaru, u xeddmen ayen ilhan, ad sâun arraz ar Mass nnsen, ur ppagwaden, ur $weblen. Mi Nga laâqed yidwen, Nessuli adrar sennig wen: "eîîfet nezzeh ayen i wen Nefka, mmektit ed i illan degs, amar a pêezzbem". Sinna, deffir waya, twexxôem. Lemmer maççi d lfevl n Öebbi fellawen, akked uêunu S, a ppilim seg imexsuôen. Ni$ tessnem wid, segwen, iccven di Ssebt. Nenna yasen: "ilit d iddawen imaâfan"! Nerra p d amedya i imuddiren akked wid i ten id ineûfen, u d aâggen i wid ipêezziben. Mi inna Musa i ugdud is: "Öebbi, s tidep, Iumeô awen d a ppezlum tafunast". Nnan: "day a tettihiv fella$"? Inna: "ad iyi Isseô Öebbi! Ur ppili$ seg at war tussna". Nnan: "nuj a$ ar Mass ik, ad a$ d Ibeggen anta p". Inna: "Neppa, s tidep, la Iqqaô: tafunast ur wessret, ur meééiyet, garasen. Xedmet i wen d ippumôen". Nnan: "nuj ar Mass ik, ad a$ d Ibeggen ini s". Inna: "Neppa, s tidep, la Iqqaô: d tafunast tawôa$t, ini imfeooeo, ad iaâoeb w ip iwalan". Nnan: "nuj ar Mass ik, ad a$ d Ibeggen anta p. £uône$, s tidep, tistan ppemcabint. Ih, ma Ib$a Öebbi, a nepwanhu". Inna: "Neppa, s tidep, la Iqqaô: d tafunast ur taâtib si tyerza n tmurt, ne$ si tissit n yigran, tûeêêa, ur tepwacôev". Nnan as: "tura, tebbwiv d tidep". Zlan p. Qôib ur ewqimen. Mi ten$am yiwen, wa irra p id $ef wa. Öebbi Issuffe$ ed ayen teppeffrem. Nenna: "ewwtet ep s kra ines". Akka i Issidir Öebbi lmeggtin. Issenâat awen issekniyen iS, amar a pfehmem. Sinna, deffir waya, qquôen wulawen nnwen; cuban aéôu, ne$ kteô, di ta$eôt. Ih, llan iéôa iseg d pfeggiven isaffen. Llan, s tidep, wid ipceqqiqen, teff$en d waman segsen. S tidep, llan wid i$ellin si tugwdi n Öebbi. Ur I$fil Öebbi $ef wayen txeddmem. Day tôe$bem a kwen amnen? Ni$ arbaâ, segsen, ssemêasen i wawal n Öebbi, sinna, mi t fehmen, ad as bedlen udem, u nitni éôan. Mi mmugren wid iumnen, ad inin: "numen". Mi qqimen garasen, qqaôen: "day ad asen tinim ayen i wen Imla Öebbi, a kwen nna$en yis, ar Mass nnwen? Day ur tepmeyyizem ara"? Ne$ ur éôin ara, Öebbi Issen ayen teffren, akked wayen qqaôen. Garasen, at war ta$uôi, ur nessin Tazmamt, siwa ayen nnwan. Nitni $ilen kan. A tawa$it n wid ipparun Tazmamt s ifassen nnsen, sinna, qqaôen: "ayagi s$uô Öebbi", iwakken ad a$en, yis, ayen ôxisen! A tawa$it nnsen, ilmend n wayen uran ifassen nnsen! A tawa$it nnsen, $ef wayen keppben! Nnan: "ur a$ tepnal tmes, d awez$i, siwa kra n wussan". Ini: "day teîîfem lemâahda s$uô Öebbi? Öebbi, d awez$i, ur Izeggil lemâahda S. Ne$ teqqaôem, $ef Öebbi, ayen ur tessinem"? Xaîi, win ikesben tucmip, u tennev as tuccva s…, widak, d at tmes, degs ad wekkôen. Wid iumnen, u xeddmen ayen ilhan, widak, d at Loennet, degs ad wekkôen. Mi Nga laâqed i At Isôail: "ur âabdet siwa Öebbi. Elhut ar imawlan, ar llzem nnwen, ar igujilen, ar igellilen. Init i medden, awal imaânen. èéÈallet, zekkit". Sinna, twexxôem, siwa kra segwen, u, kunwi, tnumrem. Mi wen Nga laâqed nnwen: "ur zzazalet idim nnwen, ur pemssuffu$et seg ixxamen nnwen". D$a twefqem, kunwi d inagan. Sinna, kunwi d wid immin$en, tessuff$em arbaâ segwen, seg ixxamen nnsen. Tezzim asen s ibekkaven akked taâdawt. Ma usan kwen id, d imeêbas, tfeddum ten. Irna, ipwagdel awen usuffe$ nnsen. Day tumnem deg uêric n Tezmamt, tnekôem wayev? Anwa ay d arraz n wid, segwen, ixedmen aya, ma maççi d ddell, di tmeddurt n ddunit, u, ass n tnekra, ad ppunefken i uâaqeb uqsiê mavi? Ur I$fil Öebbi $ef wayen txeddmem. Widak d wid iu$en tudert n ddunit s laxeôt, ur ippifsus fellasen uâaqeb, ur ppusellken. Ni$ Nefka Tazmamt i Musa. Nuzen ed imazanen, deffir es. Nefka abeggen i Âisa, mmi s n Meryem, Null it s ôôuê iqedsen. Yal tikelt ideg ara kwen id ias umazan, s wayen ur awen nehwi, tesme$wôem iman nnwen. Kra teskaddbem ten, kra ten$am ten. Nnan: "ulawen nne$ qquôen". Xaîi, Ixza ten Öebbi, ilmend n tijehli nnsen. Drus iten wid iumnen. Mi ten id tusa Tezmamt, s$uô Öebbi, d atebbet n wayen illan $uôsen, - u llan, iu$ lêal, ssuturen ad $elben wid ijehlen - mi ten id iusa wayen ssnen, ugin t. Ad Inâal Öebbi ijehliyen! I icmet wayen i$ef zzenzen iman nnsen! Ugin ayen id Issers Öebbi. Ëesden mi id Issers Öebbi, si lfevl iS, i win i S ihwan n yimdanen iS. Sebbeben urrif ar wayev. I ijehliyen, aâaqeb isdullun. Ma nnan asen: "amnet s wayen id Issers Öebbi"! A d inin: "numen s wayen id irsen $uône$". Nekôen ayen i t id itebâan, u neppa d tidep, d atebbet n wayen illan $uôsen. Ini: "acimi tneqqem lambiyya n Öebbi, zik, ma d lmumnin ay tellam"? Ni$ iusa kwen id Musa, s ubeggen. Sinna, deffir es, teddam akked uâajmi. Kunwi d imednas. Mi Nga laâqed yidwen, Nessuli adrar sennig wen: "eîîfet nezzeh ayen i wen Nefka, u ssemêesset". Nnan d: "nesla u nâuûa". Ikecm asen uâajmi ar wul, si tjehli nnsen. Ini: "dir it wayen i wen iumeô liman nnwen, ma d lmumnin ay tellam". Ini: "maday, ar Öebbi, axxam aneggaru i kunwi kan, ur pkkan ara imdanen, mennit tameppant, ma tessawalem tidep"! D awez$i, ur p pmennin, ilmend n wayen xedmen ifassen nnsen. Öebbi Issen imednas. A ten tafev, war ccekk, êemmlen tameddurt sennig medden, sennig imcurak. Atan yiwen segsen, issaram ad idder agim iseggwasen. Te$wzi n laâmeô is, ur as tessifrir aâaqeb. Öebbi Ipwali ayen xeddmen. Ini: "anwa illan d acengu n Jebrayen"? D neppa, s tidep, it id issersen $ef wul ik, s leb$i n Öebbi. D atebbet n wayen it id izwaren, d nnhaya u d abecceô n lmumnin. Win illan d acengu n Öebbi, lmalayek iS, imazanen iS, Jebrayen, Mikail…, ihi, Öebbi d acengu ijehliyen. Ni$ Nessers ak d issekniyen iberrzen. I ten inekôen, siwa iballa$en. Day yal tikelt ideg ara gen laâqed, a t ixdaâ urbaâ segsen? Ih, tegwti segsen, ur uminen. Mi ten id iusa umazan s$uô Öebbi, itebbet ayen illan $uôsen, arbaâ n wid iwumi teppunefk Tezmamt, rran Tazmamt n Öebbi s azagur nnsen, amzun ur ssinen. Ddan akked wayen xedmen ccwaîen mgal tagelda n Sliman. Sliman ur ijhil. Maca ccwaîen jehlen. Sseêfaven i medden ssêur, akked wayen id irsen, di Babil, ar lmalayek Harut akked Marut. Ur sselmaden yiwen, mebla ma nnan: "nekwni n$ewwu kan, ur jehhel"! ÊÊÊËefven, $uôsen, amek ara ssemfaôaqen argaz akked tmeîîut is. Ur îîurun yiwen syis, siwa ma Ib$a Öebbi. ÊÊÊËefven ara ten ivuôôen, ur ten ineffaâ. Ni$ éôan ar win i p iu$en, ur as illi umur di laxeôt. War ccekk, ard ucmit wayen is zzenzen leôwaê nnsen, lemmer éôin! Lemmer, s tidep, uminen u êezzben, ad ifrir warraz s$uô Öebbi, lemmer ssinen. A wid iumnen! Ur qqaret: "Âass a$ d", init: "Wali a$ d", u ssemêesset. I ijehliyen, aâaqeb aqeôêan. Ur b$in ara ijehliyen, seg wid iwumi teppunefk Tezmamt, akked imcurak, ad awen d irs kra n lxiô, s$uô Mass nnwen. Öebbi Ismenyaf, s uêunu S, win i S ihwan. Öebbi d Bab n lfevl ameqwôaêan. Ur Nessemsay assekni, ne$ ur t Nesseppu, mebla ma Nebbwi d win it yifen, ne$ i t icban. Day ur teéôiv ara Öebbi Izmer i yal cci? Day ur teéôiv ara, ar n Öebbi tagelda n tmurt akked igenwan? Ur tesâim, war Öebbi, bab, ne$ asettaô. Ne$ teb$am a ppesteqsim Amazan nnwen, akken ippusteqsa, zik, Musa? Win ibeddlen liman s tijehli, innetlaf ar yir abrid. Si leêsed nnsen, aîas seg wAt Tezmamt, mi sen d tban tidep, budden awen tijehli, mbaâd liman nnwen. Ssemêet, ssemsut, ar d Ias Öebbi s lameô iS. Ni$ Öebbi Izmer i yal cci. èéallet, zekkit. Ayen ara tezzewrem n lxiô i iman nnwen, a t tafem ar Öebbi. Öebbi, s tidep, Ipwali ayen akw txeddmem. Nnan: "ur ikeççem Loennet, siwa win illan d uday, ne$ d amasiêi". D wagi ay d asirem nnsen. Ini: "awit ed atebbet nnwen, ma tessawalem tidep". Xaîi, win iunzen i Öebbi, u d aâôvi, ad isâu arraz is, ar Mass is. Ur ppagwaden, ur $weblen. Nnan wudayen: "imasiêiyen ur sennden s acemma". Nnan imasiêiyen: "udayen ur sennden s acemma". U nitni la qqaôen Tazmamt. Akka, wid ur nessin ara, nnan am nitni. Ad Iêudd Öebbi, garasen, ass n tnekra, $ef wayen i$ef mgarraden. Anwa idensen sennig wid igedlen, di leowamaâ n Öebbi, asmekti n yisem iS, u lhan d deg ussexôeb nnsen? Widak, ur iwata ara a ten kecmen, siwa ma s tugwdi. I nitni, ddell di ddunit, u aâaqeb abarar di laxeôt. N Öebbi agmuv akked utaram. Ar wanda tezzim, din Udem n Öebbi. Ih, Öebbi d Ajemmal, d Amusnaw. Nnan: "Öebbi Isâa mmi S". Gedha s yiS! Ni$ ineS i illan di tmurt akked igenwan. Akw, péallan i Neppa, Axellaq n tmurt akked igenwan. Ma Iseyya lameô, ad as Yini kan: "ili"! Ad yili. Nnan wid ur nessin: "a lemmer ad a$ d Immeslay Öebbi, ne$ ad a$ d ias ussekni"! Akka ay nnan wid i ten id izwaren, am awalen nnsen. Ppemcabin wulawen nnsen. Ni$ Nbeggen ed issekniyen i ugdud ipputebbten. Ih, Nuzen ik id, s tidep, d abcir, u d aneddaô. Ur ippili fellak usteqsi $ef at wu$ud. Ur k pôavin wudayen ne$ imasiêiyen, alamma teddiv d ddin nnsen. Ini: "d nehhu n Öebbi ay d nehhu". Ma teddiv akked usirem nnsen, deffir wayen ik ed iusan n tmusni, ur k ipfukku, si Öebbi, bab, ne$ asettaô. Wid iwumi Nefka Tazmamt, qqaôen p leqôaya iwatan. Widak umnen yis. Wid i p iugin, widak d imexsuôen. A yAt Isôail! Mmektit ed l$it iW, is i kwen £ate$. Nek, Smenyafe$ kwen i imavalen. Ëezzbet i wass ideg ur ippuqeîîi yiwen, deg umkan n wayev, s wacemma; ur tepwaqbal le$ôama segs, ur t tenfaâ ccafuâa, ur ppusellken. Ibôahim, mi t Ijeôôeb Mass is, s wawalen, iu$ awal. Inna: "Nek, a k Rre$ d win ara inehhun medden". Inna: "u si tarwa w"? Inna: "lemâahda W ur taâna ara imednas". Ad iêezzeb i Öebbi, Mass is. Ur issenqas acemma segs. Ma illa umeîîalbu d abuhal, ne$ d uôhif, ne$ ur izmir ad yini neppa, ihi, ad yini umeddakwel is s ûûfawa. Sbeddet sin inagan seg irgazen nnwen. سُوۡرَةُ اٰلِ عِمۡرٰنَ Alm. Öebbi, ur illi ôebbi siwa Neppa, Amuddir, Imezgi. Issers ak d Tazmamt s tidep, d atebbet n wayen ip id izwaren. Issers ed Tuôa akked Linoil, uqbel, d nnhaya i medden. Issers ed Leqwôan. Ih, wid inekôen issekniyen n Öebbi, fellasen aâaqeb uqûiê. Öebbi d Uzmir, Ippara d ppaô. Ih, Öebbi ur aS iffir wacemma di tmurt, ne$ deg igenni. D Neppa i wen Ippaken udem, di tâabbav, akken i S ihwa. Ur illi ôebbi siwa Neppa, Uzmir, Bab n ûûwab. Neppa i k ed Issersen Tazmamt, degs issekniyen uvhiôen, nitni d tayimmap n Tezmamt. Wiyav d licwaô. D$a, wid iwumi mmalen wulawen, teddun akked wayen illan d licwaô, ssaramen ahewwel, ssaramen asefhem is. I Issnen asefhem is, siwa Öebbi. Qqaôen imawlan n tmusni: "numen yis. S$uô Mass nne$ akw". Id ismektayen, siwa uâqilen. A Mass nne$! Ur Smili ulawen nne$, mbaâd ma Tenhiv a$. Efk a$ d, s$uôeK, aêunu. Ih, Keçç, ard Am$it. A Mass nne$! Keçç, s tidep, ara Ijemmlen medden, ass i$ef ur illi ccekk. S tidep, Öebbi ur Izeggel lemâahda. Ih, wid ijehlen, ur sen d ippawi acemma, ar Öebbi, wayla nnsen, ne$ tarwa nnsen. Widak, d nitni ay d isufa n tmes. D tin n ugdud n Ferâun akked wid i ten id izwaren. Skaddben issekniyen nne£. Iwwet iten Öebbi, ilmend ibekkaven nnsen. Öebbi Iwâaô i uâaqeb. Ini i wid ijehlen: "a ppepwa$elbem, a ppepwafesrem di Loahennama". A yir usu! Ni$ d assekni, i kunwi, mi mlalent snat trebbuyaâ. Yiwet tepna$ deg ubrid n Öebbi; tayev d tajehlit, twala d snat, s yiéôi s. Öebbi Ippak afus, s tallalt iS, i win i S ihwan. Deg wayagi, s tidep, aselmed i wid ipwalin. D tucbiêt ay d tedheô i yimdanen leêmala n ccehwiyyat: tilawin, tarwa, iâammuôen ibararen n ddheb akked lfeîîa, iâawdiwen n ccetla, lmal, akal. Ayagi, d zzhu n tmeddurt n ddunit. Öebbi, $uôeS amkan lâali, n tu$alin. Ini: "ad awen mle$ i yifen aya? I wid ipêezziben, ar Mass nnsen, leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen, degsen ad wekkôen, tilawin iûfan, akked llza s$uô Öebbi". Öebbi Ipwali imdanen; wid iqqaôen: "a Mass nne$! Nekwni, s tidep, numen. Ihi, Semmeê a$ ibekkaven nne$, Sellek a$ seg uâaqeb n tmes". Iûebôiyen, imawlan n tidep, imvuâen, wid ipseddiqen, wid iste$fiôen di tafrara. Icuhhed Öebbi ar ur illi ôebbi, siwa Neppa. Akken lmalayek, akked imawlan n tmusni. Ibedd i lmizan. Ur illi ôebbi, siwa Neppa, Uzmir, Bab n ûûwab. Ih, ddin ar Öebbi d annuz. Ur mgarraden wid iwumi teppunefk Tezmamt, armi deffir n tisin n tussna $uôsen, wa iqheô wa. Wid inekôen issekniyen n Öebbi, ihi, Öebbi Ip$awal deg uqeîîi. Ma nuqmen k, ini: "unze$ aS i Öebbi. Akken, wid iddan yidi. Ini i wid iwumi teppunefk Tezmamt, akked at war tussna: "ma tunzem"? Ma unzen, ihi, pwanhan. Ma wexxôen, ay fellak siwa anabi. Öebbi Ipwali imdanen. Ih, wid inekôen issekniyen n Öebbi, u pna$en lambiyya, war ssebba, u pna$en wid seg yimdanen ippamôen lmizan, becceô iten s uâaqeb aqeôêan. Widak, d wid iwumi mêan igiten nnsen di ddunit, di laxert. Ur sâin isellaken. Day ur twalav ara wid iwumi ippunefk kra si Tezmamt, la ssuturen, i Tezmamt n Öebbi, aêuddu garasen? Sinna, ad iwexxeô urbaâ segsen, u nitni pnamaren. Ayagi, acku nnan: "ur a$ teppep tmes, siwa kra n wussan". I$uôô iten, di ddin nnsen, wayen id snulfuyen. Amek ihi, ma Njemmel iten, ass ideg, ur degs ccekk, yal yiwen ad i$ellet ayen ikseb, nitni ur ppudensen. Ini: "a Öebbi, Agellid n tgelda, Teppakev tagelda i win i K ihwan, Teppeksev tagelda i win i K ihwan, Tepâuzzuv win i K ihwan, Tesdulluv win i K ihwan. Lxiô deg ufus i K. Ih, Keçç, Tzemrev i yal cci. Tessekcamev iv deg wass. Tessekcamev ass deg iv. Tessuffu$ev amuddir si lmegget. Tessuffu$ev lmegget seg umuddir. Tep$itiv win i K ihwan, war aktili". سُوۡرَةُ النِّسَآءِ A yimdanen! Ëezzbet i Mass nnwen, ikwen Ixelqen seg yiwen n lxelq, u Ixelq ed segs ayugan is. Issuffe$ ed, segsen, aîas n yirgazen akked tlawin. Ëezzbet i Öebbi i$ef tepmesteqsayem, akw i tâabbuvin. Öebbi, s tidep, Izga Iquôaâ kwen. Efket ayla nnsen i igujilen, ur pparat dduni deg umkan n lâali. Ur pparat ayla nnsen d ayla nnwen. Ih, wagi d abekkav ameqwôan. Ma tugadem ur tweznem ara ar igujilen, a$et ayen i wen ihwan n tlawin: snat, kravt, kuét. Ma tugadem ur tessaâdalem ara, yiwet kan, ne$ taklatin nnwen. Akka i iwulem, ur ppakwret. Efket tuççit nnsent i tlawin, d tikci. Ma rrant awen d kra segs, s leb$i nnsent, ççet ep, s lfeôê akked llza. Ur ppaket i ije$lufen ayla nnwen, win i wen Ifka Öebbi i tmeddurt. Öeéqet pen segs, sselset pen, ééiédet awal nnwen $uôsen. Jeôôbet igujilen, alamma bbwven i jjwao. Ma tufam ten éewôen, efket asen ayla nnsen. Ur ten teppet s uveggaâ d usexseô, uqbel ad im$uôen. Ameôkanti ad iêezzeb, ame$bun ad içç s lekyasa. Mara sen tefkem ayla nnsen, s inagan fellas. Nesteqnaâ s Öebbi i leêsab. I yirgazen, amur seg wayen d ooan imawlan akked llzem. I tlawin amur seg wayen d ooan imawlan akked llzem. Ama cwiî, ne$ aîas, d amur ilezmen. Ma êedôen, i ufôaq, llzem, igujilen, igellilen, ôeéqet pen segs, tinem asen awal uûwib. Ad agwaden wid id iooan, deffir sen, tarwa tagellilt. Ad agwaden fellasen. Ad êezzben i Öebbi, s wawal iweznen. Ih, wid iteppen, s ddens, ayla igujilen, la teppen kan times deg iâabbav nnsen, ad pwagren deg ujajiê. £ef tarwa nnwen, Iweûûa kwen Öebbi: i uqcic amur n snat tullas. Ma llant sennig snat n tullas, nnsent amur wis kué n lweôt. Ma yiwet i illan, ines uzgen. I imawlan is, i yal wa, amur wis sdis n wayen id iooa, ma isâa mmi s. Ma ur isâa ara mmi s, u weôten t imawlan is, amur wis kué i immas. Ma isâa atmaten, i immas amur wis sdis, kkes ed ayen ippuseôfen ne$ îlabat. Imawlan nnwen, arraw nnwen, ur teéôim ara menyif iten, akken i kwen nefâan. D aêeppem n Öebbi. Öebbi, s tidep, Izga d Bab n ûûwab, d Amusnaw. Nnwen uzgen n wayen id ooant tlawin nnwen, ma ur sâint ara tarwa. Ma sâant mmit sent, i kunwi amur wis kué n wayen id ooant, kkes ed ayen ippuseôfen ne$ îlabat. I nitenti, amur wis kué n wayen id teooam, ma ur tesâim ara mmit wen. Ma tesâam mmit wen, i nitenti amur wis îam n wayen id teooam, kkes ed ayen ippuseôfen ne$ îlabat. Ma d argaz awêid ne$ d tameîîut tawêiî, ma isâa agmat ne$ taultmap, i yal wa segsen, amur wis sdis. Ma deg waîas ay llan, ad feôqen amur wis krav, war ccqa, kkes ed ayen ippuseôfen ne$ îlabat. D aweûûi n Öebbi. Öebbi Iéôa, Iêellem. D tigi ay d tilisa n Öebbi. Win issemêessen i Öebbi akked Umazan iS, a t Issekcem ar leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen, degsen ad wekkôen. I tid ixedmen lâaô di tlawin nnwen, awit ed, fellasent, kué inagan nnwen. Ma cehhden d, kemnet pent di texxamin, alamma teddem itent tmeppant, ne$ Iga yasent Öebbi abrid. Ayagi, Izga d ayen isehlen i Öebbi. A yimdanen! Ni$ iusa kwen id Umazan, s tidep, s$uô Mass nnwen. Amnet, ppif i kunwi. Ma tugim, ihi n Öebbi, i illan di tmurt akked igenwan. Öebbi Izga Iéôa, d Bab n ûûwab. A yAt Tezmamt! Ur sfuhruyet ddin nnwen. Ur qqaret, $ef Öebbi, siwa tidep. Lmasiê Âisa, mmi s n Meryem, d amazan kan n Öebbi; d awal iS i Irra ar Meryem, u d ôôuê s $uôeS. Ihi, amnet s Öebbi akked imazanen iS, ur qqaôet: "krav"! Ëebset, ppif i kunwi. Öebbi d Yiwen kan n Öebbi. Gedha s yiS, ma ad Isâu mmi S! IneS i illan deg igenwan, i illan di tmurt. Nesteqnaâ s Öebbi d Awkil. Ur ismummi ara lmasiê, ma illa d amdan n Öebbi. Akken lmalayek tuqôibin. Wid ismummin a T âabden, u zuxxen, ad pwafessren akw $uôeS. Wanag wid iumnen, u xedmen ayen ilhan, ad asen Ifk arraz nnsen, ad asen Irnu si lfevl iS. Ma d wid ismummin u zuxxen, a ten Iâaqeb aâaqeb aqeôêan. Ur ppafen, war Öebbi, bab ne$ asettaô. A yimdanen! Ni$ iusa kwen id utebbet s$uô Mass nnwen, u Nessers awen ed tafat ibanen. Wanag wid iumnen s Öebbi, i iîîfen degS, a ten Issekcem ar uêunu S akked lfevl. A ten Inhu $uôeS, deg ubrid uwqim. Cawôen k. Ini: "Öebbi Isfehm awen d $ef llzem. Ma immut urgaz, war tarwa, isâa taultmap, i neppat azgen n wayen id iooa. Neppa a p iwôet, ma ur tesâi tarwa. Ma snat ay llant, amur wis krav i yal ta, n wayen id iooa. Ma llan watmaten akked tessetmatin, i uqcic amur n snat n tullas". Ibeggen awen d Öebbi akken ur tepnnetlafem. Öebbi Iéôa yal cci.

سُوۡرَةُ الۡاَعۡرافِ Almû. Tazmamt ters ed $uôek, ur teppili segs lhejna deg idmaren ik, iwakken a pnabiv yis; u d asmekti i lmumnin. Ddut d wayen id irsen $uôwen, s$uô Mass nnwen. Ti$ôi nnsen, mi ten id tusa tiyta nne£, siwa mi d nnan: "ih, nella d imednas". War ccekk, a Nesteqsi wid u$uô id Nuzen, a Nesteqsi imazanen. War ccekk, ad asen Neêku, s tmusni, ur Nelli N$ab. Wagi yif iten". Ayagi seg issekniyen n Öebbi, amar a d mmektin. A tarwa n Adem! £uôwat a kwen ihewwel Cciîan, akken id issuffe$ imezwura nnwen si Loennet! Day $ilen imezda$ n temdinin, ur ten id teppawev tiyta nne£, deg yiv, nitni îîsen? Ne$ day $ilen imezda$ n temdinin, ur ten id teppawev tiyta nne£, deg wazal, nitni ppuraren? Ad Veôôfe$, seg issekniyen iW, wid isme$wôen iman nnsen di tmurt, war ssebba. Mi walan yal assekni, ur ppamnen yis. Ma walan abrid uûwib, ur teddun degs. Ma walan abrid n le$wlav, a t awin. Ayagi, acku, s tidep, skaddben issekniyen nne£, ur d celâen degsen. Wid iskaddben issekniyen nne£, akked temlilit n laxeôt, ur swin igiten nnsen. Day a ten kafin $ef wayen ur nelli d ayen xeddmen? Agdud n Musa, deffir es, isbedd, s ôôêuê is, aâjmi bu loeppa isrugmuten. Day ur walan ara ar, s tidep, ur asen d ipmeslay, ur la ten inehhu s abrid? Âabden t, llan d imednas. Mi ppuêeccmen, u walan ar, zi$ nnetlafen, nnan: "ma ur Iêun ara fella$ Mass nne$, ma ur a$ Isemmeê ara, war ccekk, a nu$al seg imexsuôen". Mi d iu$al Musa ar ugdud is, s wurrif akked lêemûa, inna: "ay d ucmit wayen is iyi tneûfem, deffir iw! Teb$am a d i$iwwel lameô n Mass nnwen"? Inna: "a Mass iw! Semmeê ane$, nek akked gma, Ssekcem a$ ar uêunu K. Keçç, Tifev akw wid ipêunun". Ih, wid iâabden aâajmi, a d i$li fellasen wurrif n Mass nnsen, ad ndellen di tmeddurt n ddunit. Llzem ppemyilin kteô di Tezmamt n Öebbi. Öebbi, s tidep, Izôa yal cci.

Ad Icehhed Öebbi ar nitni, s tidep, d ikeddaben. Ur ppili, degs, d awez$i. Iklal kteô, tilin ik, loamaâ ibnan $ef uêezzeb, seg wass amenzu. Degs irgazen i iêemmlen ad izdigen. Öebbi Iêemmel izedganen. Day win issersen lebni s $ef uêezzeb i Öebbi akked llza, ur yif ara win issersen lebni s $ef rrif n ucôuf ara iseggxen? Iseggex yis ar tmes n Loahennama. Öebbi ur Inehhu agdud imednas. Izga lebni, bnan, ippara ccekk deg ulawen nnsen, alamma gezmen wulawen nnsen. Öebbi d Amusnaw, d Bab n ûûwab. Ih, Öebbi Iu$ ar lmumnin, iman nnsen akked wayla nnsen, imi Loennet i nitni. Pna$en deg ubrid n Öebbi. Nn$an, pwan$an. D lemâahda fellas, s tidep, di Tuôa, di Linoil akked Leqwôan. Anwa yifen Öebbi di tuîîfa n lemâahda s? Feôêet, ihi, di ssuq tsewwqem. Wagi d rrbeê ameqwôaêan. Wid isteôoâen, wid iâabden, wid ipcekkiôen, ixelwiyen, wid iîîinizen, wid ikennun, wid ippamôen lewqama, wid ipgeddilen ayen n dir, wid ipêaraben $ef tlisa n Öebbi ... Becceô lmumnin. Ur issefk ara i Nnbi akked wid iumnen, ad ssutren ad pwasemmêen imcurak, xas ppilin asen, ma iban asen d ar, nitni, war ccekk, d at tmes. Ur awen illi, war Öebbi, bab ne$ amâiwen. Ni$ Issuref Öebbi i Nnbi akked iminigen, akked imâiwnen i iddan yides, di lweqt uwâiô, mbaâd ma qôib nneqlaben wulawen n urbaâ segsen. Sinna, Issuref asen. Ih, Neppa, i nitni, dUmâin, d'Aênin. U i krav id igwran, armi, tamurt iwsâan, tediyyeq fellasen. Vaqen deg iman nnsen. Ufan ur illi ssôan si Öebbi, siwa Neppa. Sinna, Issuref asen, akken ad steôoâen. Öebbi, s tidep, Issuruf, Ipêunu. A wid iumnen! Ëezzbet i Öebbi, ilit seg imawlan n tidep. Ur issefk ara i imezda$ n Lmadina, d wayen i sen d izzin n waâôaben n ucluê, ad gwrin deffir Umazan n Öebbi, ne$ ad smenyafen iman nnsen i iman is. Ayagi, acku ur ten ipêaz fad, ne$ âaggu, ne$ llaé, deg ubrid n Öebbi. Ur keçmen akal ara isserfun ijehliyen, ur ppaîîafen acemma s$uô ucengu, siwa ma dayen i sen iuran d igi n wayen ilhan. Öebbi, s tidep, ur Isôuêu arraz iâaôviyen. Ur pûeôôifen cwiî ne$ aîas, ur zeggren asif, siwa ma iura yasen, iwakken a ten Ikafi Öebbi $ef wayen ilhan deg wayen xeddmen. Ur Issefk ara i lmumnin ad ff$en akw. Awufan ad iffe$ ugraw si yal arbaâ, ad $bun di ddin, ad nabin agdud nnsen, mara u$alen $uôsen. Amar ad steêdren. A wid iumnen! Nna$et ijehliyen i kwen iqeôben. Ad afen, $uôwen, teqseê. Cfut, Öebbi Ippili d wid ipêezziben. Mi d ters tsuôep, llan garasen wid iqqaôen: "anwa degwen, iwumi terna tagi, di liman"? Ma d wid iumnen, terna yasen liman, u nitni feôêen. Ma d wid iwumi blan wulawen, terna ammus i wammus nnsen. Mmuten u nitni d ijehliyen. Day ur walan ara, ar nitni la d sskaren lfetna, yal aseggwas, yiwen ubrid ne$ berdayen? Sinna, ur steôoiâen, ur d smektayen. Mi d ters tsuôep, ad mesmuqalen: "day illa yiwen ikwen id Ipwalin"? سُوۡرَةُ يُوسُفَ Alô. Wigi d issekniyen n Tazmamt ipbegginen. Ih, Nessader it id d Leqwôan, s taâôabt, amar a pfehmem. Akka, a k Ifren Mass ik, u ak Isselmed asefru n temsal, u ad Itim l$it iS, i keçç akked twacult n Yaâqub, akken it Itam, zik, af lejdud ik: Ibôahim akked Isêaq. Mass ik, s tidep, d Amusnaw, d Uûwib". Ni$, di Yusef akked watma s, illa ussekni i wid isteqsayen. Mi nnan: "war ccekk, ifen a$, Yusef akked gma s, akken iten iêemmel babat nne$, u nekwni d îîeôma. Babat nne$, s tidep, haat di ttelfan n ûûeê. En$et Yusef, ne$ nfut ep si tmurt, a d ilhu degwen babat wen, sinna, a ppu$alem d imdanen ixeddmen ayen ilhan". Inna win d immeslayen, degsen: "ur neqqet Yusef, veggôet ep ar lqaâa n wannu. Ma tgam akka, a t iddem yiwen umsebrid". Nnan: "a babat nne$, acu k iu$en, ur a$ tuminev ara, $ef Yusef. Nekwni, fellas, s tidep, d unûiêen. Sseddu t yidne$ azekka, ad izhu, ad iurar. Nekwni, war ccekk, a nêareb fellas". Inna: "nek, s tidep, $weble$ ma tebbwim t yidwen, ugade$ a t içç lweêc, kunwi testehzam degs". Nnan: "ma içça t lweêc, u nekwni d îîeôma, s tidep a nili d imexsuôen". Mi t bbwin, mwafaqen a t rôen ar lqaâa n wannu, Nweêêa yas: "ad asen temlev, s tidep, lameô agi nnsen, nitni ur éôin". U$alen d tameddit, ar babat sen, pprun. Nnan: "a babat nne$, s tidep, nôuê a nemzizzel, neooa Yusef ar lqecc nne$, içça t lweêc. Ur a$ teppamnev, xas nenna d tidep". Bbwin d tasedrit is, degs idamen n rrya. Inna: "xaîi! D iman nnwen i wen d iccacven lameô. Ilha ûûbeô. Anuju $eô Öebbi, mgal ayen d teêkam". Usan d iminigen, uznen win id ippagwmen, issader ssvel is. Inna: "a lxiô, wagi d aqcic"! Ffren t, amzun d sselâa. Öebbi Iéôa acu xeddmen. Zzenzen t, s ôôxa, s kra iûuôdiyen. Ur as fkin ara azal. Inna, i tmeîîut is, Umaûôi i t iu$en: "eôêeb yis, amar ad a$ infaâ, at nerr d mmit nne$". Akka ay Nesseqâad Yusef di tmurt, iwakken ad as Nesseêfev asefru n temsal. Öebbi d Amezwaru s lameô iS, maca tegwti n medden ur éôin ara. Mi d immeêtel, Nefka yas ûûwab, tussna. Akka ay Nepkafi iâaôviyen. Teb$a t tin u$ur izde$. Terra tibbura, u tenna: "eyya keçç"! Inna: "ad iyi Ineooi Öebbi! Ni$ bab iw iôêeb yissi. S tidep, ur rebêen imednas". S tidep, teb$a t, u neppa ib$a p, lemmer ur iwala ara atebbet n Mass is. Akka, iwakken a Nessebâad fellas tuccva, lâaô. Neppa, s tidep, seg imdanen nne£ izedganen. Uzzlen ar tebburt, tcerreg as tasedrit is, si zdeffir. Mmugren, argaz is, ar tebburt. Tenna: "acu ay d aqeîîi n win iâabwlen ad iccmet tawacult ik, siwa lêebs ne$ aâaqeb aqeôêan"? Inna: "d neppat iyi ib$an". Icuhhed ed yiwen unagi si twacult is: "ma teqqeôs tsedrit si zdat, tenna d tidep, u neppa d akeddab. Ma teqqeôs tsedrit si zdeffir, teskaddeb, u neppa seg at tidep". Mi iwala teqqeôs tsedrit si zdeffir, inna: "ayagi, war ccekk, si nncub nnkwent. Ih, nncub nnkwent d timeqwôaêanin. A Yusef, ppu ayagi, u kem ssuter ssmaê ubekkav im. Kem, s tidep, teccvev". La qqaôent tlawin, di temdint: "tameîîut umdebbeô têemmel acrik is. Teshebl ip tayri. F akken nwala, appan, s tidep, di ttelfan n ûûeê". Mi tesla s nncub nnsent, tuzen $uôsent, thegga yasent tanalt. I yal yiwet segsent, tefka tafrut. Tenna: "effe$ ed garasent". Mi t walant, isdehc itent, jerêent ifassen nnsent, nnant: "êaca Öebbi, wagi maççi d amdan, wagi siwa d lmelk ukyis". Tenna: "d wagi i$ef iyi tlummemt. Ih, b$i$ t, neppa iqqim zeddig. Ma ur ixdim ara ay s umôe$, war ccekk, ad ipwaêbes, ad ipwaêqeô". Inna: "a Mass iw! Smenyafe$ lêebs i wayen u$ur iyi d ssawalent. Ma ur Tesbaâdev ara felli nncub nnsent, ad male$ $uôsent, ad ili$ seg wid ur nessin". Ijaweb as d Mass is. Issebâad fellas nncub nnsent. Neppa, s tidep, Issel, d Amusnaw. Sinna, mi ten usan issekniyen, ufan, war ccekk, ilaq a t irr ar lêebs, kra n tallit. Kecmen yides, ar lêebs, sin ilmeéiyen. Inna yiwen degsen: "nek wala$ iman iw, la teééme$ ccôab". Ddi$ d ddin n lejdud iw: Ibôahim, Isêaq akked Yaâqub. Ur a$ ippunefk a nezdukkel acemma i Öebbi. Ayagi si lfevl n Öebbi fellane$, akw $ef imdanen. Maca, tegwti n yimdanen ur snemmiren. A yimeddukwal iw n lêebs, menyif imawlan imfaôaqen, ne$ Öebbi Yiwen, Aqehhaô? Ay tâabdem, war Neppa, d ismawen kan i sen tefkam, kunwi akked imezwura nnwen. Ur asen d Issers ara Öebbi kra udabu. Lêukm ar Öebbi kan. Iumeô ed ur tâabdem, siwa Neppa. D wagi ay d ddin uûwib, maca tegwti n yimdanen ur ssinen. A yimeddukwal iw n lêebs, wanag yiwen degwen ad ismiri ccôab, i bab is, wayev ad ippusemmeô $ef umidag, ifrax ad nneqben aqeôôu s. Ippuseyya lameô $ef wayen iyi d testeqsam". Nnan: "d tirga iwlellsen. Ur nelli d imusnawen i usefru n tirga". Win i isellken si sin nni, armi tallit id immekti, inna: "nek, ad awen d awi$ asefru ines, aznet iyi. A Yusef, bab n tidep, ssefru ya$ d: ûa testan tiqebwaniyin, la tent teppent ûa tuvâifin, akked ûa tyedrin tizegzawin, tiyav d tiqquôanin. Amar, ma u$ale$ ar imdanen, amar ad éôen". Inna: "zerâat ûa iseggwasen imyevfaôen. Ayen tzerâam, eooet ep di tyedrin is, siwa cwiî ara teççem. Sinna, deffir sen, a d asen ûa iwaâôen. Ad ççen ayen i sen theggam siwa cwiî, seg wayen txeznem. Nnant: "êaca Öebbi, ur nufi $uôes tuccva". Tenna d tmeîîut umvebbeô: "tura, a d tban tidep. D nek i t ib$an, ma d neppa, s tidep, d bab n tidep". "Akka, iwakken ad iéeô ur t xdiâa$ ara s tuffra. Mi s immeslay, inna: "keçç, assa, nefka yak adabu, laman". Inna: "wekkel iyi $ef lemxazen n tmurt, nek d amêareb amusnaw". Akka ay Nesseqâad Yusef di tmurt, ad izde$ anda i s ihwa. Nepêunu $ef win i £ ihwan, ur Nesôuêu arraz iâaôviyen. S tidep, arraz n laxeôt yif it, i wid iumnen u llan pêezziben. Usan watmaten n Yusef, kecmen $uôes, iâqel iten, nitni ur t âqilen. Nnan: "nesôuê taqbuct ugellid. Win ip id ibbwin, ad as nefk ppâabga n ul$wem. Nek, vemne$ t". Nnan: "s Öebbi, nni$ teéôam ur d nusa ara a nessefsed tamurt, ur nelli d imakwaren". Ibda la ipqellib icekkaôen, uqbel win n gma s, sinna, issuffe$ ip id seg ucekkaô n gma s. Akka ay Nefka ticeôkep i Yusef. Ur izmir ad iîîef gma s, s lqanun ugellid, siwa ma Irad Öebbi. Öebbi Yif akw akken Iéôa ayen d teqqaôem". Nnan: "a yameqwôan, baba s, s tidep, wesser. Eîîef yiwen segne$ deg umekkan is. Nwala k, ih, telliv si lâuûam". Inna: "ur a$ Iâammed Öebbi a neîîef, siwa win u$uô nufa ta$awsa nne$. Mulac, war ccekk, a nili d imednas". Amar Öebbi a yi ten id Iawi akw. Neppa, s tidep, d Bab n ûûwab, d Amusnaw". Ijuneb iten, u inna: "a lêif iw $ef Yusef"! Allen is ijegger itent u$ilif, innu$ben. A yarraw iw, ôuêet, steqsit $ef Yusef akked gma s. Ur ppayset di tecvaî n Öebbi. Ih, i ippaysen di tecvaî n Öebbi, siwa agdud ijehliyen". Öebbi, s tidep, ur Isôuêu arraz iâaôviyen". Nnan: "s Öebbi ar k Ismenyaf Öebbi garane$. Nekwni, s tidep, neccev". Inna: "ur telli tiyta degwen, assa. Ad awen Isemmeê Öebbi! Neppa Yif akw wid ipêunun. Mi d iusa ubcir, issers as p $ef udem is, llint ed wallen is, inna: "day ur awen nni$ ara: nek ssne$, s$uô Öebbi, ayen ur tessinem"? Nnan as: "a babat nne$, ssuter ad a$ pwasemmêen ibekkaven nne$. S tidep, nella d imednab". Inna: "deqqal ad ssutre$, i Mass iw, ad awen Isemmeê. Neppa, s tidep, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu". Mi bbwven ar Yusef, isteôêeb s imawlan is. Inna: "kecmet ar Maseô, di laman, ma Irad Öebbi". Issuli imawlan is ar usgeld. £lin, knan as. Inna: "a baba! D wagi ay d asefru n targit iw, n zik. Ni$ Issuffe$ ip Mass iw! Ni$ Iga yi leqôaô mi yi d Issuffe$ si lêebs. Ikkes ikwen id si sseêôa, deffir tismin i isker Cciîan, gari d watma. Mass iw, s tidep, d Laîif i win i S ihwan. Ih, Neppa d Amusnaw, d Bab n ûûwab. A Mass iw, ni$ Tefkiv iyi si tgelda, Tesêefvev iyi asefru n temsal. Axellaq n tmurt akked igenwan, Keçç, d Bab iw di ddunit, di laxeôt, Eddem ôôuê iw d amvua, Ssiwev iyi ar wid imaânen". Tagi, si teêkayin n tbavnit, Nweêêa yak p in. Ur telliv $uôsen, mi mwafaqen a p andin. Tegwti n yimdanen, xas tâapbev, ur ppamnen. Ur asen ssutur kra n teqdiât. Neppa, d asmekti kan i imavalen. I illan deg issekniyen di tmurt akked igenwan! La teddun fellasen, maca wexxôen asen. Tegwti, segsen, ur ppamnen s Öebbi, siwa ma curken. Day ppeklen ur asen isburru yara uâaqeb n Öebbi, ne$ ur ten id ippas ara yimir, deqzalla, ur pfaqan? Ini: "wagi d abrid iw, la pnuju$ ar Öebbi ad Ildi allen, i nek akked wid iddan yidi. Gedha s Öebbi! Ur lli$ seg wid ipcaraken". Nuzen ed kan, uqbel ik, irgazen seg imezda$ n temdinin, iwumi Nweêêa. Day ur unagen ara di tmurt, ad walin amek tevôa d wid i ten id izwaren? Ih, pifxiô axxam aneggaru i wid ipêezziben. Day ur tefhimem ara? Alamma, mi uysen imazanen, u meyyzen ar skaddben ten, tusa ten id tallalt s$uône£. Nepsellik win i £ ihwan. Ur ipwakkas ara ssxev nne£, i ugdud ibe$wviyen. Ni$, di teêkayin nnsen, illa uselmed i yuâqilen. Ur telli d awal id innulfan. Neppat tetebbet ed ay d izwaren, tfeûûel ed yal cci. D nnhaya u d aêunu i ugdud iumnen.
سُوۡرَةُ الرَّعۡدِ Almô. Wigi d issekniyen n Tezmamt. Ayen i k d irsen, s$uô Mass ik, d tidep, maca tegwti n medden ur ppamnen. Öebbi i Issulin igenwan war tigwejda ara twalim, sinna, Iâannec $ef usgeld. Iêeppem i yiîij d waggur ad ddun, akw, ar lajel ipwassnen. Iseyyi lameô, Ipfeûûil issekniyen, amar a pepputebbtem $ef temlilit d Mass nnwen. Neppa i Isswesâen tamurt. Irra degs idurar, isaffen. Irra tayuga di yal ppemôa. Ip$ummu ass s yiv. Deg waya, s tidep, d issekniyen i ugdud ipxemmimen. Di tmurt, tibêirin tioiratin, leonanat n téuôin, nnaâma, tizdayin, v$an ne$ ur v$in, cerken aman nnsen. Nesmenyaf kra i kra, i wuççi. Deg waya, s tidep, d issekniyen i ugdud ifehmen. Ma twehmev, issewham ay d qqaôen: "ma nu$al d akal, day fella$, s tidep, lxelq amaynut"? D wigi i inekôen Mass nnsen. Wigi, azaglu $ef tmegôav. Wigi d at tmes, nitni, degs, ad wekkôen. Sêaren k ar tucmip, uqbel ise$. Ni$ vôant am tigi, uqbel nnsen. Mass ik, s tidep, $uôeS ssmaê i imdanen deg wayen ccven. Mass ik, s tidep, Iwâaô deg uâaqeb. La qqaôen wid ijehlen: "a lemmer id irs $uôes ussekni, s$uô Mass is". Keçç, d aneddaô kan. I yal agdud, win inehhun. Öebbi Iéôa i illan di yal tadist, amek teddun inzikmiren. Yal cci, $uôeS, s lmizan. Amusnaw n wayen iffren akked wayen ur neffir. Ameqwôan, Aâlayan. Iâuva segwen win i$emven awal, d win it iberêen, win iffren deg iv, d win d ivehôen deg wass. Isâa iâssasen zdat es, deffir es, pêaraben fellas, s lameô n Öebbi. Öebbi, s tidep, ur Ipbeddil i illan deg ugdud, alamma bedlen i illan deg iman nnsen. Ma Irad Öebbi ayen n dir, i ugdud, ur t itekkes yiwen. Ur sâin amâiwen, war Neppa. D Neppa i wen d Ippawin lebôaq, degs tugdi, asirem. Isskar ed asigna aéayan. Tesbuccuâ aS termegt, s ccekôan, akken lmalayek, seg wakken ugadent eP. Ippazen ed ssiâqat, Ipêaz yisent win i S ihwan. Nitni pnamaren $ef Öebbi. Neppa teqseê tezmert iS. £uô Neppa, anuju n tidep. Wid u$uô la pnujun, war Neppa, ur asen d pparan s wacemma. Am win issendin ifassen i waman, ib$a ad awven s imi s, ur ibbwiv ar leb$i s. Anuju ijehliyen ar ttelfan kan. I Öebbi la kennun wid illan di tmurt akked igenwan, b$an ne$ ugin, akked tili nnsen, taûebêit, tameddit. Ini: "anwa ay d Mass n tmurt akked igenwan"? Ini: "d Öebbi. Ihi day a pperrem d iêbiben, war Neppa, wid ur nemlik, i yiman nnsen, aba$uô ne$ vveôô"? Ini: "day iaâdel uder$al akked win ipwalin? Ne$, day âadlent tillas akked tafat? Ne$, rran imcurak i Öebbi, i ixelqen am lxelq iS, ufan t ippemcabi"? Ini: "d Öebbi i Ixelqen yal cci. D Neppa ay d Yiwen, d Aqehhaô". Isse$lay ed aman, seg igenni. Serrun deg $ezôan, s leqdeô nnsen. Acercuô ippawi ikuftan ippifliwen. Ppemcabin ikuftan ar wayen fessin di tmes, iwakken ad ûenâen ôôêuê ne$ dduzan. Akka ay d Isskan Öebbi tidep akked tkerkas. Ihi ikuftan ad ppuveggôen, ma d wayen inefâen medden, a d igwri di tmurt. Akka ay d Ippak Öebbi imedyaten. Lfayeq i wid ijawben i Mass nnsen. Wid ur aS njaweb ara, xas ad sâun i illan akw di tmurt, berdayen, ur ten id ifeddu. I widak, leêsab adiran. Axxam nnsen d Loahennama. A tanezdu$t tucmip! Day win iéôan ar ayen i k d irsen, s$uô Mass ik, d tidep, am win idre$len? Siwa uâqilen id ismektayen. Wid iîîfen di laâqed n Öebbi, ur pôuéun nnesba. Wid issemlilen ayen id Iumeô Öebbi ad imlil, u ppagwaden Mass nnsen, u ppagwaden aqeîîi adiran. Wid iûebôen, ssaramen udem n Mass nnsen, bedden i téallit, pseddiqen seg wayen is iten N$at, s tuffra u âinâni, swexxiôen tucmip s yise$. I nitni, agwav s Axxam. Leonanat n Âaden ara kecmen, akked wid ixeddmen ayen ilhan, seg ibabaten nnsen, si tlawin nnsen, si tarwa nnsen. Lmalayek a d ppasent $uôsen si yal tabburt. Tifrat fellawen, ilmend n wayen tûebôem! D asaâdi, wagwav s Axxam! Wid ipôuéun laâqed n Öebbi, deffir lemwafaqa s, wid igezmen ayen d Iumeô Öebbi ad imlil, u ssefsaden di tmurt, wigi, i nitni xezzu, i nitni yir axxam. Öebbi Issugut ôôeéq i win i S ihwan, u Iwezzen. Taâoeb iten tmeddurt n ddunit. Tameddurt n ddunit, d urar kan, zdat laxeôt. La qqaôen wid ijehlen: "a lemmer id iris, $uôes, ussekni s$uô Mass is"! Ssaâd, akked taggara igerzen, i wid iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan. Akka ay k id Nuzen, i lois id zwaren leoyus, ad asen temlev, ayen ik d Nweêêa. Nitni jehlen $uô Uênin. Day ur éôin ara wid iumnen, ar, ma ihwa yaS, Öebbi ad Inhu medden meôôa? Zgan wid ijehlen a ten tewwet ssixîa, ilmend n wayen xeddmen. Ne$ a ppevôu ar tama n yixxamen nnsen, alamma tusa d lemâahda n Öebbi. Öebbi, s tidep, ur Ipzeggil ppaâud. Ni$ mmaâlken, uqbel ik, deg imazanen. Ooi$ lmudda i wid ijehlen, sinna, Ïîfe$ ten. Wid ijehlen, âaobent pen nncub nnsen. Ppuveôôfen seg ubrid. Win Itlef Öebbi, ur isâi w ara t inhun. Fellasen aâaqeb, di tmeddurt n ddunit. Aâaqeb n laxert, s tidep, aâer. Taggara ijehliyen, d times. Wid iwumi Nefka Tazmamt, ad feôêen s wayen i k d irsen. Illa wayen ugin kra ikabaren. Ini: "pwamôe$ kan ad âabde$ Öebbi, ur aS pcarake$. Pnuju$ $uôeS, tu$alin iw $uôeS". سُوۡرَةُ اِبۡرَاهِيۡمَ Alô. سُوۡرَةُ الۡحِجۡرِ Alô. Wigi d issekniyen n Tezmamt, u d Leqwôan ipbegginen. Ahat wid ijehlen ssaramen ad ilin d imvuâen. Eoo iten ad ççen, ad zhun, a ten issedhu usirem. Deqqal ad éôen. سُوۡرَةُ النَّحۡلِ Ad ias lameô n Öebbi, ur pêirit $uôes. Gedha s yiS! Ay Aâlay, sennig wayen pcaraken. Ixelq ed amdan si tiqqit; atan iu$al aS, d axûim n ûûeê. Ixelq awen d lmal, segsen iceîîiven iêman, aba$uô, u, segsen, teppeppem. D ccbaêa nnwen mara ten id terrem, u mara ten teksem. D Öebbi i Ippawin d ubrid. Ff$en segs. Ma ihwa yaS, a kwen Inhu meôôa. D Neppa i wen d Isse$layen aman seg igenni. Segsen tissit nnwen, segsen ttjuô i itepp lmal. Deg waya, s tidep, issekniyen i ugdud ifehmen. I wen d Ixleq di tmurt, degs initen imgarraden. Deg waya, s tidep, assekni i ugdud ismektayen. D Neppa i Inuben s yill, iwakken a pteppem, segs, aksum aleqqaq, a d teksem, segs, rrêuê i teppeqqnem. A pwaliv lbabuô ipcerrig it, iwakken a pnadim si lfevl iS, amar a ppesnemmrem. Issers idurar $ef tmurt, ur teppembwiwil yiswen; isaffen, iberdan, amar a ppepwanham; timuliwin: s yitran, nitni pwanhan. Day Win Ixelqen am win ur nxelleq? Day ur d tesmektayem ara? Ur ppara, ar tama n Öebbi, ôebbi nniven, mulac a ppepwaveggôev ar Loahennama d ambaûi, d amnafeq. Day wen d Ifren Mass nnwen arrac, u Iddem, i iman iS, tullas, si lmalayek? Ini: "lemmer llin yides iôebbiten, akken la d qqaôen, yili ad nadin abrid ara ten iawin ar n Bab n usgeld". Gedha s yiS, aîas i Aâlay sennig wayen d qqaôen! Ppanzen aS igenwan di ûa, tamurt, u wayen illan degsen. Ur illi wayen ur aS neppanez, ur T Nesbuccuâ s ccekôan. Maca, ur tfehmem ara annuz nnsen. Ih, Neppa Iêellem, Ipsemmiê. Mara teqqaôev Leqwôan, Neppara, garak d wid ur numin ara s laxeôt, aêurrim abavni. Nerra $ef ulawen nnsen ssteô, iwakken ur t fehmen; di tmejjin nnsen, tiâéegt. Ma tesmektiv d, di Leqwôan, Mass ik d Yiwen, ad zzin akin, s u$unfu. Nekwni, Nif akw akken Neéôa, acu iwumi sellen, mara k ssemêasen, mara hedôen, mi qqaôen imednas: "la teppeddum kan d urgaz iwumi sseêren". Wali amek i k d bbwin imedyaten. Nnetlafen. Ur zmiren ad afen abrid. Nnan: "day mi nu$al d i$san, d a$webbaô, d ûûeê a d nu$al di lxelq amaynut"? Ini: "ilit d azôu ne$ d uzzal, ne$ d lxelq id iusan deg idmaren nnwen". A d inin: "anwa ara a $ d irren"? Ini: "d Win ikwen id Ixelqen, abrid amenzu". Ad huzen iqweôôa nnsen $uôek, ad inin: "melmi ayagi"? Ini: "izmer ad yili iqeôb ed". Ass ideg ara awen d Isiwel, a d tjawbem s ccekôan iS, a p$ilem cwiî kan ay teqqimem. Ini i imdanen iw ad inin awal ifuqen. Cciîan, s tidep, isskar ameôéi garasen. Ih, Cciîan d acengu n ûûeê i umdan. Mass nnwen Yif akw akken ikwen Issen. Ad Iêun fellawen, ma Ib$a; a kwen Iâaqeb ma Ib$a. Ur k id Nuzen ara d awkil nnsen. Mass ik Yif akw akken Iéôa i illan di tmurt akked igenwan. Ni$ Nesmenyaf kra n lambiyya i wiyav. I Dawed Nefka Ihellilen. Ini: "nujet $eô wid tepkabarem, war Neppa. Ur zmiren ad awen kksen ccqa, ne$ a t bedlen. Wigi u$uô la pnujun, la pqelliben ppawil ara ten isqeôben nezzeh ar Mass nnsen. Ssaramen aêunu S, ppagwaden aâaqeb iS". Ih, aâaqeb n Mass ik, issagwad. Ur telli temdint ur Nesquccu, uqbel ass n tnekra, ne$ ur Nâaqeb s leqseê. Ayagi iura di Tezmamt. I £ iîîfen $ef uceggaâ issekniyen, d nnkeô nnsen, kan, s$uô imezwura. Nuzen ed tal$wemt i Tamud, d ayen pwalin. Densen p. Ur d Neppazen issekniyen siwa i ussigwed. Mi k Nenna: "Mass ik, s tidep, Izzi i imdanen". Ma dayen i k Nerra teéôiv t, d ahewwel kan i medden. Akken ttejôa tamenâult di Leqwôan. Nessagwad iten. Ay sen d irennu siwa nnfaq ameqwôan. Mi Nenna i lmalayek: "knumt i Adem", knant, siwa Iblis. Inna: "day ad knu$ i win Txelqev s talaxt"? Inna: "Twalav wagi i Tâuzzev sennig iw, lemmer a yi Teooev, ar ass n tnekra, war ccekk, ad $wu$ tarwa s, siwa ixeîîayen". Inna: "Öuê! Wid, segsen, i iddan yidek, ihi, aqeîîi nnwen d Loahennama, d aqeîîi meqqwôen. Laâaj win iwumi tzemôev, degsen, s ta$wect ik. £ewwes fellasen s imnayen ik, d iterrasen ik. Ecrek yidsen ayla, tarwa. Âahed asen". I yasen iâahed Cciîan, siwa a$uôôu. " Ma d imdanen iW, ur tesâiv adabu fellasen". Mass ik Iqadd d Awkil. Mass nnwen, i wen Isselêayen lbabuô di yill, a pnadim lfevl iS. Ih, Neppa Ipêunu fellawen. Ma tevôa yidwen lmuûiba di yill, ayen u$uô tepnujum, war Neppa, ittellif. Mi kwen Isellek ar lberr, twexxôem. Amdan izga d lkaraâ. Day t$ilem ur Ipseggix ara tamurt yiswen, ne$ ur awen d Ippazen ara tabucivant, d$a ur teppafem awkil? Ne$ day t$ilem ur kwen id Ippara ara tikelt nniven, ad awen d Iazen aûeôûaô, a kwen I$mes ilmend n tijehli nnwen, sinna ur teppafem, mgal a£, amalal? Ni$ Nkeyyes tarwa n Adem. Nebbwi ten di lberr, di yill, N$at iten s wayen ilhan, Nesmenyaf iten, nezzeh, i waîas seg wid i Nexleq. Ass ideg ara Nenced akw imdanen, s imvebôen nnsen; win id tusa tezmamt is yeffus is, widak ad $ôen tazmamt nnsen, ur pwadensen s tissegnit; win illan d ader$al di tagi, ad yili d ader$al di laxeôt, ad izid di tuff$a n ubrid. S tidep, qôib i k hewwlen $ef wayen i k d Nweêêa, a d tesnulfuv ayen nniven, mgal a£. D$a, a k rren d aêbib. Lemmer ur k Ntebbet ara, qôib tmalev cwiî $uôsen. Yili ad ak Nesâaddi tudert akked tmeppant, berdayen, sinna, ur teppafev, mgal a£, w ara k isellken. Ih, qôib i k id srewlen si tmurt, a k id ssuff$en segs. Yili cwiî kan ara d gwrin, deffir ek. D tannumi imazanen nne£, id Nuzen, uqbel ik. Ur teppafev ara abeddel, di lâadda nne£. Bedd i téallit mi istu$la yiîij, alamma d tellis n yiv. Leqwôan, tafrara. Ih, Leqwôan, tafrara, isâa inagan. Aâwez yis kra n yiv, d nnafila k, amar a k id Irr Mass ik, deg umkan i pcekkiôen. Ini: "a Mass iw! Ssekcem iyi, anekcum n tidep. Ssuffe$ iyi, tuff$a n tidep. Efk iyi, s$uôeK, adabu ipselliken". Ini: "tusa d tidep, $abent tkerkas. Ih, tikerkas ilaq ad $abent". Nesrusu d, si Leqwôan, ayen illan d êellu akked uêunu i lmumnin. I irennu, i imednas, siwa lexsaôa. Ma N$at amdan ad iwexxeô, ad iveôôef iman is. Ma iêuza t wugur ad iayes. Ini: "yal yiwen ixeddem akken ipwali. Mass nnwen Yif akw akken i Issen anwa i ipwanhan kteô". Steqsan k id $ef ôôuê. Ini: "ôôuê si lameô n Mass iw. Drus kan n tmusni i wen ippunefken". Ma ihwa ya£, a Nekkes ayen i k Nweêêa. D$a ur teppafev, mgal a£, awkil, siwa aêunu s$uô Mass ik. Ih, lfevl iS, i keçç, izga meqqweô. Ini: "lemmer ad mlilen imdanen akked leonun, iwakken a d awin am Leqwôan agi, ur d ppawin i t icban, xas mâawanen". Ni$ Nefka d i imdanen, di Leqwôan agi, si yal imedyaten. Tegwti n yimdanen ur b$in, siwa tijehli. Nnan: "ur k neppamen alamma tesfeggvev a$ d a$balu, si tmurt; ne$, tesâiv leonan n tezdayin akked tfeôôant, ideg feggven isaffen; ne$, a d tesse$liv igenni d ifeûlan, akken i $ tzuxxev; ne$, a d tasev s Öebbi akked lmalayek, zdat nne$; Ne$ a ppesâuv axxam imzewweq, ne$ a ppaliv s igenni. Ur neppamen, s walluy ik, alamma tessersev ane$ d tazmamt ara n$eô". Ini: "gedha s Mass iw! Day lli$ d ayen nniven, siwa d amdan amazan"? I iîîfen imdanen ur uminen, mi ten id tusa nnhaya, mara d inin kan: "Iuzen ed Öebbi amdan d amazan". Ini: "lemmer llint, di tmurt, lmalayek, teddunt di laman, yili Nessers asent ed, seg igenni, lmelk amazan". Ini: "Iqadd Mass iw d Anagi, gari yidwen. Neppa, s tidep, Ipwali imdanen iS, Issen iten". Win Inha Öebbi, atan idda d ubrid. Wid Itlef, ur asen teppafev imawlan, war Neppa, d awez$i. A ten id Nefser ass n tnekra $ef udmawen nnsen, dre$len, gugmen, âaégen. Axxam nnsen d Loahennama. Mi tenqes tmes, ad asen Nernu ajajiê. D wagi ay d aqeîîi nnsen, imi nekôen issekniyen nne£, u nnan: "day mi nu$al d i$san, d a$webbaô, a d nu$al di lxelq amaynut"? Ne$, day ur walan ara ar Öebbi i Ixelqen tamurt akked igenwan, Izmer a d Ixleq i ten icban? Irra yasen lajel, ur degs ccekk. Ur b$in imednas, siwa tijehli. Ini: "lemmer tesâim igerrujen uêunu n Mass iw, ur ten tepnalem, a ppagwadem a ten tûeôôfem. Amdan izga d imceêêi". Ni$ Nefka, i Musa, tza issekniyen iberrzen. Steqsi At Isôail. Mi d iusa $uôsen, inna yas Ferâun: "a Musa! Nek, wala$, war ccekk, seêêern ak". Inna: "ni$ teéôiv ur d issers yiwen wigi, d tiftilin, siwa Mass n tmurt akked igenwan. Nek, wala$, a Ferâun, war ccekk, tîeêênev". Ib$a a ten iééaâ si tmurt, N$emmeq it, akked wid iddan yides, meôôa. Deffir es, Nenna i At Isôail: "zed$et tamurt. Mi d tusa lemâahda n laxeôt, a kwen id Nawi, d îayfat". Nessers it id s tidep. S tidep, ay d irs. Nuzen ik id, kan, i ubecceô d uneddeô. Leqwôan Nfeôq it, iwakken a t temlev i medden, s laâqel. Nessader it id, s l$eôv. Ini: "amnet yis, ne$ qqimet". Ih, ma mlan t i wid tebbwev tussna, uqbel is, ad $lin $ef udmawen, knan. Ad inin: "gedha s Mass nne$! Tûaô lemâahda n Mass nne$". Ad $lin $ef udmawen s imeîîawen. Ad innerni wannuz nnsen. Ini: "nujet $er Öebbi, ne$ nujet $er Uênin. Akken tnujem, ineS ismawen imaânen yifen akw wiyav". Di téallit ik, ur saâlay ûûut ik, ur t ssrusu. Ad isker kan. Ini: "ccekôan i Öebbi, ur Nesâi aqcic, ur Nesâi acrik di tgelda, ur Nesâi bab mgal asdullu". Ssem$weô iT yal tem$weô.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡكَهۡفِ Ccekôan i Öebbi, id Issersen Tazmamt, i uxdim iS. Aâwaj, degs, ur Irri. Tewqem, iwakken a ppâaggen $ef ssxev uwâiô, s$uôeS; u a pbecceô lmumnin ixeddmen ayen ilhan, ar nnsen warraz igerzen. Ad ilin degs, i lebda. A ppâaggen i wid innan: "Öebbi Isâa mmi S". Ur illi wayen ssnen fellas; akken, imezwura nnsen. D awal uqbiê id iff$en seg imawen nnsen. D tikerkas kan ay ssawalen. Ahat a phelkev iman ik, ar loiha nnsen, a p$weblev, imi ur uminen ara s usali agi? Ni$ Nerra i illan di tmurt, d ccbaêa ines, iwakken a Néeô menyif iten, ar igiten ilhan. A Nu$al a Nerr, i illan degs, d akal ibuôen. Ne$ t$ilev d At yifri kan, akked Öaqim, ay d lwehma, ger issekniyen nne£? Mi ssôen iman nnsen ilmeéiyen deg ifri, nnan: "a Mass nne$! Efk ane$ d aêunu s$uôeK; Err a$ lameô nne$ d uûwib". Deg ifri, Nesle$ imeééu$en nnsen, acêal iseggwasen. Sinna, Nessker iten id, a Néeô anta, ger snat n trebbuyaâ, i iêesben acêal qqimen. Nekwni, ad ak Neêku, s tidep, taqsiî nnsen. Nitni, ih, d ilmeéiyen, umnen s Mass nnsen. Nerna yasen nnhaya. Nesseohed ulawen nnsen, mi kren nnan: "Mass nne$ d Mass n tmurt akked igenwan. Ur nepnuju, d awez$i, ar ôebbi, war Neppa, mulac a d nini awal dduni. Widak d agdud nne$. Âabden iôebbiten, war Neppa. Ay$eô ur a$ d bbwin, fellasen, adabu n ûûeê? Anwa i idensen sennig win id igren tikerkas $ef Öebbi? Mi ten tfuôqem, nitni akked wayen âabden war Öebbi, essôet iman nwen deg ifri. Ad awen Izraâ, Mass nnwen, seg uêunu S. Ad awen Iheggi amwanes i lameô nnwen". A pwaliv iîij, mi d inqeô, iwexxeô i ifri nnsen, ar yeffus. Mi i$li, ad asen iâaddi $eô zelmev. Nitni, din, di littsaâ. Ayagi seg issekniyen n Öebbi. Win Inha Öebbi, neppa ipwanha; win Itlef, ur isâi, d awez$i, bab ara t inhun. Ad as tiniv ukin, nitni îîsen. Ntezzi ten yeffus, zelmev. Aydi nnsen, $ef umnaô, iééel ivaôen is. Lemmer a ten twaliv, ad asen trewlev, si tugdi; a k terkeb, segsen, lefqaâ. Akka ay ten id Nessenker, iwakken ad mesteqsin. Inna yiwen segsen: "acêal n lweqt ay tesâaddam"? Nnan d: "nesâadda ass ne$ ur ibbwiv wass". Nnan: "Mass nnwen Yif akw akken Izôa ay tesâaddam. Aznet ar temdint, yiwen segwen, s idrimen agi nnwen. Ad iwali anwa lqut iûfan mavi, ad awen d iawi ôôeéq, segs. Ad iêader iman is, iwakken ur awen ipfaq yiwen. Nitni, war ccekk, ma éôan kwen, a kwen ôeomen, ne$ a kwen rren ar ddin nnsen, d$a ur trebêen, d awez$i". Akka ay sen ten Nessken, iwakken ad éôen ar lemâahda n Öebbi d tidep; u, $ef yimir, ur illi ccekk. Mi mqellaân $ef lameô nnsen, nnan: "bnut axxam sennig sen. Mass nnsen Yif akw akken iten Issen". Nnan wid iwumi iâadda wawal, $ef lameô nnsen: "a nerr, ihi, lemqam sennig sen". Ad inin: "di krav yidsen, aydi nnsen d wis kué"; u ad inin: "di semus yidsen, aydi nnsen d wis sdis", pqelliben tabavnit. U ad inin: "di ûa yidsen, aydi nnsen d wis îam". Ini: "Mass iw Yif akw akken Iéôa amvan nnsen. Drus kan i t iéôan". Ur pnamar fellasen, siwa $ef wayen id ivehôen. Ur ppesteqsay yiwen fellasen. Ur qqaô ta$awsa a p xedme$, s tidep, azekka, siwa ma Irad Öebbi. Mmekti d Mass ik, ma teppuv. Ini: "amar ad iyi Inhu Mass iw, ar wayen yifen ayagi di ûûwab". Sâaddan, deg ifri nnsen, krav twinas iseggwasen, rnan tza nniven. Ini: "Öebbi Yif akw akken Iéôa, acêal sâaddan. IneS tabavnit n tmurt akked igenwan. Amek Neppa Ipwali, Isell! Ur sâin bab, war Neppa. Ur Izdukkul yiwen i useyyi S". Mel ayen ik ed ippuweêêan, si Tezmamt n Mass ik. Ur illi ubeddel deg wawal iS. Ur teppafev ssôan, war Neppa, d awez$i. Üebbeô iman ik, akked wid ipnujun ar Mass nnsen, taûebêit, tameddit, pnadin udem iS. Ur ten tekkes si ger wallen ik, a pvemâav lefnun n tmeddurt n ddunit. Ur ssemêas i win iwumi Nesse$fel ul is, ar usmekti nne£, i iddan d lhawiyya s, iwumi iffuhri lameô. Ini: "tidep s$uô Mass nnwen. Ad iamen win ib$an, ad ijhel win ib$an". Ih, Nhegga d times, i imednas; ad asen zzin iêeoouoa s. Ma ppren d, ad asen ppunefken waman am uzzal ifsin. Ad cwin wudmawen nnsen. A tissit tamcumt, a tanezdu$t tucmip! Ih, wid iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan, s tidep, ur Nveggiâ akafi n win ixedmen ayen ilhan. I wigi, leonanat n Âaden, ddaw sen isaffen ppazzalen. Ad qqnen, dinna, imeqyasen n ddheb, ad lsen iceîîiven izegzawen n leêrir, êewcen s ddheb. Ad élen, degs, $ef imîeôêen izewwqen. A lebsa lâali, a tanezdu$t tumâint! Awi yasen d amedya n sin irgazen. I yiwen, Nefka snat tebêirin n téuôin, Nezzi yasent tizdayin, Nerra iger garasent. Yal tibêirt teppak ed l$ella s, ur ipxuûûu, segs, wacemma. Nesfeggev asif garasent. I$ellet ed ppemôa. Inna i umdakwel is, mi s immeslay: "$elbe$ k taôkunt, iffe$ k alag". Idens iman is mi ikcem leonan is, inna: "ur cukke$ ara, d awez$i, ad iqucc wayagi. Ur cukke$ ara ad yili yimir, u ma bbwve$ ar Mass iw, ard affe$, war ccekk, ayen yifen aya, deg umekkan is". Inna yas umdakwel is, mi s immeslay: "day tnekôev Win ik Ixelqen seg wakal, sinna, si tiqqit, sinna, Imessel ik d argaz? Maca, Neppa d Öebbi, Mass iw. Ur pcarake$ yiwen, i Mass iw. Lemmer id tenniv, mi tkecmev ar tebêirt ik: akken Irad Öebbi. Ur telli tezmert siwa s$uô Öebbi. Ma twalav iyi d, nek, tifev iyi ayla, tarwa, Izmer Mass iw ad iyi d Ifk ayen i ifen tibêirt ik. A d Iazen $uôes ssxev, seg igenni, a ppu$al d aêecraruf issiccigen; ne$, ad zzren waman is, ur ten teppafev, d awez$i". Tqucc l$ella s. D$a la izeyyeô ifassen is, $ef wayen iseôôef fellas. Tqucc tfeôôant is. Inna: "a yamxix iw, a lemmer ur curke$ yiwen, i Mass iw"! Ur as illi urbaâ ara t isellken, war Öebbi. Ur isellek iman is. Akka, laânaya s$uô Öebbi, Tidep. Yif akw i ukafi, Yif akw i taggara. Awi yasen d amedya n tmeddurt n ddunit. Am aman id Nesse$li seg igenni. Eâluâlen yissen im$an n tmurt. D$a u$alen d asa$uô, issebruzzaâ iten wavu. Ni$ Öebbi Izmer i yal cci. Ayla akked dderya d ccbaêa n tmeddurt n ddunit. Ar Mass ik, leûlaê idumen ifen ten i ukafi, ifen ten i tmeôoiwt. Ass ideg ara Nesselêu idurar, a pwaliv tamurt d aza$aô. A ten Nefser, ur Neppaoa yiwen segsen. A d rsen zdat Mass ik, d leûfuf: "ni$ tusam a£ d, akken ikwen Nexleq tikelt tamenzut. Irna tetebbtem ar ur awen Neppara ppaâud, d awez$i". Ters ed Tezmamt. A pwaliv ibe$wviyen s uêebbiô, $ef wayen illan degs. Qqaôen: "a yamxix nne$! Acimi tazmamt agi ur teooi ayen meééiyen, u wayen meqqwôen, armi ten teêseb"? Ufan illa wayen xedmen. Mass ik ur Idennis yiwen. Mi Nenna i lmalayek: "knumt i Adem", knant, siwa Iblis. Neppa, si leonun, iaâûa lameô n Mass is. Day a ten terrem, neppa akked tarwa s, d imawlan, war Nek? U nitni d icenga nnwen! D abdil ucmit n imednas. Ur ten Rri$ d inagan n lxelq n tmurt akked igenwan, ne$ n lxelq nnsen. Ur Ïîife$ im$eôôqen d imâiwnen. Ass ideg ara d Yini: "neccdet wid iyI terram d icriken iW". Ad asen siwlen, ur asen d pparan. Nerra, garasen, asif n twa$it. Ibe$wviyen ad walin times. ÊëËûan ar nitni, degs, ara $lin. Ur ppafen, segs, tisensert. Ni$ Nefka d, di Leqwôan agi, yal amedya, i imdanen. Maca, ipnamar umdan sennig akw. D acu i iîîfen imdanen ad amnen, mi ten id tusa nnhaya, u ad ste$fôen Mass nnsen? Ar ten id tas kan, tin ivôan d imezwura, ne$ ar d irs, zdat sen, uâaqeb? Ur Neppazen imazanen, siwa i ubecceô d uneddeô. Wid ijehlen pnamaren, s tkerkas, îîeggiôen yissent tidep. Pmaâliken $ef issekniyen iW, akked wayen i$ef ppunedôen. Anwa idensen sennig win iwumi d pwafekkôen issekniyen n Mass is, iwexxeô asen, u ippu i ixdem ufus is. Ih, Nerra aêurrim $ef wulawen nnsen, ur t fehhmen; akked tiâéegt deg imeééu$en nnsen. Ma tneccdev ten ar nnhaya, ur pwanhan, d awez$i. Mass ik Ipsemmiêen, d Bab uêunu. Lemmer ad Iêud fellasen ilmend n wayen kesben, ad I$iwel ar uâaqeb nnsen. Maca, sâan ppaâud, ur ppafen segs tisensert. Timdinin nni i Nesqucc mi densent, Nga ppaâud i usquccu nnsent. Mi inna Musa i uqeddac is: "ur êebbse$ alamma bbwve$ ar umlili n sin ilellen, xas ad sâaddi$ tallit". Mi bbwven ar umlili nnsen, ppun aslem nnsen. Iu$al ar yill d ilelli. Mi zegren, inna i uqeddac is: "awi a$ d imekli nne$, ni$ naâteb deg inig nne$ agi". Inna: "ur twalav ara, mi nreyyeê ar teéôut, nek ppu$ en aslem? D Cciîan kan iyi isseppun ur ak nni$. Ibbwi abrid is ar yill, d lwehma"! Inna: "d ayagi ay neb$a". D$a u$alen d $ef isurifen nnsen. Ufan d amdan seg imdanen nne£, iwumi Nefka aêunu s$uône£. Neslemd as tussna i illan $uône£. Inna yas Musa: "Ma ad ddu$ yidek, ad iyi tesêefvev ay tesnev n ûûwab"? Inna d: "keçç, s tidep, ur tezmiôev, yidi, a pûebôev. Amek ara tûebôev i wayen i$ef ur tesâiv asali"? Inna: "ad iyi tafev, ma Irad Öebbi, d aûebôi. Ur pnaqwame$ lameô ik". Inna: "ma teddiv yidi, ur iyi d steqsay $ef wacemma, alamma smekti$ k id fellas". Lêan, armi rekben di lbabuô. Ixeôq it. Itlef Ferâun agdud is, ur inhi. A yAt Isôail! Ni$ Nsellek ikwen seg ucangu nnwen. Nefka yawen ppaâud, ar loiha tayeffus n udrar. Nessers awen d lmenna, ifeôôuoen. Inna: "ih, ni$ Njeôôeb agdud ik, deffir ek. Itelf iten Usamiri". Iu$al ed Musa s agdud is, s zzâaf d wumri. Inna: "a yagdud iw! Day ur awen Ifka ara, Mass nnwen, lemâahda lâali? سُوۡرَةُ الۡاَنۡۢبِيَآءِ Iqeôb ed i medden uqeîîi nnsen, u nitni stehzan, ur d rzin. Ur ten d ippas usmekti amaynut, s$uô Mass nnsen, mebla ma ppuraren, mara s sslen. Ur d rzin wulawen nnsen. A tawa$it nnwen, ilmend n wayen d teggarem! IneS kra illan di tmurt akked igenwan. Wid illan $uôeS, ur sme$wôen ara iman nnsen, $ef uâabed iS. Ur âaggun. Ppanzen iv akked wass, ur sêissifen. Ni$ nella ne$fel $ef waya. U, aâer, nella d imednas. Kunwi, s tidep, akked wayen tâabden, war Öebbi, d is$aôen n Loahennama. £ures, kunwi, teppeddum. Lemmer llin widak d iôebbiten, ur p keççmen. سُوۡرَةُ الۡحَجِّ A yimdanen! Ëezzbet i Mass nnwen, zzenzla n yimir, stidep, d tadyant tabarart. Ass ideg ara p twalim, yal timôebbit a ppeppu win tessuîîuv, yal tadist a ppexseô. A pwaliv imdanen ssekôen, ur sskiôen. Maca, aâaqeb n Öebbi iwâaô. Ger yimdanen, illa win ipnamaren $ef Öebbi, war tamusni. Iteddu d yal cciîan imcebbwel. Iura fellas: "ar wagi, win i t irran d bab is, ara t itlef, s tidep, u a t inheô ar uâaqeb ujajiê". A yimdanen! Ma di ccekk ay tellam f tnekra, ihi, Nekwni, s tidep, Nxelq ikwen seg wakal, sinna, si tiqqit n l$ella, sinna, seg urgan, sinna, si tecriêt, texleq ur texliq, iwakken ad awen Nbeggen. Neppara, di tâabbuvin, ayen i £ ihwan, alamma d lajel ipwassnen. Sinna, Nessuffu$ ikwen id d llufanat, sinna a ppim$uôem. Segwen llan wid ippemmten, u segwen win ara iawven d awessur, ard ur ippisin acemma seg wayen issen. A pwalid akal d a$uôaô. Ma Nesse$li d ageffur fellas, ad ikker, ad icuff, a d ifk tayuga n yal ûûenf uziyn n le$ôus. Ayagi, acku Öebbi d Tidep. D Neppa id Issidiren lmeggtin. Neppa Izmer i yal cci. U imir a d ias, war ccekk fellas. U Öebbi a d Issker wid illan di tneîlin. Ger imdanen, illa win ipnamaren $ef Öebbi, war tamusni, ne$ nnhaya, ne$ Tazmamt ifeten. Icuff aqenduô, iwakken ad itlef seg ubrid n Öebbi. Fellas xezzu di ddunit. Deg wass n tnekra, a Nessuk fellas aâaqeb n tmeô$iwt. Ayagi, $ef wayen id urwen ifassen ik. U Öebbi ur Idennis imdanen. Ger yimdanen, win iâabden Öebbi, $ef rrif. Ma iusa t id lxiô, ad ithenni yis. Ma iusa t id uhewwel, ad iswexxeô udem is. Öuêent as, ddunit, laxeôt. Ayagi d lexsaôa n ûûeê. Ipnuju, war Öebbi, ar wayen ur t neîîuôôu, ur t neffaâ. D wagi ay d ttelfan u$miq. Ipnuju ar bu vveôô izwaren aba$uô ines. Ay d bab ucmit, ay d acrik ucmit. Öebbi, s tidep, ad Issekcem wid iumnen, i ixeddmen ayen ilhan, ar Loennet, ddaw as isaffen ppazzalen. Öebbi, s tidep, Ixeddem ayen Ib$a. Win i oaâlen ur t Ipsellik ara Öebbi, di ddunit, di laxeôt, ad iâalleq amrar s igenni, sinna, ad igzem nnefs is. Ad iéeô ma tiêêeôci s temêa ayen i t irêan. Öebbi, s tidep, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu. Wid itehmen tilawin nnsen, ur sâin inagan, siwa iman nnsen, yiwen segsen ad iggal s Öebbi, kué iberdan, ar neppa d bab n tidep, akked ubrid wis smus ar a t Ixzu Öebbi ma iskaddeb. Ur teppuâaqeb tmeîîut, ma teggul s Öebbi, kué iberdan, ar neppa seg wid iskadben, akked ubrid, wis smus ar fellas zzâaf n Öebbi, ma issawel ed tidep. A lemmer ur illi fellawen lfevl n Öebbi akked uêunu S! Öebbi, s tidep, Issuruf, d Bab n ûûwab. Ih, wid isweûlen tikerkas, d agraw segwen. Ur p$ilit d cceôô i kunwi, xaîi, d lxiô nnwen. Yal yiwen, degsen, ibbwi ayen ibbwi ubekkav. Aâaqeb abarar i win, segsen, i ibbwin amur ameqwôaêan. A lemmer lmumnin, argaz tameîîut, mi s slan, meyyzen lxiô, deg iman nnsen, u nnan: "wagi d tikerkas ibanen"! A lemmer d bbwin, fellas, kué inagan! Ma ur d bbwin ara inagan, ar Öebbi, wigi, d ikeddaben. Lemmer ur illi fellawen lfevl n Öebbi akked uêunu S, di ddunit akked laxeôt, a ppesâaddim aâaqeb abarar $ef wayen i$ef temcawaôem. Ih, wid ib$an a d iazel lâaô, ar wid iumnen, fellasen aâaqeb aqeôêan di ddunit, di laxeôt. Öebbi Issen, kunwi ur tessinem. A lemmer ur illi fellawen lfevl n Öebbi akked uêunu S! U Öebbi d Umâin, Ipêunu. A wid iumnen! Ur teddut di lateô n Cciîan. Win iteddun di lateô n Cciîan, ar la iteddu di lâaô akked tuccva. Öebbi Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu. Ih, wid ipqeôôiven tilawin zeddigen, istehzan, iumnen, ad pwaxzun di ddunit, di laxeôt. Fellasen aâaqeb abarar. Ass ideg ara d cehhden $ef igiten nnsen, ilsawen nnsen, ifassen nnsen, ivaôen nnsen, assen, ad asen Ifk Öebbi ayen ppalasen, s tidep. Ad éôen ar Öebbi d Tidep ibanen. Yir tlawin i yir irgazen, yir irgazen i yir tlawin. Tilawin n lâali i irgazen n lâali, irgazen lâali i tlawin n lâali. Wigi ur ppkan deg wayen qqaôen. I nitni, ssmaê akked ôôeéq ukyis. A wid iumnen! Ur keçmet ixxamen ur nelli nnwen, alamma s tsriê, u alamma tselmem $ef imawlan nnsen. Ppif akka i kunwi, amar a d tesmektim. Ma ur tufim êedd degsen, ur keçmet alamma s tsriê. Ma nnan awen d: "u$alet", u$alet. Yif it wakka i ûûfawa nnwen. Öebbi Iéôa ayen txeddmem. Ulac u$ilif fellawen ma tkecmem ixxamen ur nepwazde$, ma tella t$awsa nnwen degsen. Ini i tid iumnen ad brunt i wallen nnsent, ad ssôent tuzzuft nnsent, ur d sskanent, di zzin nnsent, siwa ayen d ivehôen segs, ad $umment idmaren nnsent. Ur d sskanent ccbuê nnsent, siwa i irgazen nnsent, ne$ ibabaten nnsent, ne$ im$aôen nnsent, ne$ iqcicen nnsent, ne$ irbiben nnsent, ne$ atmaten nnsent, ne$ iqcicen n watmaten nnsent, ne$ wid n tsetmatin nnsent, ne$ tiqeddacin nnsent, ne$ taklatin nnsent, ne$ iqeddacen imudduzen, ne$ arrac ur nelleméi. سُوۡرَةُ الۡقَصَصِ Ïsm. Atnan issekniyen n Tezmamt ipbegginen. Ad ak d Neêku si teqûiî n Musa akked Ferâun, s tidep, i ugdud iumnen. سُوۡرَةُ الۡعَنۡكَبُوۡتِ Alm. Day $ilen imdanen a ten ooen qqaôen: "numen", u nitni ur ppuhewwlen? Ni$ Nhewwel wid i ten id izwaren. War ccekk, ad Yissin Öebbi wid iqqaôen tidep, ad Yissin ikeddaben. Wid iugin issekniyen n Öebbi, akked temlilit yideS, widak ad aysen aêunu W. I widak, aâaqeb aqeôêan. Tiririt n ugdud is, siwa mi d nnan: "en$et ep, ne$ sseô$et ep". Isellek it Öebbi, si tmes. سُوۡرَةُ السَّجۡدَةِ Alm. Tarusi n Tezmamt, ur illi degs ccekk, s$uô Mass imavalen. Ne$ a d inin: "isnulfa p id". سُوۡرَةُ الزُّمَرِ Tarusi n Tezmamt s$uô Öebbi, Uzmir, Bab n ûûwab. Ih, Nessader ak d Tazmamt, s tidep. Ihi, aâbed Öebbi, s laâqida i Neppa. Day maççi i Öebbi laâqida? Wid ippaddamen imawlan, war Neppa, nnan: "naâbed iten kan, iwakken ad a$ rnun aseqôeb ar Öebbi". Ih, Öebbi ad Iêudd garasen, $ef wayen i$ef mgarraden. Ay d ismektayen, kan, d uâqilen". Ini: "a yimdanen iW iumnen, êezzbet i Mass nnwen. Ayen ilhan i wid imaânen di ddunit agi. Tamurt n Öebbi tewsaâ. Ihi, arraz, war aktili, ad ippunefk i iûebôiyen". Wid ur numin ara, âaégent tmejjin nnsen. Neppa, i nitni, d tider$elt. Widak pwanecden seg umkan ibaâden". Ni$ Nefka yas Tazmamt i Musa. Mgarraden fellas. Lemmer ur d izwar ara wawal s$uô Mass ik, yili tefra garasen. Nitni, fellas, di ccekk imcebbwel. Win ixedmen ayen ilhan, i iman is; win iccven, mgal iman is. Mass ik ur Idennis ara imdanen. £uôeS ay tella tmusni n yimir. Ur d iteffe$ uzway si txeddact is, ur treffed nnta tadist, ur tepparew, siwa ma Iéôa. Ass ideg ar asen Isiwel: "anda ten icriken iW"? Ma Nseêess as aêunu nne£, deffir ccqa i t iêuzan, war ccekk, ad yini: "ayagi inu. Ur cukke$ ara imir a d ias. Ma bbwve$ s afus n Mass iw, ad afe$ $uôeS ûûam". Ih, a Nbeggen ayen xedmen, i wid ijehlen, u, ih, ad Nsâaddi fellasen aâaqeb iwaâôen. Ma N$at amdan ad iwexxeô, izzi akin. Ma iêuza t lêif, ad ipnuju, irennu. Ini: "tmeyyzem ma iusa d s$uô Öebbi, u kunwi tnekôem t"? Anwa innetlafen sennig win illan di ticuîna tu$miqt? سُوۡرَةُ الشُّوۡرٰي Ëm. Âsq. Akka i Iweêêa i keçç, akked wid ik id izwaren, Öebbi, Uzmir, Bab n ûûwab. IneS i illan deg igenwan, i illan di tmurt. Neppa, d Aâlayen, d Ameqwôahan. Qôib ad ccergen igenwan seg ixfawen nnsen, mara d lhint lmalayek deg usbuccaâ s ccekôan n Mass nnsent, u ssuturent ad pwassemêen kra illan di tmurt. War ccekk, Öebbi Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu? Wid irran imawlan, war Neppa, Iquôaâ ten Öebbi. Ur telliv, keçç, d awkil nnsen. W ad ak imlen, ahat imir iqeôb ed? Ëaren $uôes wid ur numin ara yis. Ma d wid iumnen, ugaden t; éôan ar neppa d tidep. Ih, wid icukken deg imir, haaten, war ccekk, di ttelfan u$miq. A pwaliv imednas feqâen ilmend n wayen kesben, u neppa iddehm ed fellasen. Wid iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan, ad ilin di tebêirin n leonanat. Nnsen i sen ihwan $uô Mass nnsen. سُوۡرَةُ الزُّخۡرُفِ Ëm. S Tezmamt ipbegginen! Nerra p d Leqwôan s taâôabt, amar a pfehmem. Neppa, ih, ata $uône£, ar Tyimmap n Tezmamt, d aâlayan, d uûwib. سُوۡرَةُ الدُّخَانِ Ëm. S Tezmamt ipbegginen! Nessader ip id, ih, deg iv iôqan. Ih, Nekwni, Nella d ineddaôen! Iban ed degs, yal lameô uûwib. Lameô s$uône£. Ih, Nekwni Nella d wid Ippaznen.
