Menyif nitni ne$ agdud n Tubbaâ, akked wid i ten id izwaren? Nessenger iten. S tidep, nitni llan d ibe$wviyen. Ur Nexliq ara tamurt, igenwan, akked wayen illan garasen, i wurar. Nxelq iten kan s tidep, maca, tegwti degsen, ur ssinen. S tidep, ass n ufraz, ad mlilen meôôa. Ass ideg aêbib ur i$ennu aêbib, s wacemma; nitni ur pwasellken. Kkes ed wid i$ef Iêun Öebbi. Neppa, s tidep, d Uzmir, Ipêunu. Ih, ttejôa n Zaqqum, uççi umednub, am nnêas ifsin, ippayzag di tâabbuvin, akken ppayzagen waman. "Ddemt ep, zu$ôet ep, ar pnaûfa ujajiê, sinna, smiret sufella uqeôôu s, aâaqeb ippayzagen". "Jeôôeb! Ni$ keçç d uzmir, d ukyis"! Ih, wagi d ayen i la tepcukkum. Wanag wid iêezzben, deg umekkan n laman; di leonanat akked tliwa; lebsa nnsen s leêrir, leêrir iêewwcen. Mqabalen. Akka, a ten Njewweo akked têuôtin lâin. A d ssutren, dinna, yal izwayen, di laman. Ur pjeôôiben, dinna, tameppant, siwa tameppant tamezwarut. Isellek iten seg uâaqeb ujajiê. D lfevl n Mass ik, d wagi ay d rrbeê ameqwôaêan. Nsehhel it kan, s tmeslayt ik, amendeô ma a d mmektin. Ggani, ula d nitni la pganin.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡجَاثِيَةِ Ëm. Tarusi n Tezmamt s$uô Öebbi, Uzmir, Bab n ûûwab. Di tmurt akked igenwan, s tidep, llan issekniyen i lmumnin. Di lxelq nnwen, akked wayen id Issefôuôex n lewêuc, d issekniyen i ugdud ipputebbten. Di lemgarda n yiv akked wass, akked wayen id Issrusu Öebbi n ôôeéq, seg igenni - Issidir yis tamurt, deffir tmeppant is -, deg udewwel n wavu, issekniyen i ugdud ipmeyyizen. D wigi ay d issekniyen n Öebbi; Nemmal ak ten, s tidep. Anwa ameslay ara amnen, deffir Öebbi akked issekniyen iS? A ssxev n yal akeddab amednub! Issemêas i issekniyen n Öebbi, qqaôen as ten, sinna, iggernen di tem$weô, amzun ur asen isli. Ihi, becceô it s uâaqeb aqeôêan. Ma illa wayen iwumi isla, seg issekniyen nne£, ad ittihi fellas. I widak, aâaqeb isdullun. Deffir sen Loahennama. Ur ten i$ennu s wacemma wayen kesben akked wayen rran d imawlan, war Öebbi. I nitni, aâaqeb abarar. Tagi d nnhaya. Wid iugin issekniyen n Mass nnsen, fellasen aâaqeb n daâwessu taqeôêant. Öebbi i Inuben fellawen s yill; ipcali, fellas, lbabuô, s lameô iS; a pnadim l$it iS. Amar a ppesnemrem! Inub fellawen s wayen akw illan deg igenwan, akked wayen illan di tmurt. Akw s$uôeS. S tidep, deg waya, d issekniyen i ugdud ismektayen. Ini i wid iumnen ad semmêen i wid ur negguni ara ussan n Öebbi, iwakken ad Ikafi agdud $ef wayen keppben. Win ixedmen ayen ilhan, i iman is; win ifalîan, mgal is. Sinna, ar Mass nnwen tu$alin nnwen. Ni$ Nefka, i At Isôail, Tazmamt, ûûwab, lambiyya. Nôeéq iten s wayen ilhan. Nesmenyaf iten i imavalen. Nefka yasen abeggen si Lameô. Ur mgarraden, armi i ten id tusa tmusni, wa iqheô wa. Ih, Mass ik ad Iêudd garasen, ass n tnekra, $ef wayen i$ef mgarraden. Sinna, Nebbwi k deg ubrid n Lameô. Ddu degs, ur teddu akked chawi n wid ur nessin. Ih, nitni ur ak d ppawin acemma s$uô Öebbi. Imednas, ih, d imawlan wa n wa. Öebbi d Bab n wid ipêezziben. Ayagi d assekni i l$aci, d nnhaya u d aêunu i ugdud ipputebbten. Ne$ $ilen wid imôôeôen iman nnsen s tucmitin, a ten Neêseb am wid iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan, d imuddiren ne$ d lmeggtin. Dir it uêuddu nnsen. Öebbi Ixleq tamurt akked igenwan, s tidep, iwakken yal amdan ad ippuqeîîi af wayen ikseb. Nitni ur pwadensen. Twalav win irran lhawiyya s d ôebbi is? Itelf it Öebbi, asali $uôeS. Iskweô as ul, timejjin, Irra yas aâbôuq af allen is. Anwa ara t inhun, deffir Öebbi? Day u la tesmektayem ara? Nnan: "i illan kan, d tudert nne$, di ddunit. A nemmet, a nidir. Ad a$ in$en kan d akud". £ef ayagi, ur sâin kra n tmusni. Nitni $ilen kan. Ma mlan asen issekniyen nne£ iberrzen, anamer nnsen, siwa mara d inin: "erret ed imezwura nne$, ma tessawalem tidep"! Ini: "Öebbi Issidir ikwen, sinna, Ineqq ikwen. Sinna a kwen Issemlil ass n tnekra, ur illi degs ccekk". Maca, tegwti n yimdanen ur ssinen. N Öebbi, tagelda n tmurt akked igenwan. Ass ideg ara d ias yimir, ass nni, ad xesôen ucmiten. A pwaliv yal lois $ef tgwecrar, yal lois ipwanced ar tezmamt is. Assa, a p$eltem ayen txeddmem. Tagi d tazmamt nne£, tessawal tidep fellawen. Nella Nepjerrid ayen akw txeddmem. Ihi, wid iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan, a ten Issekcem, Mass nnsen, s aêunu S. Wagi d rrbeê n ûûeê. Wanag wid ijehlen: "day ur awen $ôan ara issekniyen iW? Tesme$wôem iman nnwen, tellam d agdud ibe$wviyen". Mi nnan: "ih, lemâahda n Öebbi, d tidep; imir, ur degs ccekk", tennam: "ur neéôi d acu ay d imir; $uône$ d nnwaya kan, ur nepputebbet". Ad asen d vehôent tucmitin xedmen, ad asen izzi wayen i$ef ttihin. Ad asen Inin: "assa, a kwen Neppu, akken teppum timlilit n wass nnwen agi. Axxam nnwen d times, ur awen illi useîîaô. Ayagi, acku kunwi la tettihim $ef issekniyen n Öebbi. T$uôô ikwen tudert n ddunit. Assa, ur d teff$en segs". Ur isti$fiô êedd fellasen. I Öebbi annuz, Mass igenwan, Mass n tmurt, Mass imavalen. I Neppa akw ayen iufraren, di tmurt akked igenwan. Neppa, d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡاَحۡقَافِ Ëm. Tarusi n Tezmamt s$uô Öebbi, Uzmir, Bab n ûûwab. Ur Nexliq tamurt, igenwan, akked wayen illan garasen, siwa s tidep, ar lajel ipwassnen. Wid ijehlen numren ayen u$uô pwanedôen. Ini: "day ur twalam ara wigi u$uô la tepnujum, war Öebbi? Sseknet iyi d, d acu xelqen si tmurt, ne$ ma sâan amur deg igenwan? Awit iyi d tazmamt id izwaren tagi, ne$ lateô n tmusni, ma tessawalem tidep". Anwa innetlafen sennig wid ipnujun, war Öebbi, $eô wayen ur asen d nepparra, ar ass n tnekra, u nitni stehzan deg unuju nnsen? Mara twafesrem imdanen, ad ilin d icenga nnsen, ad skiddben aâbad nnsen. Ma $ôan asen issekniyen nne£ iberrzen, wid iugin tidep, mi ten id tusa, ad inin: "wagi d ssêur n ûûeê". Ne$ ad inin: "isnulfa t id". Ini: "lemmer it id snulfa$, ur tezmirem ad iyi tsellkem, s wacemma, si Öebbi. Neppa, Yif akw akken Issen, acu têekkum fellas. Iqadd Neppa d Anagi gari yidwen. Neppa, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu. Ini: "ur lli$, ger imazanen, d win id isnulfuyen. Ur éôi$ acu ara ivôun yidi, ne$ yidwen. La îîafaôe$, kan, ayen iyi d ippuweêêan. Aql i, kan, nek, d aneddaô ipbegginen". Ini: "meyyzet ma, ayagi, s$uô Öebbi, u tnekôem t? Icehhed unagi n At Isôail, $ef lmetl is, d$a iumen. Tesme$wrem iman nnwen". Ih, Öebbi ur Inehhu agdud imednas. Nnan wid ijehlen, i wid iumnen: "lemmer d ayen ilhan, ur a$ zeggwiren $uôes". Imi ur pwanhan ara syis, qqaôen: "ayagi d tikerkas n zik". Uqbel is, Tazmamt n Musa, d nnhaya u d aêunu. Tagi d Tazmamt itebbiten, s wawalen n taâôabt, a ppendeô wid idensen, a ppessefôeê lâuûam. Ih, wid iqqaôen: "Mass nne$ d Öebbi, d$a îfen degs, ur ppagaden, ur $weblen". Widak d at Loennet, degs ad wekkôen, d arraz n wayen xeddmen. Nweûûa amdan ar lewqama s imawlan is. Imma s temêen s tadist, temêen di tinnufra. Ger tadist akked ujumi, caret wagguren. Armi ibbwev d anqaqôi, issawev kuéet isegwasen, inna: "a Mass iw! Eoo iyi a K snemmre$ af l$it i $ T$atev, nek akked lwaldin iw; ad xedme$ ayen ilhan ara K iôavin. Efk iyi d tarwa ilhan. Aql i utube$ K, aql i seg imvuâen". £uô wigi, Nqebbel lmefruz igiten nnsen, a Nessuref i tucmitin nnsen, ger at Loennet; d lemâahda n tidep, i sen ippuwaââden. Win innan i imawlan is: "tfuh nnwen! Day yi tâahdem a d kkre$? Ni$ âaddan isuta uqbel i". Nitni teppren tacvaî n Öebbi: "a ssexv ik, amen! Ih, lmâahda n Öebbi, d tidep". A d yini: "ayagi, siwa tiêkayin imezwura". D wigi i$ef iûaô wawal iaânan leoyus n leonun akked yimdanen, i ten id izwaren. Ih, nitni d imexsuôen. I akw tiseddarin n wayen xedmen, iwakken ad yili warraz igiten nnsen. Nitni ur pwadensen. Ass ideg ara kecmen ar tmes, wid ijehlen: "tvegâam tiéidanin i s tezham, di tmeddurt nnwen di ddunit. Assa, a ppeppuqeîîim s uâaqeb isdullun, imi tessem$waôem iman nnwen di tmurt, ur teklalem; imi tellam tbe$wlem". Mmekti d agmat n Âad, mi indeô agdud is deg igidan, u, s tidep, âaddan d ineddaôen zdat es, u zdeffir es: "siwa Öebbi ara tâabdem. Nek ugade$, fellawen, aâaqeb n wass abarar". Nnan d: "day a$ d tusiv, ad a$ tfaôqev akked iôebbiten nne$? Awi a$ d ayen i$ef la $ tessagwadev, ma tessawalev tidep"! Inna: "tamusni ar Öebbi kan. Ssawve$ awen ayen i$ef id ppuceggâa$. Maca, wala$ kwen d agdud ur nessin". Mi t walan d asigna id ileêêun ar t$wezza nnsen, nnan: "wagi d asigna ar a$ d iawin ageffur". Xaîi! D ayen i$ef têarem, d avu, degs aâaqeb aqeôêan; ad isqucc yal cci, s lameô n Mass is. Gwran d ur tepwaliv siwa ixxamen nnsen. Akka i Nepqeîîi igduden ibe$wviyen. Ni$ Nessakrer asen ayen ur awen Nessakrer. Nefka yasen imeééu$en, allen, akked wulawen. Ula i sen d bbwin deg wacemma imeééu$en, allen, akked wulawen, mi skaddben issekniyen n Öebbi. Ayen i$ef ttihin, izzi d fellasen. Ni$ nessenger akw timdinin i wen d izzin, u Nenewwel asent issekniyen, amar a d u$alent s abrid. Acimi ur ten sellken ara wid rran d iôebbiten iééaéan, war Öebbi? Xaîi! Ooan ten. D ayagi ay d tikerkas nnsen, u d wayen id snulfuyen. Mi k ed Nebbwi agraw n leonun, ad ssemêessen i Leqwôan; mi s êedôen, nnan: "êesset"! Mi ifukk, u$alen s agdud nnsen d ineddaôen. Nnan: "a yagdud nne$, aql a$ nesla i Tezmamt id irsen, deffir Musa, id itebbten ayen ip id izwaren, i inehhun ar tidep akked ubrid uwqim. A yagdud nne$, erret awal i uberraê n Öebbi, amnet yiS, ad awen Isemmeê seg ibekkaven nnwen, a kwen Isellek seg uâaqeb aqeôêan". Win isâaweégen i uberraê n Öebbi, ur ipsellik di tmurt, ur ippaf imawlan, war Neppa. Widak di ttelfan n ûûeê. Day ur walan ara ar Öebbi d Win Ixelqen tamurt akked igenwan, ur Ifcil seg uxlaq nnsen? Izmer a d Issider lmeggtin. Ih, Neppa Izmer i yal cci. Ass ideg ara d rsen, ar tmes, wid ijehlen: "maççi s tidep ayagi"? A d inin: "ih, s Mass nne$"! A d Yini: "jeôôbet aâaqeb $ef wayen la tnekôem"! Eûbeô akken ûebôen wid iôeûmen seg imazanen. I nitni, ur p$awal. Ass ideg ara walin acu i sen ippuwaââden, amzun ur kminen siwa saâa n wass. D aberreê: "anwa ara ipwakksen, siwa agdud icemten"?
سُوۡرَةُ مُحَمَّدٍ Wid ijehlen, u ssefôa$en abrid n Öebbi, Itlef igiten nnsen. Wid iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan, umnen s wayen id irsen ar Muêemmed, u neppa d tidep s$uô Mass nnsen; Issemsa yasen tucmitin nnsen, Iûeggem asen lêala nnsen. Ayagi, acku wid ijehlen îîafaôen tikerkas; ma d wid iumnen, îîafaôen tidep n Mass nnsen. Akka id Ippak Öebbi imedyaten nnsen i imdanen. Mara d temlilem akked wid ijehlen, ewwtet ar tmegrav ar ten t$elbem. Arzet pen nezzeh. Sinna, d aserreê ne$ d feddu, alamma isers îôad tiâekkwmin is. Akka, lemmer i S ihwi i Öebbi, yili I$leb iten, maca a kwen Ijeôôeb, kra s kra. Wid ipwan$an deg ubrid n Öebbi, ur pôuêun igiten nnsen, d awez$i. A ten Inhu, ad Iûeggem lêala nnsen. A ten Issekcem di Loennet i sen Imla. A wid iumnen! Ma tefkam afus i Öebbi, ad awen Ifk afus, ad awen itebbet isurifen. Wid ijehlen, ay amxix nnsen, ad weddôen igiten nnsen. Ayagi, acku ugwin ayen id Issers Öebbi; ihi, Imêa igiten nnsen. Aâni ur nudan ara tamurt, ad walin amek tevôa d imezwura nnsen? Issexv iten Öebbi. Am akka i ijehliyen. Ayagi, acku Öebbi d bab n wid iumnen. Ijehliyen, ur asen illi bab. Ih, Öebbi ad Issekcem wid iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan, di leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen. Wid ijehlen zehhun, teppen akken itepp lmal. D times ay d leqôaô nnsen. Acêal n at temdinin i yifen, di tezmert, tamdint i k id iéâan! Nesqucc iten, ur asen illi useîîaô. Day win illan ar ubeggen n Mass is, am win, iwumi ppucebbêen yir igiten is, u iîîafaôen chawi nnsen? Amek tga Loennet i ippuwaââden i wid ipêezziben: degs isaffen n waman ur nxeppeô, isaffen n yi$i ur tfessed lbenna s, isaffen n ccôab aéidan i wid itessen, isaffen n tament ippuneqqan. Degs, i nitni, yal ppemôa, akked ssmaê n Mass nnsen. Day am wid iwekkôen di tmes; sswan ten s waman ippayzagen, ara icergen afwad nnsen? Llan garasen wid i k issemêasen. Sifat ff$en d s$uôek, ad inin i wid iwumi teppunefk tmusni: "d acu id inna kan, llinna"? Wigi d wid iwumi Isle$ Öebbi ulawen, teddun kan d chawi nnsen. Wid ipwanhan, Irna asen nnhaya, Ifka yasen aêezzeb nnsen. Day la pôaoun kan imir, a ten id ias, deqzalla? Ni$ usant ed licaôat is. Ma iusa d $uôsen, iwumi t usmekti nnsen? Cfu ar, s tidep, ur illi ôebbi siwa Öebbi; ssuter ssmaê ubekkav ik, akked wid n lmumnin, argaz tameîîut. Öebbi Iéôa anda têebkem, akked wanda tberrkem. La qqaôen wid iumnen: "a lemmer a d ters tsuôep"! Maca, mi d ters tsuôep tuêkimt, ideg id ipwader umennu$, a pwaliv at wul iblan, la k id pmuqulen s tiî n win tessexcawat tmeppant. Yif it i nitni wannuz, akked wawal uwqim. Mi ipwagzem ôôay, ma ssawlen tidep ar Öebbi yif it i nitni. Day maççi, ma twexxôem, ahat a ppesfesdem tamurt, a pfaôqem alag nnwen? Wigi d wid i Ixza Öebbi; Isgugem iten, Isder$el iéôi nnsen. Day ur pmeyyizen ara Leqwôan, ne$ u$alent tsergal $ef wulawen? Ih, wid ixedâan, deffir ubeggen n nnhaya $uôsen, ikellex iten Cciîan. Iooa ten tallit. Ayagi, acku nitni nnan i wid iugin ayen d Issader Öebbi: "ad awen na$ awal di kra n lumuô". Öebbi Iéôa lesrar nnsen. Amek ihi, ma ddment lmalayek leôwaê nnsen, la ten kkatent ar udmawen nnsen, iârar nnsen? Akka, ihi, ddan akked wayen isserfayen Öebbi. Ugin llza S. D$a Isseôxes igiten nnsen. Ne$ $ilen at wul amehzul, ard awez$i, ur d Issuffu$ ara Öebbi leb$wev nnsen? Lemmer i £ ihwi, ad ak ten id Nessken, war ccekk, a ten tâaqlev ar udem nnsen, a ten tâaqlev ar ûûenf umeslay. Öebbi Issen igiten nnwen. S tidep, a kwen Njeôôeb, alamma Nessen imjuhad, akked iûebôiyen, segwen. A Njeôôeb isallen nnwen. Ih, wid ijehlen, issefôa$en abrid n Öebbi, i inuqmen Amazan, deffir ubeggen n nnhaya $uôsen, ur vuôôen Öebbi s wacemma. Ad Isseôxes igiten nnsen. A wid iumnen! A$et awal i Öebbi, a$et awal i Umazan, ur ssiôxiset igiten nnwen! Ih, wid ijehlen, issefôa$en abrid n Öebbi, sinna, mmuten d ijehliyen, war ccekk, ur sen Ipsemmiê Öebbi, d awez$i. Ur ppiôhifet, ur ssuturet tifrat, mara tilim d ine$laben! U Öebbi yidwen, ur kwen Ipêewwio, d awez$i, seg igiten nnwen. Tameddurt di ddunit, d urar kan, akked lhawiyya. Ma tumnem u têezbem, ad awen d Ifk arrazen nnwen. Ur awen issutur ayla nnwen. Ma Issuter awen t, a kwen Icebbwel, a pcuêêem, a d iffe$ leb$wev nnwen. D kunwi i ipwanecden a pseddqem deg ubrid n Öebbi. Llan degwen wid ipcuêêun. Win ipcuêêun, ipcuêêu kan $ef yiman is. Öebbi d Asâay, kunwi d igellilen. Ma twexxôem, a kwen Ineûûef s ugdud ur nelli segwen. D$a ur ppemcabin $uôwen.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡفَتۡحِ Ih, Nefya yak l$elb iberrzen, iwakken ad Isemmeê Öebbi ibekkaven ik id izwaren akked wid igwran. Ad ak Itim l$it iS, a k Iawi d ubrid uwqim. A k Iall Öebbi tallalt tuzmirt. D Neppa id Issersen talwit deg ulawen n lmumnin, iwakken ad yim$uô liman nnsen. N Öebbi Iâsekôiwen n tmurt akked igenwan. Öebbi Izga Iééeô, d Bab n ûûwab. Iwakken ad Issekcem wid akked tid iumnen, ar leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen, degsen ad wekkôen. Ad asen Issemsu tucmitin nnsen. D wagi, ar Öebbi, ay d rrbeê abarar. Ad Iâaqeb ixabiten, tixabitin, imcurak, timcurak, wid id ipfekkiôen Öebbi yir afekkeô. Izzi yasen ddens. Irfa Öebbi fellasen, Ixza ten. Ihegga yasen d Loahennama. A tu$alin tucmip! N Öebbi iâsekôiwen n tmurt akked igenwan. Öebbi Izga d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab. Ih, Nuzen ik id d anagi, d abcir, d aneddaô, iwakken a ppamnem s Öebbi akked Umazan iS, a T kfum, ad aS tanzem, a T tesbuccuâem taûebêit, tameddit. Wid iâaqden yidek âaqden kan d Öebbi. Afus n Öebbi nnig ufus nnsen. Win iêenten, d imanis kan i isseênet. Win iîîfen deg wayen i$ef iâuhed Öebbi, ad as Ifk arraz abarar. Ad ak inin wid igwran, seg uâôaben n ucluê: "i $ ice$wlen, d ayla nne$ akked twaculin nne$. Ssuter a neppusemmeê". Qqaôen s yilsawen nnsen, ayen ur nelli deg ulawen nnsen. Ini: "anwa ara kwen iselken si Öebbi, s wacemma, ma Ib$a yawen vveôô, ne$ ma Ib$a yawen aba$uô? Xaîi, Izga Öebbi Ippuxebbeô af wayen txeddmem. Xaîi, t$ilem Amazan akked lmumnin ur d ppu$alen ara, d awez$i, ar twaculin nnsen. Ayagi, issefôeê ulawen nnwen. Nnwaya nnwen dir ip. Kunwi d agdud imsenger. Wid ur numin s Öebbi, akked Umazan iS, ihi, aql a£ Nhegga d ajajiê i ijehliyen. N Öebbi, tagelda n tmurt akked igenwan. Ipsemmiê i win i S ihwan, Ipâuqub win i S ihwan. Öebbi Izga Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu. A d inin wid igwran: "ma tôuêem a d t$eltem, ooet a$ a neddu yidwen". B$an ad bedlen awalen n Öebbi. Ini: "ur teppeddum yidne$, d awez$i. Akka ay d izwar wawal n Öebbi". A d inin: "teêsedm a$"! Xaîi, cwiî kan ay fehhmen. Ini i wid igwran, seg uâôaben n ucluê: "a ppepwanecdem s agdud amaâwaôu, uqsiê; a t tenna$em, ne$ ad anzen. Ma tu$em awal, ad awen Ifk Öebbi arraz igerzen. Ma twexxôem, akken twexxôem uqbel, a kwen Iâaqeb s lqeôê". Ur telli tiyta deg uder$al, ne$ deg urejdal, ne$ deg umuvin. Win iunzen i Öebbi akked Umazan iS, a t Issekcem di leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen. Win iwexxôen, a t Iâaqeb s lqeôê. Ni$ Iôuva Öebbi lmumnin, mi âaqden yidek, seddaw ttejôa. Iéôa i illan deg ulawen nnsen, Issers d fellasen talwit, I$na ten s l$elb aqôib, akked waîas n lerbaê, ara îîfen. Öebbi Izga d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab. Iwaââed awen Öebbi a d teîîfem lerbaê aîas. I$awel awen d deg waya. Ikkes fellawen afus n medden. Akken ad yili ussekni i lmumnin, a kwen iawi d ubrid uwqim. Tayev, iwumi ur tezmirem, ihi, Izzi as Öebbi. Öebbi Izga Izmer i yal cci. Lemmer i kwen nnu$en wid ijehlen, ad rewlen, sinna, ur ppafen bab, ne$ asettaô. D tannumi n Öebbi i illan si zik. Ur teppafev abeddel, d awez$i, di tannumi n Öebbi. D Neppa i Ikksen afus nnsen segwen, akked ufus nnwen segsen, di te$zut n Mekka, siwev Iss$elb ikwen fellasen. Öebbi Izga Ipwali ayen txeddmem. D nitni i ijehlen. Swexxôen kwen si Loamaâ n Lêaôam, ugin ad iawev usfel s amkan is. Lemmer maççi d lmumnin, argaz tameîîut, ur ten tessinem, a ten têazem ur teéôim; segsen a d tegwrim di le$ôuô - ni$ Öebbi Issekcam s aêunu S, win i S ihwan - lemmer mfaôaqen, yili, war ccekk, Nesâadda, $ef wid segsen ijehlen, aâaqeb aqeôêan. Mi rran wid ijehlen, aêernun deg ulawen nnsen, aêernun n war tussna, Issers ed Öebbi talwit iS af Umazan iS, akked lmumnin. Iqqen asen awal uêezzeb. Iwata ten, klalen t. Öebbi Izga Iéôa yal cci. Ni$ Issawev Öebbi, i Umazan iS, tamu$li s tidep: war ccekk, a pkecmem Loamaâ n Lêaôam, ma Irad Öebbi, di laman, iqweôôa nnwen ûûeîlen u qeôcen, ur teppagwadem. Iéôa ayen ur teéôim. Ihegga yawen d, ugwar aya, l$elb aqôib. Neppa id Iuznen Amazan iS s nnhaya, akked ddin n tidep, iwakken a t Issifrer $ef ddin meôôa. Iqadd Öebbi d Anagi. Muêemmed d Amazan n Öebbi. Wid illan yides, qesêen ar ijehliyen, êninit garasen. A ten twaliv îîinizen, kennun, ssuturen lfevl s$uô Öebbi akked llza. Ccama nnsen, deg udmawen nnsen, d lateô n lekni. Ata wayen i ten icban di Tuôa akked wayen i ten icban di Linoil: am uâaqqa, iger ed im$i s, isoehd it. Ad iuzur, ad iâaooeô $ef yile$ is. Ippaâoab ifellaêen; i$webben yissen ijehliyen. Iwaââed Öebbi ssmaê akked warraz abarar, i wid degsen iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡحُجُراتِ A wid iumnen! Ur zeggwiret zdat Öebbi akked Umazan iS. Ëezzbet i Öebbi. Öebbi, s tidep, Issel, d Amusnaw. A wid iumnen! Ur zzuhriyet tu$ac nnwen, sennig ta$wect n Nnbi. Ur zaââvet $uôes, akken tepzaââvam garawen, mulac ad mêun igiten nnwen, kunwi ur tfaqem. Ih, wid issrusun ûut n ta$wect nnsen, ar Umazan n Öebbi, d wid iwumi Issefsi Öebbi ulawen nnsen, ar uêezzeb. Ad asen ippunefk ssmaê akked warraz abarar. Ih, tegwti n wid ik n issawlen, deffir texxamin, ur pmeyyizen. Lemmer ûbiôen ard teff$ev $uôsen, ppif i nitni. Öebbi Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu. A wid iumnen! Aballa$ ma ibbwi yawen d asali, ppuêeqqeqet, mulac a pvuôôem agdud, war tamusni, a ppu$alem tnedmem deg wayen txedmem. Cfut illa garawen Umazan n Öebbi. Ma issemêes awen deg waîas n lumuô, a pjafem. Maca, Öebbi Issaâzez awen liman, Imelleê it deg ulawen nnwen, Isseôéeg awen tijehli, dd$el, lmaâûegga. Widak d wid ipwanhan. D lfevl s$uô Öebbi, d l$it. Öebbi Iéôa, d Bab n ûûwab. Ma nnu$ent snat n îayfat n lmumnin, êuddet pent. Ma tebw$ev yiwet degsent, $ef tayev, nna$et tin ibwe$ven alamma tevfeô lameô n Öebbi. Ma tevfeô it, ssemûalêet pent, s lmizan. Wezznet. Öebbi Iêemmel wid iwezznen. Lmumnin d atmaten kan i illan. Ssemûalêet atmaten nnwen, êezzbet i Öebbi, amar fellawen aêunu. A wid iumnen! £uôwat ad imaâlek ugdud $ef wayev, ahat d widen i ten yifen. Ne$ tilawin $ef tiyav, ahat d tiden i tent yifen. Ur pqeôôidet iman nnwen, ur pmirgamet s tselleqwbin. Dir it isem n dd$el, anda illa liman. Wid ur nutub ara, d widak ay d imednas. A wid iumnen! Janbet aîas n nnwaya. Ih, nnwaya, tikwal, d abekkav. Ur ppemâassat ara. Ur kkatet wa deg wa. Day ib$u yiwen, degwen, ad içç aksum n gmas lmegget? A t tagwim. Ëezzbet i Öebbi. Ih, Öebbi Issuruf, Ipêunu. A yimdanen! Ni$ Nxelq ikwen si ddker akked nnta. Nerra kwen d igduden, d laâôac, a ppemyussanem. Ihi, ukyis nnwen amxallef, ar Öebbi, d win degwen ipêezziben sennig wiyav. Ih, Öebbi Iéôa, Ippuxebbeô. Nnan uâôaben n ucluê: "numen". Ini: "ur tuminem". Maca init ed: "nunez"; ur ikcim ara liman ar wulawen nnwen. Ma tôuvam Öebbi akked Umazan iS, ur awen Isôuêu acemma seg igiten nnwen. Öebbi, s tidep, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu. Lmumnin d wid kan iumnen s Öebbi akked Umazan iS, d$a, ur pcukun. Pna$en s wayla nnsen akked yiman nnsen, deg ubrid n Öebbi. D widak ay d imawlan n tidep. Ini: "day ad aS temlem i Öebbi, ddin nnwen"? Öebbi Iéôa i illan deg igenwan, i illan di tmurt. Öebbi Issen yal cci. Rran ak annuz nnsen, d tajmilt. Ini: "ur iyi telli tejmilt deg annuz nnwen. Xaîi, d Öebbi ikwen I$aten mi kwen Inha ar liman, ma d imawlan n tidep ay tellam". Ih, Öebbi Issen tabavnit n tmurt akked igenwan. Öebbi Ipwali ayen txeddmem.
سُوۡرَةُ قٓ Q. S Leqwôan, mucaâ! Xaîi! Wehmen mi ten id iusa uneddaô, segsen. Nnan ijehliyen: "ayagi d lwehma! Ma nemmut, nu$al d akal, ayagi d tu$alin si mbâid"! Ni$ Neéôa acêal, segsen, i issenqes wakal. £uône£ Tazmamt iêerrzen. Xaîi! Nekôen tidep, mi ten id tusa, d$a terwi lêala nnsen. Day ur muqlen ara igenni, sennig sen, amek i t Nebna? Ncebbeê it, ur isâi i$isan. Tamurt, Nvelq ip, Nerra degs idurar, Nessem$i d degs tayuga n yal ûûenf amxallef, i tmu$li akked usmekti n yal amdan isteôoiâen. Nesse$li d seg igenni aman iôqan. Nessem$i d yissen leonanat akked uâqqa n tmegra, akked tezdayin ti$wezfanin, s ijeooigen mbabben, d ôôeéq i imdanen. Nessider d yissen tamurt immuten. Akka tanekra. Inkeô, uqbel nnsen, ugdud n Nuê, At Rrass, Tamud, Âad, Ferâun, atmaten n Luî, At Laika, akked ugdud n Tubbaâ. Nekôen akw imazanen. Iûaô ussigwed iW. Day £ issefcel uxlaq amezwaru? Wanag nitni di ccekk $ef uxlaq amaynut. Ni$ Nxelq ed amdan. Neéôa s wacu i t t$ewwu, teôwiêt is. Neqôeb $uôes, sennig iéuôan n temgaôt is. Mara îîfen wid ippaîîafen; qqimen, wa $eô yeffus, wa $eô zelmev, ur d iqqaô awal, siwa ma illa $uôes, uâssas imêelles. Iusa d ddux n tmeppant, ibbwi d tidep: "atan wayen iseg la treggwlev". Aûuvu di lbuq. D wagi ay d ass n ussigwed. Yal iman a d ias s unehhaô, akked unagi. Ni$ telliv testehzav $ef waya. Nekkes ak taduli k. Iéôi k, assa, d uzzal. Ad yini umsaâef is: "ata $uôi wayen id ippuheggan". Veggôet, ar Loahennama, yal ajehli amâaûi, i iugwin lxiô, amjuô, imcebbwel, i irran ar tama n Öebbi, ôebbi nniven. Ihi, veggôet ep s aâaqeb uqsiê! A d yini umsaâef is: "a Mass nne$! Ur t rri$ d amjuô, d neppa i illan di ttelfan u$miq". Inna: "ur ppemnamaret ara $uôI, imi wen d Zzewre$ aâggen. Ur ipbeddil $uôI wawal. Nek, ur Ïîuôôu$ imdanen". Ass ideg ara Nini i Loahennama: "ma teççuôev"? A d tini: "ma tella tmerna"? Tqeôb ed Loennet, ar wid ipêezziben, ur tebâad. "D tagi i wen ippuwaââden; i yal atubi iêerzen, ippagwaden Aênin di tbavnit, iteddun s wul ucâif. Ekcemt ep, di tifrat, d wagi ay d ass uwekkeô"! Nnsen, dinna, ayen i sen ihwan; s$uône£, timerna. Acêal isuta ay Nesqucc uqbel nnsen! Llan $elben ten di loehd. Qelben, di tmurt, anda t ssôan? Deg waya, s tidep, asmekti i win isâan ul, ne$ ifkan tameééu$t, u d anagi. Ni$ Nxelq ed tamurt, igenwan, akked wayen illan garasen, di sdis wussan, ur Naâyi. Eûbeô i wayen d qqaôen, sbuccaâ s ccekôan Mass ik, uqbel ad inqeô yiîij, uqbel ad i$li. Deg iv sbuccaâ iT, akked deffir lekni. Ssemêes, ass ideg ara d iberreê uberraê, si tama iqeôben. Ass ideg ara slen i usu$u, s tidep, ass nni, d ass n tuff$a. Ih, Nekwni Nessidir u Nneqq. £uône£ tu$alin. Ass ideg ara tceqqeq tmurt $uôsen s tazla. Afesser agi d ayen isehlen fellane£. Nekwni Nif akw akken Neéôa acu id qqaôen. Ur telliv fellasen d aqehhaô. Mmekti d, s Leqwôan, wid ippagwaden aâggen iW.
سُوۡرَةُ الذَّارِياتِ S wavu iwezzâen! I ibubben taâkkwemt! Wid ippazalen s shala! Tid ifeôqen lameô! Ar ayen i wen ippuâahden, d tidep. Aqeîîi, ih, ad iûaô. S igenni bu idurra! Kunwi temgarradem $ef wawal. Iooa t win iooan. Tameppant i ikeddaben! Nitni, di maylellif, stehzan, steqsayen: "anda t wass uqeîîi"? Ass ideg, ara ppuhewlen di tmes: "Jeôôbet ahewwel nnwen agi i$ef têarem"! Ih, wid ipêezziben, di leonanat akked tliwa; Ïîfen ayen i sen Ifka Mass nnsen. Ih, nitni llan, iu$ lêal, d lâuûam. Deg iv, cwiî ay gganen. Di tafrara, nitni ste$fiôen; deg wayla nnsen: amur i umappar akked ume$bun. U di tmurt, issekniyen i wid ipputebbten. Llant deg iman nnwen. Aâni ur tepwalim ara? U deg igenni, ôôeéq nnwen, akked wayen i wen ippuwaââden. S Mass n tmurt akked igenwan, ar neppa d tidep, am akken kunwi tepmeslayem! Ma tebbwev ik id tedyant inebgawen ukyisen n Ibôahim? Kecmen $uôes, nnan as: "tifrat"! Inna: "tifrat a wid ur nessin!" Inser ar twacult is, ibbwi d aâjmi iqebbwan. Iqeôb asen t id; inna: "day ur teppeppem ara"? Iêus iugad iten. Nnan as: "ur ppagwad"! D$a beccôen t s uqcic amusnaw Tqeôb ed tmeîîut is, tsu$, tewwet deg udem is, tenna d: "tam$aôt tiâiqeôt?" Nnan: "akka id Inna Mass im. Ih, Neppa, d Bab n ûûwab, d Amusnaw". Inna: "anwa ay d awal nnwen, a yimceggâan"? Nnan: "nekwni neppuceggaâ d ar ugdud ibe$wviyen. Iwakken a ten neôoem s uéôu n talaxt i ipwaôecmen s$uô Mass ik i ucmiten". Nessuffe$ kra illan, degs, n lmumnin. Nufa kan degs, yiwen uxxam n imvuâen. Neooa p id d assekni i wid iugaden aâaqeb aqeôêan. I di Musa, mi t id Nuzen i Ferâun, s udabu n ûûeê. Iaâûa, akked imalalen is, inna: "d aseêêar, ne$ d aôehbani". Neddem it, neppa akked iâsekriwen is, Nveggeô iten ar yill. Tiyta degs. I di Âad, mi sen Nuzen avu asexvi. Ur ippaooa ayen immuger, alamma irra t am rrmim. I Tamud, mi pwanecden: "siwa tallit ara tezhum". Âuûan lameô n Mass nnsen. Tewwet iten id ssiâqa, nitni la pwalin. Ur zmiren a d kren, ur pwasellken. Agdud n Nuê, uqbel, llan, s tidep, d agdud iballa$en. Igenni, Nebna t s loehd, d Nekwni it Issewsaân. Tamurt, Nessa p. Ay gerzen Wid Itessun! Di yal cci, Nexleq tayuga, ahat a d tesmektim. Ihi, srifget ar Öebbi. Nek, ih, s$uôeS ar $uôwen, d aneddaô ipbegginen. Ur sâut, ar tama n Öebbi, ôebbi nniven! Nek, ih, s$uôeS ar $uôwen, d aneddaô ipbegginen. Akka, ur iusi umazan ar wid i ten id izwaren, mebla ma nnan as: "d aseêêar ne$ d aôehbani". Day ppuweûûan $ef waya? Xaîi, nitni d agdud izegren tilas. Ïîixxeô asen; ur deg k tiyta. Smektay ed. Asmekti, s tidep, infaâ lmumnin. Xelqe$ leonun akked imdanen, iwakken kan ad iyI âabden. Ur b$i$ segsen ôôeéq, ur b$i$ ad iyi cceççen. Öebbi, s tidep, d Aôeééaq, d Bu tezmert n ûûeê. Ih, i wid idensen, amur am umur imeddukwal nnsen. Ulay$eô iyI $eûben. A tawa$it n wid ijehlen, ilmend n wass i sen ippuwaââden!
سُوۡرَةُ الطُّوۡرِ S udrar! S Tezmamt ippujerrden di lka$ev ivelqen! S texxamt iâamôen! S tseddarit aâlayen! S yill icebbwlen! Aâaqeb n Mass ik, s tidep, ad ivôu. Ur isâi ara t sfunngen. Ass ideg ara imbwiwel igenni, d ambwiwel, Ad lêun idurar, d tikli. A ssexv, assen, n wid iskiddiben! Wid inexôen deg uraren. Ass ideg ara pwaveggôen ar tmes n Loahennama, d aveggeô. Apan tmes nni i la tnekôem! D ssêur waya, ne$ d kunwi ur nwala ara? Kecmet ep. Iâuva fellawen, tûebôem, ne$ ur teûbiôem. A ppeppuqeîîim kan $ef wayen txeddmem. Wanag wid ipêezziben, di leonanat, akked zzhu. Feôêen s wayen i sen Ifka Mass nnsen. Isellek iten, Mass nnsen, seg uâaqeb ujajiê. àçet, teswem, di lehna, ilmend n wayen txeddmem! èélen af imîeôêen, d idurra; d tiêuôiyin lâin ukud iten Njewweo. Wid iumnen, u âanden ten, warraw nnsen, ar liman nnsen, a ten Nessemlil akked warraw nnsen. Ur Nessenqas acemma seg igiten nnsen. Yal amdan ad immager ayen ikseb. Ad asen d Nefk izwayen akked uksum seg wayen cedhan. Dinna ad ppemyeppaken lkas, ideg ur illi usîeômel, ne$ ssebba n tuccva. Garasen, ddewiôen ilmeéiyen i nitni, amzun d tiyaqutin mesîuôen. Zzin, kra $er kra, pmesteqsayen. Nnan d: "ni$ nella, zik, di twacult nne$, nugad. I$at a$ Öebbi, Isellek a$ seg ujajiê n tmes. Ni$ nella, zik, nepnuju $uôeS. Neppa, s tidep, d A$eyyat Ipêunun". Ihi, ccfu ar keçç, s l$it n Mass ik, ur telliv d agezzan, ne$ d aôehbani. Ne$, ad inin: "d amedyaz. A naôou asali s akud". Ini: "gganit! Nek, yidwen, seg wid ipganin". Ne$ d tirga nnsen i sen iumôen aya, ne$ nitni d agdud izegren tilas. Ne$ ad inin: "isnulfa t id". Xaîi! Ur uminen. Ihi, a d awin ameslay i t icban, ma d tidep ay ssawalen! Ne$ pwaxelqen seg ulac, ne$ d nitni ay d ixellaqen? Ne$ xelqen tamurt akked igenwan? Xaîi, ur pputebbten! Ne$ $uôsen lexzayen n Mass ik, ne$ nitni d imvebbôen? Ne$ sâan sellum ad ssemêessen, segs. Ihi, win islan segsen, a d iawi adabu n ûûeê! Ne$ i Neppa tullas, i kunwi arrac? Ne$ tessutrev asen taqdiât, fellasen d îîlaba ééayen? Ne$ $uôsen tabavnit, d$a la pparun? Ne$ b$an ad andin? D wid ijehlen ara ipwaîîfen. Ne$ sâan ôebbi, ur Nelli d Öebbi? Gedha s Öebbi, seg wayen pcaraken! Lemmer ad walin amur igenni i$li, ad as inin: "d asigna i izdin". Ihi, eoo iten, ard mlilen d wass n ssiâqa nnsen, Ass, ideg ur asen d teppawi acemma, tandit nnsen; ur asen illi usettaô. I wid idensen, s tidep, aâaqeb nniven, maca tegwti degsen, ur éôin. Eûbeô i wayen d Iêudd Mass ik, aql ak, s tidep, ger wallen nne£. Sbuccaâ s ccekôan Mass ik, mara d tekkrev. Sbuccaâ iT deg iv, u mara xsin yitran.
سُوۡرَةُ النَّجۡمِ S yitri mara ixeppi! Ur innetlaf, ur i$liv umeddakwel nnwen. Ur d iqqaô akken i s ihwan. D aweêêi kan, id ippuweêêan. Islemd it bab n tezmert iqwan. D bab n tezmert irs ed u neppa di lejba aâlayen. Sinna iqeôb ed, ippucengel, atan tasurift n sin ixtucen, ne$ ur tebbwiv. D$a iweêêa i umdan iS, ayen iweêêa. Ur iskaddeb wul deg wayen iwala. Day a t tnaqwmem, $ef wayen iwala? Ni$ iéôa t di trusi s nniven, ar tedxwent n talast, u$uô illa leonan usemlili. Mi tesbur tedxwent ta$wlaft, ur iwweônenni yiéôi, ur izgir. Ni$ iwala kra issekniyen imeqwôaêanen, n Mass is. Twalam Allat akked Lâuzza? Akked Manat, tis krav nniven? Day i kunwi ddkeô, i Neppa nnta? Wagi, ihi, d beîîu aneêyaf. Wigi d ismawen kan i sent tefkam, kunwi akked imezwura nnwen. Ur sent d Issers Öebbi kra udabu. Ïîafaôen kan nnwaya, akked wayen cehwant teôwiêin. Ni$ tusa ten id nnhaya s$uô Mass nnsen. Aâni, i umdan, ayen issaram? Tamezwarut akked tneggarut, n Öebbi. Acêal n lmalayek deg igenwan, ur d teppawi acemma ccafuâa nnsent, siwa deffir tsriê n Öebbi, $ef win Ib$a u Iôuva. Ih, wid ur numin ara di laxeôt, ppaken i lmalayek ismawen n nnta. Ur sâin fellas kra n tmusni. Ïîafaôen kan nnwaya. Wanag nnwaya ur tebbwi acemma si tidep. Ihi, eoo win iwexxôen i usmekti nne£, i ib$an kan tudert n ddunit. D aya ay sen tefka tmusni. Mass ik, war ccekk, Iéôa sennig akw, anwa innetlafen seg ubrid iS; Iéôa sennig akw, anwa i ipwanhan. N Öebbi ayen akw illan deg igenwan, illan di tmurt. Ad Iqeîîi wid ifalîan $ef wayen xedmen, ad Ioazi wid issweqmen, s ûûam. Wid ijunben ibekkaven ibararen akked tucmitin, siwa lfalîat fessusen, ihi, d uwsiâ ssmaê n Mass ik. Neppa Issen ikwen sennig akw, mi kwen id Ixleq seg wakal, mi tellam d icelleqluqen, deg iâabbav n tyimmatin nnwen. Ur staâmilet tezdeg deg iman nnwen! Neppa Iéôa sennig akw, anwa iêezzben. Twalav win iwexxôen, i ifkan cwiî, iccuêen? Day isâa tamusni n tbavnit, d$a iwala? Ne$ ur ippuxebbeô $ef tewôiqin n Musa? Akked Ibôahim ineûêen? Ur ipbibbi yiwen taâkkwemt n wayev. I umdan, siwa ayen inki. Ankay is a t iwali. Sinna, a t Ikafi s lufa. Ih, ar Mass ik, taggara. D Neppa i Issevûan, i Issruyen. D Neppa i Ineqqen, i Issidiren. D Neppa i Ixelqen tayuga, ddkeô akked nnta, Si tiqqit n l$ella ma tuzzel. FellaS, axlaq nniven. D Neppa i I$ennun, i Iqenâan. D Neppa i d Mass n Ciâra. D Neppa i Isnegren Âad imezwura. Si Tamud, ur d Iooi ara. Agdud n Nuê, uqbel nnsen, war ccekk, iugar iten ddens, lbbwe$v. Issenger tid inneqlaben; Idel iten s wayen idellen. Anta talalt n Mass ik ara tnamerev? Wagi d aneddaô seg ineddaôen n zik. A d taéé tin d ippaééen. War Öebbi, ur illi ara p id issdehôen. Iswehm ikwen wawal a? La tdessem ur la tepprum! Kunwi di zzhu. Knut i Öebbi, âabdet.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡقَمَرِ Iqeôb ed yimir; ifelleq waggur. Ma walan assekni, ad wexxôen, ad inin: "ipkemmil ssêur"! Nekôen, îîafaôen lemcihwat nnsen. Ad iûaô yal lameô. Ni$ usan ten id kra isallen, u wayen degsen iswexxiôen. Üûwab issakwayen. Maca ula iwumi aâaggen. Ihi, îîixxeô asen! Asmi ara d isiwel, uberraê, ar wayen iwaâôen, s wallen ibran, ara d ff$en si tneîlin, am ujôad iwezzâen. Ad éedmen, âaooôen, ar uberraê, ad inin ijehliyen: "wagi d ass uwâiô". Agdud n Nuê, uqbel nnsen, iskaddeb. Skaddben amdan nne$. Nnan: "d aôehbani". Rran t id. Inuj ar Mass is: "nek pwa$elbe$, Awes"! Nelli tibbura igenni, i waman d ihedman, Nesgguffaâ d laânaûeô n tmurt, mlalen waman akken ipwagzem lameô; Nebbwi t af tencirin, akked tavuî n tiffest. Teppeddu zdat wallen nne£, d arraz i win ipwanekôen. Ni$ Neooa p id d assekni. Day llan wid id ismektayen? Amek illa uqeîîi W u llant licaôat iW! Ni$ Nsehhel Leqwôan i usmekti. Day llan wid id ismektayen? Âad skaddben. Amek illa uqeîîi W u llant licaôat iW! Ih, Nuzen asen aûeôûaô, ass amekêus, imezgi. Ippawi medden amzun d iqeôôumen n tezdayin ipwaqelâen. Amek illa uqeîîi W u llant licaôat iW! Nsehhel Leqwôan i usmekti. Day llan wid id ismektayen? Tamud skaddben aâeggen. Nnan: "day a neddu d yiwen n umdan segne$? Ihi, nekwni, war ccekk, di ttelfan, akked tisselbi. Day d neppa, garane$, u$uô id iusa uneddeô? Wanag neppa, d akeddab uqbiê". Ad walin azekka, anwa ay d akeddab uqbiê! A Nazen, ih, tal$wemt i ujeôôeb nnsen. Qaôaâ ten, ili k d aûebôi. Xebbeô iten ar aman ad pwafeôqen. Mkul tissit s tidwelt. Ssawlen i umeddakwel nnsen. Iusa d, igezm as ivaôen. Ihi, Nuzen asen ajebwani, kkes ed tawacult n Luî, i Nsellek qbel tafara, d l$it s$uône£. Akka ay Nepkafi wid isnemmiren. Ni$ iâaggen asen, Newâaô. Rran aâeggen di ccekk. Ni$ ssutren t $ef inebgawen is. Nesder$el allen nnsen: "jeôôbet aâaqeb iW, akked uâaggen iW". Iusa ten id, ssbeê zik, uâaqeb imezgi. Jeôôbet aâaqeb iW, akked uâeggen iW! Nsehhel Leqwôan i usmekti. Ne$ tesâam laânaya deg Ihellilen? Ne$ a d inin: "nekwni d agraw ara irebêen"? Agraw ad ixseô, ad wexxôen. Ih, imir d ppaâud nnsen. Imir d lhejna, u ôéag kteô. سُوۡرَةُ الرَّحۡمٰنِ Aênin. Isseêfev Leqwôan. Ixleq amdan. Isselmed as ôôkuz. Iîij akked waggur, s leêsab. Itran akked ttjuô, knan. Igenni, Issuli t; Issers ed lmizan. Ur xedâat di lmizan. Weznet s tidep, ur ssexsaôet lmizan. Issewsaâ tamurt i imexlaq. Degs izwayen, tizdayin sut tkummiwin; iâqqayen s usa$uô, iferrawen utebtil. Anwa seg i$iten n Mass nnwen ara teskiddben, i sin? سُوۡرَةُ الۡوَاقِعَةِ Mara d tas, tin ara d iasen, $ef tisin is, ur illi ucehrir. Tessrusu, treffed. Ma tenhez tmurt, lhezz iqesêen, idurar ftutsen, u$alen d a$ebbaô ippuwezzâen, a d tevêum krav leûnaf: at uyeffus. At uyeffus, anwi ten? At uzelmav. At uzelmav, anwi ten? Akked imezwura, imezwura, Widak d iqôiben; di leonanat isaâdiyen. Seg imenza, deg waîas idsen. Seg ineggura, drus nnsen. £ef imîeôêen iévan, éélen fellasen, mqabalen. Tezzin asen ilmeéiyen iwekkôen, s tbuqalin, iqbucen, akked lkas n tissit iûfan. Yis, ur ppavnen, ur sekkôen. Izwayen, seg wid smenyafen. Aksum n yifôax, seg win cedhan. Tiêuôiyin lâin, am tyaqutin iffren. D arraz n wayen xeddmen. Ur din sellen awal n leqbaêa, ne$ n tuccva; siwa awal n tifrat, tifrat! At uyeffus, at uyeffus, d acu ten? Ar tzegwart, war isennanen. Tulmatin iurwen. Tili iwsâen. Aman ippazalen. Aîas n yizwayen, ur zegzawit, ur ppugedlen. Imîeôêen aâlayen. D Nekwni itent Ixelqen, Nerra tent d tiêuôiyin; pêemmilent, d tizyiwin, i at uyeffus. Seg imenza, deg aîas idsen. Seg ineggura, deg aîas idsen. At uzelmav, at uzelmav, d acu ten? Deg wavu, akked waman iô$an. Tili n wabbu iô$an. Ur degs tasmuvi, lekyasa. Ih, nitni zik, llan ôwan. Zgan deg ubekkav abarar. Llan qqaôen: "ma nemmut, nu$al d akal, akked i$san, day a d a$ d rren? Akked imezwura nne$ imenza"? Ini: "ih, imezwura akked ineggura, ad ppujemmlen ar temlilit n wass ipwassnen". D$a, ih, a yim$eôôqen, i illan d inekkaôen, a ppeççem, war ccekk, si ttejôa n Zaqqum. A ppacaôem segs ifwaden. Sinna, a ppernum tissit seg waman iô$an. A ppetessem tissit ile$wman. D wagi ar asen d irsen, ass uqeîîi. D Nekwni ikwen Ixelqen. Lemmer a ppamnem. Twalam l$ella id iteff$en segwen? D kunwi ip ixelqen, ne$ d Nekwni ay d ixellaqen? Nseyya tameppant garawen. Ur a£ izeggwir yiwen iwakken a Nerr deg umkan nnwen wid i kwen icban; u kunwi, a kwen Nexleq d ayen ur tessinem. Ni$ tesnem axlaq amenzu, lemmer tesmektayem! Twalam ayen tkerrzem? D kunwi i t ikerzen, ne$ d Nekwni ay d imekrazen? Ma ihwa ya£, a t Nerr d uêvim, d$a a kwen tekkat lwehma: "Aql a$ nepwalas! Sennig waya: aql a$ neppuêeôôem"! Twalam aman i teppessem? D kunwi iten id isse$layen seg usigna, ne$ d Nekwni? Ma ihwa ya£, a ten Nerr d imeô$anen. A lemmer tesnemmiren! Twalam times i tesskarem s uêukku? D kunwi i s d ixelqen ttjuô is, ne$ d Nekwni ay d Ixellaqen? D Nekwni i p Irran d asmekti, u d lâafia i wid ineêwwaoen. Sbuccaâ, s ccekôan, isem n Mass ik, Ameqwôaêan! Ih, gulle$ seg wanda llan itran! U, tagi, lemmer a ppeéôem, ard tagallit tameqwôaêant! Ar neppa d Leqwôan ukyis, di Tezmamt iffren. Ur t pnalen, siwa wid zeddigen. D tarusi s$uô Mass imavalen. S usali agi, amendeô ma a ppiéidem? S ôôeéq nnwen, kunwi tnekôem? Mara d tawev s agerjum, kunwi, imiren, teppaôoum, Nekwni, sennig wen, i Neqôeb $uôes, maca, ur twalam ara. Xas ma ur tellim d wid ur nepwalas, erret p id, ma tessawalem tidep! Ma illa seg iqôiben, ihi, abeêri, laâîeô, di leonan n ssuâada. Ma illa seg iyeffusen: "i keçç tifrat, seg iyeffusen"! Ma illa seg inekkaôen innetlafen, axxam is seg waman ippayzagen, ad iô$ deg ujajiê. Ayagi, ih, d tidep itebbten. Sbuccaâ, s ccekôan, isem n Mass ik Ameqwôaêan!
سُوۡرَةُ الۡحَدِيۡدِ Sbuccuâen, s ccekôan Öebbi, ayen akw illan di tmurt akked igenwan. Neppa d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab. IneS tagelda n tmurt akked igenwan; Issidir, Ineqq; u Neppa Izmer i yal cci. D Neppa ay d amezwaru, ay d aneggaru; d ayen d ibanen akked wayen iffren. Neppa Iéôa yal cci. D Neppa i Ixelqen tamurt akked igenwan di sdis wussan. Sinna, Iâannec af usgeld. Iéôa i ikeççmen ar tmurt, akked wayen id iteff$en segs, ayen id ippadren seg igenni, akked wayen ippalin $uôes. Neppa yidwen, anda ma tellam. Öebbi Ipwali ayen txedmem. IneS tagelda n tmurt akked igenwan. Ar Öebbi ara u$alen lumuô. Issekcam iv deg wass, Issekcam ass deg yiv. Iéôa ayen illan deg idmaren. Amnet s Öebbi akked Umazan iS! Efket seg wayen i$ef i kwen Irra, degs, d igensas. Wid iumnen segwen, iseddqen, d ameqwôan warraz nnsen. Acu ikwen iu$en, ur tuminem ara s Öebbi? Amazan ipnabi kwen a ppamnem s Mass nnwen. Ni$ $uôes nnesba nnwen, ma tellam d lmumnin. D Neppa id Issadren i umdan iS, issekniyen iberrzen, iwakken a kwen Issuffe$ si tillas ar tafat. Ih, Öebbi, fellawen, d Umâin Ipêunun. Acu ikwen iu$en, ur tepseddiqem deg ubrid n Öebbi? N Öebbi lweôt n tmurt akked igenwan. Ur taâdilem ara: wid iseddqen uqbel l$elb, u nnu$en, widak, ad aâlayen, nezzeh, sennig wid iseddqen sin $er da, u nnu$en. Iwaââed asen akw Öebbi ûûam. Öebbi Iéôa ayen txedmem. Win iôevlen i Öebbi aôeîîal umâin, ad as d Irr s lufa, u ines warraz ukyis. Asmi ara twaliv lmumnin, argaz tameîîut, teddun tafat nnsen zdat sen, u yeffus nnsen: "a lxiô nnwen, assa, di leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen, degsen a pwekkôem! D wagi ay d rrbeê ameqwôaêan". Ass ideg ixabiten, argaz tameîîut, ad inin i wid iumnen: "arout a$, a neddem si tafat nnwen"! A d inin: "u$alet ar deffir, a d tqelbem tafat"! Ad yili garasen lêiv, s tebburt. Zdaxel d aêunu, beôôa, zdat es: aâaqeb. Ad sen d siwlen: "day ur nella ara yidwen"? Ad inin: "ih! Maca, thewwlem iman nnwen, tekkukram, tcukkem, $elvent kwen lemcihwat, armi d iusa lameô n Öebbi. I$elv ikwen af Öebbi, u$ellav". Assa, ur ipwaîîaf feddu segwen, ne$ seg wid ijehlen. Axxam nnwen d times; d neppat ay d bab nnwen. A tu$alin tucmip! Âani maççi d lawan, i wid iumnen, ad rgagin wulawen nnsen ar usmekti n Öebbi, akked wayen id Issers n tidep? Ur ppilin am wid iwumi teppunefk Tezmamt, zik, u tvul fellasen lmudda. D$a qquôen wulawen nnsen; aîas degsen d iballa$en. Ecfut ar Öebbi Issidir tamurt, deffir tmeppant is. Ni$ Nbeggen awen d issekniyen, amendeô ma a pfehmem? Ih, wid akked tid ipseddiqen, iôeîlen i Öebbi aôeîîal umâin, ad asen d Irr s lufa, u nnsen arraz ukyis. Wid iumnen s Öebbi akked imazanen iS, d nitni ay d iêeqqiyen, u d inagan ar Mass nnsen. Ad awin arraz nnsen akked tafat nnsen. Wid ijehlen u skaddben issekniyen nne£, widak d at ujajiê. Cfut ar tameddurt n ddunit d urar kan, d zzhu, d acebbeê, d zzux garawen, asuget n wayla akked derya. Am umedya ugeffur. Im$an is âaoben ijehliyen; sinna, ad isliwen, a ten twaliv ppiwôi$en; d$a ad êevmen. Di laxeôt, aâaqeb uqsiê akked ssmaê s$uô Öebbi, akked llza. Tameddurt n ddunit d zzehwa kan ip$uôôun. £iwlet ar ssmaê n Mass nnwen, akked Loennet iwesâan am tmurt akked igenni, teppuhegga d i wid iumnen s Öebbi akked imazanen iS. D wagi ay d lfevl n Öebbi. Ippak it i win i S ihwan. Öebbi d Bab n lfevl ameqwôaêan. Ur d tveôôu twa$it di tmurt, ne$ deg iman nnwen, siwa ma tura di Tezmamt, uqbel a p id Nawi. Ayagi, s tidep, d ayen isehlen i Öebbi. Iwakken ur kwen ip$av wayen tzeglem, ur kwen issefôaê wayen i wen Ifka. Öebbi ur Iêemmel ara yal amzuxi, imnefxi, wid ipcuêêun, iêeppmen ccêa af medden. Win i iwexxôen…ihi, Öebbi d Asâay, d Amaâzuz. Nuzen ed imazanen nne£, s ubeggen. Nessader ed yidsen Tazmamt akked lmizan, iwakken ad ddun imdanen s lêeqq. Ur qumen ara yis, akken iwata. Nefka arraz nnsen i wid iumnen segsen. Aîas, segsen, d iballa$en. A wid iumnen! Ëezzbet i Öebbi. Amnet s Umazan iS. Ih, lfevl deg ufus n Öebbi; Ippak it i win i S ihwan. Öebbi d Bab n lfevl ameqwôaêan.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡمُجَادَلَةِ Ni$ Isla Öebbi i wawal n tin i k d ihedôen $ef urgaz is. Tepcetkay i Öebbi. Öebbi Isla i umeslay nnwen. Öebbi, s tidep, Isell, Iéeô. Wid ipmettilen tilawin nnsen ar izugar n tyimmatin nnsen, ur llint d tiyimmatin nnsen - imi tiyimmatin d tid, kan, i ten id iurwen -, ihi, ar d nnan yir awal, akked tikerkas. Ih, Öebbi ard Win Ipsemmiêen, Ipqilin. Wid imetlen, akka, tilawin nnsen, sinna, wexxôen i wayen d nnan, ad brun i wakli, uqbel a tent nnalen. D ayen u$uô i kwen nuban. Öebbi Iéôa ayen txedmem. Day ur twalav ara ar Öebbi Iéôa i illan di tmurt, i illan deg igenwan? Ur ippili wawal ger krav, mebla ma Illa, Neppa, d wis kué; ne$ ger smus, u Neppa, d wis sdis. Ama seddaw, ne$ sennig waya, ad Yili yidsen, anda ma llan. D$a, ad asen Imel acu xedmen, ass n tnekra. Ih, Öebbi Iéôa yal cci. Ur twalav ara wid i$ef tepwagdel temlilit i umeslay, sinna, u$alen ar wayen i sen ipwagedlen? Ppemlilin i ubekkav, i wanfal, i âaûûu i Umazan. A tu$alin icemten! A wid iumnen! Ma temlalem i wawal, ur ppemlilit ara i ubekkav, i wanfal, i âaûûu i Umazan. Ppemlilit i tezdeg akked uêezzeb. Ëezzbet i Öebbi u$uô ara tepwafesrem. Timlilit i wawal si Cciîan kan, iwakken ad $weblen wid iumnen. Acemma ur ten iîîuôôu, siwa ma Irad Öebbi. £ef Öebbi ara ppeklen lmumnin. A wid iumnen! Öebbi Iéôa ayen txedmem. A wid iumnen! Ma temlalem i wawal akked Umazan, seddqet uqbel timlilit. Akka i wen ilha, i wen iûfa. Ma ur tewâam ara, ihi, Öebbi Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu. Tekukram a pseddqem uqbel timlilit nnwen? Ma ur tseddqem ara, u Issuref awen Öebbi, ééallet, zekkit, a$et awal i Öebbi akked Umazan iS. Öebbi Iéôa ayen txedmem. Day ur twalav ara wid idduklen akked ugdud i$ef Izzaâf Öebbi? Ur llin segwen ne$ segsen. Pgalan s tkerkas, u nitni éôan. Ihegga yasen d Öebbi aâaqeb uqsiê. Ih, ar dir it wayen xeddmen! £ilen tagallit nnsen d ssôan. Swexxiôen seg ubrid n Öebbi. Fellasen aâaqeb isdullun. Ur sen d ippawi acemma wayla nnsen, ne$ dderya nnsen, mgal Öebbi, d awez$i. Widak d at tmes. Degs, nitni, ad wekkôen. Ass ideg ara ten id Issker Öebbi, meôôa, ad aS gallen akken i wen pgallan. Ad $ilen ar ad yili wacu ideg ara îîfen. Aâni maççi, war ccekk, nitni d ikeddaben? Imelk iten Cciîan armi ppun asmekti n Öebbi. Widak d akabar n Cciîan. Ni$ akabar n Cciîan d imexsuôen. Ih, wid ipqamaôen Öebbi akked Umazan iS, widak, ad ndellen sennig wiyav. Iura Öebbi: war ccekk, d Nek akked imazanen iW, ara irebêen. Öebbi, s tidep, d Uohid, d Uzmir. Ur teppafev ara agdud iumnen s Öebbi akked wass aneggaru, ad iddukwel akked wid ipqamaôen Öebbi akked Umazan iS. Xas ma llan d ibabaten nnsen, ne$ d arraw nnsen, d atmaten nnsen, d alag nnsen. Widak, Iura yasen liman deg ulawen nnsen, Iul iten s ôôuê s$uôeS. A ten Issekcem di leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen, degsen ad wekkôen. Öuvan Öebbi, Iôuva ten. Widak d akabar n Öebbi. Day akabar n Öebbi maççi d win ara irebêen?
سُوۡرَةُ الۡحَشۡرِ Sbuccuâen Öebbi kra illan deg igenwan, akked kra illan di tmurt. Neppa d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab. D Neppa i Issuff$en seg ixxamen nnsen wid ijehlen seg At Tezmamt, i ujemmal amezwaru. Ur tuminem ara ad ff$en. £ilen leswaô nnsen a ten sellken si Öebbi. Ikka yasen d Öebbi seg wanda ur bnin. Issekcem tugdi deg ulawen nnsen. Hudden ixxamen nnsen, s ifassen nnsen, akked ifassen n lmumnin. Meyyzet a wid ipwalin! Lemmer ur asen Iura ara Öebbi neffu, yili Iqeîîa ten di ddunit, u, di laxeôt, fellasen aâaqeb n tmes. Ayagi, acku numren Öebbi akked Umazan iS. Win inumren Öebbi, ihi, Öebbi, Iwâaô i uqeîîi. Ayen tgezmem n tezdayin akked wayen teooam beddent af iéuôan nnsent, s wannuf n Öebbi, iwakken a d Isdull iballa$en. Ayen i s Ifka Öebbi, s$uôsen, i Umazan iS, ur tebgisem fellas s ioedâen akked lemrakeb. Maca, Öebbi Ippak adabu i Umazan iS, $ef wid i S ihwan. Öebbi Izmer i yal cci. Ayen Ifka Öebbi i Umazan iS, s$uô at tuddar, n Öebbi akked Umazan iS, llezm is, igujilen, ime$ban, akked win d ibbwi ubrid. Iwakken ur ippu$al ara ger ifassen imeôkantiyen nnwen. Ayen i wen ifka Umazan, ddmet ep. Ayen i wen ikkes, kkset ep. Ëezzbet i Öebbi. Ih, Öebbi, Iwâaô i uqeîîi. I igellilen iminigen, id ssuff$en seg ixxamen nnsen akked seg wayla nnsen, ssaramen lfevl n Öebbi akked llza, fkan afus i Öebbi akked Umazan iS, d widak ay d imawlan n tidep. Wid ized$en ixxamen, iumnen uqbel nnsen, êemmlen wid id iunagen $uôsen. Ur néifen idmaren nnsen af wayen i sen ippunefken, smenyafen ten i iman nnsen, xas ma gwran d xuûûen. Wid irran akin ccêa af yiman nnsen, widak d imerbaê. Wid id iusan deffir sen, qqaôen: "a Mass nne$! Semmeê a$, akked wamaten nne$, i $ d izwaren ar liman. Ur Ppara deg ulawen nne$, a$ullu n wid iumnen. A Mass nne$! Keçç, s tidep, d Umâin Ipêunun". Ur twalav ara ixabiten, la qqaôen i watmaten nnsen ijehlen, seg wAt Tezmamt: "ma ssuff$en kwen, ard a neffe$ yidwen, ur nessemêas i yiwen, d awez$i, mgal nnwen. Ma nnu$en kwen, ar ad awen nefk afus". Ad Icehhed Öebbi, ar nitni d ikeddaben. Ma ssuff$en ten, ur teff$en yidsen. Ma nnu$en ten, ur asen ppaken afus. Ma âawnen ten, ad rewlen; ihi, ur ppâawanen! D kunwi, sennig Öebbi, ay ugaden idmaren nnsen, ayagi, acku nitni d agdud ur nefhim. Ur kwen pna$en, ddukwlen, siwa ma di temdinin ippwaéeôben, ne$ deffir leswaô. Lbe$wv garasen qesseê. A pxilev dduklen, wanag rwin wulawen nnsen. Ayagi, acku nitni d agdud ur nepxemmim. Cban wid i ten id izwaren s cwiî kan, jeôôben lwexda igiten nnsen, fellasen aâaqeb aqeôêan. Cban Cciîan, mi s inna i umdan: "ejhel"! Mi ijhel, inna: "nek mgirrde$ k, nek ugade$ Öebbi, Mass imavalen"! D times, ih, ara yilin d taggara nnsen, ad wekkôen dinna. Ayagi d arraz imednas. A wid iumnen! Ëezzbet i Öebbi. Yal yiwen iwata ad iwali acu ihegga i uzekka. Ëezzbet i Öebbi. Ih, Öebbi Ippuxebbeô $ef wayen txeddmem. Ur ppilit am wid ippun Öebbi. Irra ten, ppun iman nnsen. Widak d iballa$en. Ur aâdilen ara at tmes akked at Loennet. At Loennet d imerbaê. Lemmer id Nessader Leqwôan agi af udrar, a t twaliv iunez, ifelleq, si tugdi n Öebbi. D wigi ay d imedyaten id Neppawi i medden, amar ad meyyzen. Neppa d Öebbi, ur illi ôebbi siwa Neppa, Amusnaw n wayen iffren akked wayen ur neffir. Neppa, d Aênin Ipêunun. D Neppa, ur illi ôebbi siwa Neppa, ay d Agellid, d Ssid, d Tifrat, d Bab n liman, d Aâssas, d Uzmir, d Ajebbaô, d Ameqwôaêan. Gedha s Öebbi, mgal wayen pcaraken! Neppa d Öebbi, d Axellaq, d Bab usisi, d Amessal. I Neppa ismawen imxulaf mavi. Sbuccuâen T akw kra illan di tmurt akked igenwan. Neppa, d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡمُمۡتَحِنَةِ A wid iumnen! Ur ddukulet d icenga W akked icenga nnwen. Teram ten d iêbiben, u nitni nekôen ayen id iusan, $uôwen, n tidep. Èèéaân Amazan, ééaân kwen, imi tumnem s Öebbi, Mass nnwen. Ma teff$em a ppenna$em deg ubrid iW, u tepnadim ôôva W, day a ten terrem, s tuffra, d iêbiben? Nek, Ife$ akw akken èôi$, ayen teffrem akked wayen tennam. Win, segwen, ixedmen akka, innetlaf seg ubrid umâin. Ma $elben kwen, ad u$alen d icenga nnwen, a kwen merten s ifassen nnsen akked yilsawen nnsen, ad ssirmen a pjehlem. Ass n tnekra, ur kwen infaâ walag, ne$ tarwa nnwen, d awez$i. Ad Ifrez garawen. Öebbi Ipwali igiten nnwen. Ni$ illa i kunwi umedya ucbiê di Ibôahim akked wid illan yides, mi nnan i ugdud nnsen: "nemgirred ikwen, kunwi akked wayen teppanzem, war Öebbi. Nenkeô ikwen. Taâdawt akked dd$el, ersen d garane$, i lebda, alamma tumnem s Öebbi Yiwen". Kkes ed awalen i inna Ibôahim, i baba s: "ad velbe$ a ppeppusemmêev, xas ur iyi Ikellef Öebbi, fellak, s wacemma". A Mass nne$! Ppkal nne$ fellaK; nutub iK; $uôeK tu$alin. A Mass nne$ ur a$ Ppara d ahewwel i wid ijehlen. A Mass nne$! Semmeê a$. Ih, Keçç d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab. Ni$, i kunwi, amedya nnsen ucbiê, i wid iggunin Öebbi akked wass aneggaru. Ma d win iwexxôen, ihi, Öebbi d Asâay, d Amaâzuz! Ahat Öebbi ad Irr tadukli garawen akked wid, segsen, i illan d icenga nnwen. Öebbi d Uzmir, Öebbi Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu. Ur awen Ikkis ara Öebbi, a pmaânem u tweznem, ar wid ur kwen nepna$ di ddin, ur kwen nessuffu$ seg ixxamen nnwen. Öebbi, s tidep, Iêemmel wid iweznen. I awen Ikkes Öebbi, d tadukli akked wid i kwen ipna$en di ddin, i kwen issuff$en seg ixxamen nnwen, ppaken afus mara kwen ssuff$en. Wid iddan yidsen, widak d imednas. A wid iumnen! Ma usant ed $uôwen tid iumnen, iunagen, jeôôbet pent. Öebbi Iéôa sennig akw liman nnsent. Ma tufam tent d tid iumnen, ur tent pparat ara i ijehliyen. Ur asen êellent, ur asent êellen. Efket asen ayen ûûeôfen. Ulac u$ilif ma tu$em tent, ma tefkam asent tuççit nnsent. Ur pnasabet tijehliyin. Ssutret ayen tûeôôfem, ad ssutren ayen ûûeôfen. Akka ay d aêuddu n Öebbi. Ipêuddu garawen. Öebbi d Amusnaw, d Bab n ûûwab. Ma terwel tmeîîut, si tlawin nnwen, ar ijehliyen, sinna, tâaqbem, efket, ayen ûûeôfen, i wid iwumi ôôuêent tlawin nnsen. Ëezzbet i Öebbi, syiS ay tumnem. A Nnbi! Ma usant ed $uôek tid iumnen, ad ak gallent ur pcarakent i Öebbi acemma, ur ppakwrent, ur zennunt, ur neqqent tarwa nnsent, ur teccvent s ifassen ne$ s ivaôen nnsent, ur k ppâuûunt di lewqama, eôêeb yisent, ssuter i Öebbi ad asent Isemmeê. Öebbi, s tidep, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu. A wid iumnen! Ur ddukulet akked agdud i$ef Izzâaf Öebbi. Ni$ uysen laxeôt, akken uysen ijehliyen wid illan di tneîlin.
سُوۡرَةُ الصَّفِّ Sbuccuâen Öebbi, kra illan deg igenwan, akked kra illan di tmurt. Neppa d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab. A wid iumnen! Acimi id teqqaôem ayen ur txeddmem? D lâaô meqqwôen, ar Öebbi, ma teqqaôem ayen ur txeddmem. Ih, Öebbi Iêemmel wid ipna$en deg ubrid iS, d ûûef, nitni, amzun d lebni, iéevêen. Mi inna Musa i ugdud is: "a yagdud iw! Acimi la yi teîîuôum, u ni$ teéôam nek d amazan n Öebbi $uôwen"? Mi ff$en i ubrid, Öebbi Issuffe$ i ubrid ulawen nnsen. Öebbi ur Inehhu ara agdud iballa$en. Mi inna Âisa, mmi s n Meryem: "A yAt Isôail! Nek d amazan n Öebbi $uôwen, ad tebbte$ ayen iyi d izwaren n Tuôa. U a kwen beccôe$ s Umazan ara d iasen, deffir i, ism is Aêmed". Mi ten id iusa s ubeggen, nnan: "wagi d ssêur n ûûeê". Anwa idensen sennig win id igren tikerkas af Öebbi, u neppa ipwanced ar wannuz? Öebbi ur Inehhu agdud imednas. B$an ad ssexsin tafat n Öebbi, s imawen nnsen. Öebbi ad Itim tafat iS, di nneqwma ijehliyen. D Neppa id Iuznen Amazan iS, s nnhaya, d ddin n tidep, iwakken a t issifrir f ddin meôôa, di nneqwma ijehliyen. A wid iumnen! Ma d awen Mle$ ssuq ara kwen isellken seg uâaqeb aqeôêan? Amnet s Öebbi akked Umazan iS. Nna$et deg ubrid n Öebbi s wayla nnwen, u s yiman nnwen; ppif akka i kunwi, lemmer tessinem. Ad awen Isemmeê ibekkaven nnwen; a kwen Issekcem ar leonanat degsen isaffen ppazzalen, tinezdu$in igerzen, di leonanat n Âaden; d wagi ay d rrbeê ameqwôaêan. Ayen têemmlem nniven: afus s$uô Öebbi akked l$elb aqôib. Ssefôeê lmumnin. A wid iumnen! Illit d iwiziwen n Öebbi, akken inna Âisa, mmi s n Meryem, i inmahalen is: "anwi ay d iwiziwen iw ar Öebbi"? Nnan d inmahalen: "nekwni d iwiziwen n Öebbi". Tumen terbaât, tejhel terbaât, n At Isôail. Nefka afus i wid iumnen, mgal icenga nnsen, d$a rebêen.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡجُمُعَةِ Sbuccuâen Öebbi, kra illan deg igenwan, u kra illan di tmurt. Agellid, Ssid, Uzmir, Bab n ûûwab. D Neppa id Iuznen i wid ur ne$ôi, Amazan segsen, iqqaô asen issekniyen iS. Izizdig iten, isselmad asen Tazmamt akked ûûwab, xas llan, zik, di ttelfan n ûûeê. U i wid nniven, mara awven $uôsen. Neppa, d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab. D wagi ay d lfevl n Öebbi. Ippak it i win Ib$a. Öebbi, d bab n lfevl ameqwôahan. Am wid iwumi ippukelfen s Tuôa, ur p ssawven. Cuban a$yul ibubben tizmamin. I icmet umedya n ugdud inekôen issekniyen n Öebbi! Öebbi ur Inehhu ara agdud imednas. Ini: "a yudayen, ma t$ilem d kunwi ay d iêbiben n Öebbi, war imdanen, ssutret tameppant, ma tessawalem tidep"! Ur p ssuturen ara, d awez$i, ilmend igiten nnsen. Öebbi Issen imednas. Ini: "tameppant iwumi tregwlem, a kwen id temmager, war ccekk. Sinna, a kwen awin ar Win Iéôan ayen iffren akked wayen ur neffir. Ad awen Imel ayen txeddmem". A wid iumnen! Ma ssawlen d i téallit, ass unejmuâ, $iwlet ar usmekti n Öebbi, êebset ttjaôa. Ppif akka i kunwi, lemmer tessinem. Mi tfukk téallit, mfaôaqet di tmurt, nadit lfevl n Öebbi, mmektit ed aîas Öebbi, amar a prebêem. Mi walan ssuq, ne$ anecôeê, ad azlen $uôes, a k ooen tbeddev. Ini: "ayen illan ar Öebbi yif anecôeê akked ssuq. Öebbi Yif akw iôeééaqen".
سُوۡرَةُ الۡمُنَافِقُوۡنَ Ma usan d $uôek ixabiten, ad ak inin: "a ncehhed ar keçç, war ccekk, d Amazan n Öebbi". Öebbi Iéôa ar keçç, war ccekk, d Amazan iS. Öebbi ad Icehhed ar, s tidep, ixabiten d ikeddaben. Ëesben tagallit nnsen d laânaya, d$a ssefôa$en abrid n Öebbi. Ihi, a yicmet wayen xeddmen! Akka, acku llan umnen, sinna, jehlen. Ppusel$en wulawen nnsen, d$a nitni ur mêiûen. Mi ten twalav, a k taâoeb tiddi nnsen. Ma mmeslayen, tessemêasev i wawal nnsen. Amzun nitni d is$aôen i isenden, $ilen yal ti$ôi fellasen. Acengu, d nitni; êader iman ik segsen. A ten Ine$ Öebbi! Acêal wexxôen! Ma nnan asen: "yyaw, ad issuter Umazan n Öebbi a ppeppusemmêem", ad bernen iqweôôa nnsen, a ten twaliv wexxôen s tem$weô. Iâuva fellasen tessutrev, ne$ ur tessutrev ad ppusemmêen. Ur sen Ipsemmiê Öebbi, d awez$i. Öebbi, s tidep, ur Inehhu agdud iballa$en. Nitni i iqqaôen: "ur pseddiqet, i wid iddan akked Umazan n Öebbi, alamma mmebruzzâen". N Öebbi igerrujen igenwan akked tmurt, maca ixabiten ur mêiûen. Qqaôen: "ma nu$al ar Lmadina, war ccekk, uzmir ad issuffe$, segs, uôhif". Tazmert, n Öebbi akked Umazan iS, akked lmumnin, maca, ixabiten ur éôin. A wid iumnen! £uôwat a kwen ssbaâden, af usmekti n Öebbi, wayla nnwen akked tarwa nnwen! Wid igan akka, ihi, widak d imexsuôen. Ssedqet seg wayen i wen Nefka, uqbel a d tas tmeppant ar yiwen degwen, ad yini: "a Mass iw! Lemmer ad iyi Teswexxôev ar lajel aqôib, ad seddqe$, ad ili$ seg wid imaânen". Ur Irennu Öebbi di laâmeô, d awez$i, ma iusa d lajel is. Öebbi Ippuxebbeô $ef wayen txeddmem.
سُوۡرَةُ التَّغَابُنِ I illan deg igenwan, i illan di tmurt, sbuccuâen Öebbi. IneS tagelda; ineS wannuz; Neppa Izmer i yal cci. Neppa ikwen Ixelqen; segwen ajehli, segwen lmumen. Öebbi Ipwali ayen txeddmem. Ixleq tamurt akked igenwan, s tidep. Imsel ikwen, Iûeggem amsal nnwen. £uôeS tu$alin. Iéôa i illan di tmurt akked igenwan. Iéôa ayen teffrem akked wayen tennam. Öebbi Iéôa i illan deg idmaren. Ma iusa kwen id usali n wid illan, zik, d ijehliyen? Jeôben lwexda n tikli nnsen. Fellasen, aâaqeb aqeôêan. Ayagi, imi sen ppasen imazanen nnsen s ubeggen. Nnan: "aâni d amdan ara $ inhun"? D$a jehlen, xedâan. Ur Iclaâ Öebbi. Öebbi d Asâay, d Amaâzuz. Pputebten ijehliyen ar, d awez$i, ur d pnekkaren. Ini: "xaîi! S Mass iw, ard a d tekkrem, sinna ard a ppepwaxebbôem $ef wayen txeddmem"! Ayagi, i Öebbi, d ushil. Ihi, amnet s Öebbi akked Umazan iS, akked tafat id Nessers. Öebbi Ippuxebbeô $ef wayen txeddmem. Ass ideg ara kwen Issemlil, i wass ujemmel, ass nni, d ass um$uôôu. Win iumnen s Öebbi, ixeddmen ayen ilhan, ad as Ikkes tucmitin is, a t Issekcem ar leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen, degsen ad iwekkeô i lebda. D wagi ay d rrbeê ameqwôaêan. Wid ijehlen u inekôen issekniyen nne£, widak d at tmes, degs ad wekkôen. A taggara icemten! Ur d teppas twa$it, siwa ma Irad Öebbi. Win iumnen s Öebbi, ad Inhu ul is. Öebbi Iéôa yal cci. A$et awal i Öebbi, a$et awal i Umazan! Ma twexxôem, i iwatan kan, i Umazan nne£, siwa anabi ipbegginen. Öebbi, ur illi ôebbi siwa Neppa. £ef Öebbi ara ppeklen lmumnin. A wid iumnen! S tidep, kra n tlawin nnwen akked tarwa nnwen, d icenga nnwen. Ëadret iman nnwen segsen! Ma tsemmêem, teppum, tsemmêem, Öebbi, s tidep, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu. Ayla nnwen akked dderya nnwen, d ahewwel kan, wanag, ar Öebbi, illa warraz ameqwôahan. Ëezzbet i Öebbi ayen iwumi tzemrem. Ëesset, ôavit, seddqet! Yif it i iman nnwen. Wid ikksen ccêa i iman nnsen, widak d imerbaê. Ma tôevlem i Öebbi aôeîîal igerzen, ad awen d Irr sin imuren, ad awen Isemmeê. Öebbi Iceffu, Iêellem. Amusnaw n wayen iffren akked wayen ivehôen, Uzmir, Bab n ûûwab.
سُوۡرَةُ الطَّلَاقِ A Nnbi! Mara tebrum i tlawin, brut asent mara tâaddi tallit n tarda nnsent. Ëesbet tallit. Ëezzbet i Öebbi, Mass nnwen. Ur tent ssuffu$et si texxamin nnsent, ur d teff$ent, siwa ma, s tidep, ccvent. D tigi ay d tilisa n Öebbi. Win izegren tilisa n Öebbi, ni$ idens imanis. Ur teéôiv ara, ahat Öebbi a d Iazen lameô, ssyen $eô da. Mi ssawvent lajel nnsent, âacôet pent s lewqama, ne$ mfaôaqet yidsent, s lewqama. Awit ed sin inagan iêeqqiyen segwen, a d cehhden zdat Öebbi. Ataya wayen u$uô ppunedôen, wid iumnen s Öebbi akked wass aneggaru. Win ipêezziben i Öebbi, ad as Ildi tibbura, a t I$it s wanda ur iêtim. Win iîîfen di Öebbi, a t Iqennaâ. Ih, Öebbi Issâadday lameô iS. Ni$ Öebbi Iwzen yal cci. I tigad, n tlawin nnwen, i iuysen tarda, ma illa ccekk, tallit ugani nnsent: krav wagguren. Akken i tid ur nebdi tarda. Tid ibbwin tadist, tallit nnsent ar tinnufra nnsent. Win ipêezziben i Öebbi, s lameô iS, ad as Istiser. D wagi ay d lameô n Öebbi i wen d Issers. Win ipêezziben i Öebbi, ad as Ikkes tucmitin is, ad Issali arraz is. Ad asent tefkem tanezdu$t anda tzed$em, akken tewâam. Ur tent îîuôôut s tririt nnsent ar lêeôs. Ma llant s tadist, ûeôôfet fellasent, alamma d tinnufra nnsent. Ma ssuîvent tarwa nnwen, efket asent taqdiât nnsent; mwafaqet s tiéeî. Ma temnamarem, a ppessuîîev tmeîîut nniven. Bu udrim ad iûeôôef segs. Win ixuû ôôeéq ad iûeôôef seg wayen i s Ifka Öebbi. Ur Ipkellif Öebbi taôwiêt, siwa ar ayen i s Ifka. Öebbi ad Issuffe$ laâtab ar tafat. Acêal n temdinin i inuqmen lameô n Mass nnsent akked imazanen iS! Nêuseb itent leêsab uqsiê. Nâaqeb itent s uâaqeb issexven. Jeôôbent lwexda igiten nnsent. D lexsaôa ay d iooa lameô nnsent. Öebbi Ihegga yasen aâaqeb uqsiê. Ëezzbet i Öebbi a yuâqilen iumnen! Ni$ Öebbi Issers awen d asmekti; Amazan i wen immalen issekniyen n Öebbi iberrzen, iwakken ad Issuffe$, si tillas ar tafat, wid iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan. Wid iumnen s Öebbi, ixeddmen ayen ilhan, a ten Issekcem ar leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen, degsen ad wekkôen i lebda. Ni$ Öebbi Igerrez asen ôôeéq. Öebbi i Ixelqen ûa igenwan, akked tmurt am nitni. Lameô iprusu garasen, iwakken a ppeéôem ar Öebbi Izmer i yal cci, u Öebbi Izzi i yal cci s tmusni.
سُوۡرَةُ التَّحۡرِيۡمِ A Nnbi! Ay$eô tgedlev ayen i k Iêell Öebbi? Tqennâav tilawin ik. Öebbi Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu. Öebbi Iêeppem fellawen a pêentem. Öebbi d Bab nnwen. Neppa d Amusnaw, d Bab n ûûwab. Mi inna Nnbi sser, i yiwet si tlawin is, u temla, Öebbi Issken it i neppa. Ixebbeô s wumur, iffer amur, segs. Mi p iaâlem s waya, tenna: "wi k imlan aya"? Inna: "Imla yi t Win Issnen, Ippuxebbôen". Ma tutubemt Öebbi, ihi knan wulawen n kwent. Ma tedduklemt as, ihi, d Öebbi ay d Bab is, u, deffir waya, ad ilin di talalt is: Jebrayen, ûûam n lmumnin, u lmalayek ad fkent afud. سُوۡرَةُ الۡمُدَّثِّرِ A win ipwadlen! Ekker, endeô! Mass ik, ssem$weô! Iceîîiven ik, zzizdeg! Timenqas janeb! Ur ppak ma tuôoiv kteô! I Mass ik, eûbeô! Ma ûuven di lbuq, assen, ihi, d ass uwâiô. Ur ippili d yiser, i ijehliyen. Eooet iyI, akked win Xelqe$ d afôid. Fki$ as ayla iwerrken, akked tarwa d imsaâfen. Ssehle$ as, ad istumen. Sinna issarem ad Rnu$. Xaîi! Atan, issekniyen nne£, inkeô iten. Ad êeppme$ fellas ssxev. Ih, ixemmem, d$a iseyya. Ipwasxev f akken iseyya. Da$en, ipwasxev f akken iseyya. Sinna, imuqel. Sinna, ikres tagwenza, innu$ben. Sinna, izzux, ibren. D$a inna: "wagi d ssêur kan ippulemden. Ayagi d awal kan n umdan". A t Fke$ i tmes iôeqqen. W ara k imlen, d acu p tmes iôeqqen? Ur teppaooa, ur tessagwar. Tesseô$a igwelman. Nnig es mrawtza. D lmalayek kan i Nerra d imawlan n tmes. Nefka d kan amvan nnsent, iwakken ad hewwlen wid ijehlen; ad pputebbten wid iwumi teppunefk Tezmamt; ad innerni liman n wid iumnen; ur ippili ccekk ar wid iwumi teppunefk Tezmamt, akked lmumnin; akken ad inin at wul iblan, akked ijehliyen: "acu i Ib$a Öebbi s umedya agi"? Akka, Itellif Öebbi win i S ihwan, Inehhu win i S ihwan. Iâsekôiwen n Mass ik, siwa Neppa iten Issnen. Wagi d asmekti kan i imdanen. Xaîi! S waggur! S yiv ma isahel! S tafrara ma tecâal! Ar neppat d tabarart. D aâggen i medden. I win ib$an, segwen, ad iqeddem, ne$ ad iwexxeô. Yal iman d ameôhun n wayen ixdem. Kkes ed iyeffusen. Di Loennet pmesteqsayen af ibe$wviyen: "ar tmes acu i kwen ibbwin"? A d inin: "ur nelli seg wid iéullen. Ur necceççay aéawali. Nella nepjuôu akked imjuôen. Nella d inekkaôen n wass iqeîîiyen, armi d iusa i a$ itebbten". Ur ten tenfaâ ccafuâa imcafâen. Mi ugin asmekti, d acu ten iu$en? Cuban i$wyal ixelâan, i irewlen i izem. Zi$ yal yiwen degsen ib$a ad as d asen isebtar ifesren. Xaîi! Laxeôt, ur p ugaden. Xaîi! Wagi, war ccekk, d asmekti. Win ib$an, a t ismekti. Siwa ma Ib$a Öebbi ara d smektayen. D Neppa ay d Bab uêezzeb, d Bab n ssmaê.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡقِيَامَةِ Ggule$ s wass n tnekra! Ggule$ s yiman bu tuzzma! Aâni i$il umdan, i$san is, ur ten Nessemlili ara? Xaîi! Nezmer a Nesserked iduren is. Maca, ib$a umdan ad irnu di tucmitin. Isteqsay anda t wass n tnekra. Ma tullsent wallen, u i$ab waggur, u iîij akked waggur pwazdin; assen, amdan ad yini: "tarewla sani"? Xaîi! Ssôan ur illi. Axxam ippuôe$ben, ar Mass ik, ass nni. Assen, ad ippuxebbeô umdan $ef wayen ibbwi ar zdat, akked wayen irra ar deffir. Ih, amdan, deg iman is, ad iwali. Xas issuter ssmaê. Ur pêerrik, yis, iles ik, a d t$iwlev yis. Fella£ ajemmel is akked t$uôi s. Mara t N$eô, ihi, ssel i t$uôi s. Sinna, ih, fella£ abeggen is. Xaîi! Wanag têemmlem taêemmaqt. Di laxeôt, testehzayem. Udmawen, assen, ad feooeoen. Ar Mass nnsen, ad pmuqulen. Udmawen, assen, ad neééfen. Ëûan, i twa$it ad ppunefken. Xaîi! Mi tuli ar irawen, ad inin: "anwa ay d agezzan"? U iêûa ar wagi d lefôaq. Imlal ufud ar ufud. Ar Mass ik, assen, tanheôt. Ur iumin, ur ipéalla; U irna inkeô, iwexxeô. Sinna, ar twacult is irra s pnefxa. A lwexda k, a lwexda! D$a, a lwexda k, a lwexda! Aâni i$il umdan d ilelli i ippuserreê? Aâni ur illi d tiqqit iuzlen n l$ella? Sinna, iu$al d argen. D$a Ixleq, Imsel. Irra segs tayuga, ddkeô akked nnta. Aâni Wa ur Izmir a d Issider lmeggtin?
سُوۡرَةُ الدَّهۡرِ Day tâadda tallit $ef umdan ideg ur illi d ayen ipwabedren? Ih, Nexleq amdan si tiqqit n l$ella ixelven. A t Njeôôeb, Nerra t isell, ipwali. Nebbwi t d ubrid, ama isnemmir, ne$ inkeô. Nhegga, ih, i ijehliyen, sslasel, aruz, u$ud. Iâaôviyen, s tidep, ad swen, di lkas, ayen ixelîen akked lkafuô. Tala ideg tessen ixdimen n Öebbi, aman is pfeggiven. Ppaîîafen di tuqqna, ugaden ass ideg lhemm immebruzzaâ. Ppaken lqut, ilmend n lemêibba S, i igellil, i ugujil, i umeêbus. "F udem n Öebbi kan, ay kwen necceççay. Ur neb$i segwen tiririt ne$ tajmilt. Nekwni, ih, nugad Mass nne$, ass awaâôan, aqessêan". Isellek iten Öebbi si lhemm n wassen. Ccbaêa, lfeôê, Ifka yasen. Ikufa ten af wayen ûebôen: leonan, leêrir. Ad éélen din af imîeôêen; ur pwalin iîij, asemmiv. Tili ines $uôsen, izwayen wâan asen. A sen tezzin ibuqalen n lfeîîa, lkisan ulelluc. Alelluc n lfeîîa; taceôt nnsen, s lmizan. Dinna sswan asen lkas n wayen iwumi xelîen skenjbir. Dinna tala; Salsabil i s ssawalen. Ilmeéiyen imezgiyen tezzin asen. Ma twalav ten, ad as tiniv d tiyuqat imfaôaqen. Ma tmuqlev ar din, a pwaliv ssaâd akked tgelda meqqwôen. Iceîîiven i llsan d leêrir aêcici iêewwcen; imeqqyasen n lfeîîa; Isswa ten Mass nnsen, s tissit iûfan. Ih, wagi d arraz nnwen, u d tajmilt igiten nnwen. D Nekwni, s tidep, i k id Issersen Leqwôan, s lmizan. Eûbeô i uêuddu n Mass ik; segsen, ur teccev, ur jehhel. Mmekti d isem n Mass ik, tafrara, tameddit. Deg iv, knu yaS, u sbuccaâ iT tallit $wezzifen. Ih, wigi êemmlen taêemmaqt, stehzan deg wass amôay. Nekwni Nxelq iten, Nesseohed i$san nnsen. Ma ihwa ya£, a Nerr ay ten icban, wakali, deg umkan nnsen. Wagi, s tidep, d asmekti. Win ib$an, ad iddem abrid ar Mass is. Ur tbeqqum, siwa ma Ib$a Öebbi. Öebbi, s tidep, d Amusnaw, d Bab n ûûwab. Win i S ihwan, a t Issekcem ar uêunu S; ma d imednas, Ihegga yasen aâaqeb aqeôêan.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡمُرۡسَلَاتِ S tmersulin, ta s ta! Ipûuvun s lqewwa. ï Veôôêent anevôuê. S tid ifeôqen akken iwata. Ssawavent asmekti, i ssmaê ne$ i uâaggen. A d ias, s tidep, wayen i wen ippuwaââden. Itran, ma xsin; igenni ma inceqq; idurar ma pwiôôéen; imazanen, ma d lweqt nnsen; Anwa t wass u$uô pweoolen? D ass n ufraz. Anwa a d ak imlen d acu t wass n ufraz? Assen, a ssxev inekkaôen! Day ur Nesqucc ara imezwura? Sinna, Nerra ineggura deffir sen. Akka ay Nxeddem i ibe$wviyen. Assen, a nnger inekkaôen! Day ur kwen Nexliq ara si cwiî n waman? Nerra ten deg umekkan muman, ar lajel ipwassnen. Nseyya. Amarezg n Wid Ipseyyin! Assen, a nnger inekkaôen! Day ur nerra ara tamurt d ayen ijemâen wid idren, akked wid immuten. Nerra degs idurar âaooôen. S waman iéidanen, Nesswa kwen. Assen, a nnger inekkaôen! Ddut ar wayen tepnekkiôem! Ddut ar tili m krav idurna! Ur tesburru, ur tesdaray si tmes iôeqqen. Neppat teîîegiô ifîiwjen, am lebôuj aâlayen, amzun d ile$wman iwôa$en. Assen, a nnger inekkaôen! Assa, d ass ideg ur d pmmeslayen. I usuter n ssmaê, ur sen pserriêen. Assen, a nnger inekkaôen! Assa d ass n ufraz. Nessemlal ikwen akked imezwura. Ma tundim, andit iyI! Assen, a nnger inekkaôen! S tidep, di tili akked tliwa, ara ilin wid ipêezziben. Lfakia, d ayen ccihwan. Eççet tesswem, di lehna, ilmend n wayen txeddmem! Ih, akka ay Nepkafi izedganen. Assen, a nnger inekkaôen! Eççet, zzhut cwiî kan, kunwi, war ccekk, d ibe$wviyen! Assen, a nnger inekkaôen! Ma nnan asen: "îîinzet"! Ur îîinizen. Assen, a nnger inekkaôen! Ihi, anwa awal, deffir wagi, ara amnen?
سُوۡرَةُ النَّبَاِ £ef aydeg pmesteqsayen? £ef usali abarar, i$ef mgarraden. Xaîi, ad éôen. Sinna, xaîi, ad éôen. Day ur Nerra ara tamurt d usu, idurar, d ibudiden? Nexleq ikwen d tiwugiwin. Nerra ives nnwen d ôôaêa. Nerra iv d talaba. Nerra ass i tmeddurt. Nebna sennig wen ûa uohiden. Nerna asavef ipôeqôiqen. Nesse$li d, seg usigna, aman d ihedman, iwakken a Nessker, yissen, im$an, iâqqayen, tibêirin ideôsen. Ih, ass n ufraz ipwassen. Ass uûuvu n lbuq, a d tasem d iorawen. S tidep, i wid ipêezziben, amkan n laman; tifeôôanin, iqwiôen; tizzyiwin ifazen; lkisan ifalen. Ur din sellen yir awal ne$ tikerkas. D arraz s$uô Mass ik, d tikci klalen. Mass n tmurt, igenwan, akked wayen illan garasen; Aênin, ur zmiren a ten Ioo a d mmeslayen. Asmi ara beddent lmalayek akked ôôuê, d idurra, siwa win Iooa Uênin ara d immeslayen; a d yini awal uûwib. D wagi ay d ass n tidep; win ib$an, idda d ubrid n tu$alin ar Mass is. Ih, Nâaggen awen: aâaqeb d ayen iqeôben. Ass ideg ara iéeô umdan, acu xedmen ifassen is, ad yini ujehli: "a ssexv iw, a lemmer lli$ d akal"!
سُوۡرَةُ النَّازِعَاتِ S tid iqelâen $evsent! S tid iteddun éewôent! S tid ippâumun s sshala! S tid ipêizwaren d amêizwer! S tid idebbiôen lameô! Ass ideg ara d i$eô ûûut, a t id ivfeô uvfiô, ulawen, ad rgagin, assen. Ad brunt wallen nnsen. Ad inin: "day, s tidep, a d nu$al akken nella? Xas nekwni d i$san irkan"? Ad inin: "ayagi, ihi, d tu$alin n lexsaôa"! Neppa, d yiwet n ti$ôi kan. Atnan u$alen ar tmurt. Ma tusa k id tedyant n Musa? Mi s d Issawel Mass is di Ïuwa, ta$zut iôqan: "ôuê ar Feôâun, atan ijuô. Ini: ma tzemrev a ppizdigev? A k nhu$ ar Mass ik, d$a a ppagwadev". Issenâat as assekni abarar. D$a, iskaddeb, iâuûa. Sinna, ibren, icqa. Issemlal ed, iberreê. Inna: "d nek ay d mass nnwen aâlayan"! Wanag win iugaden ibeddi zdat Mass is, u ikkes cchawi i teôwiêt, ihi, d Loennet ay d ûûôan. Steqsan k af yimir, melmi tisin is. Amek ara t id tdekôev, keçç? Ar Mass ik, agwav is. Keçç d aneddaô kan i win it iugaden. Ihi, nitni, ass ideg ara t walin, amzun qqimen kan tameddit, ne$ tasebêit nni.
سُوۡرَةُ عَبَسَ Ikres anyir, ibren, imi d ader$al it id iusan. W ar ak yinin, ahat d azedgan? Ne$ ismektay, asmekti isfayda t? Wanag, win isâan, d neppa iwumi tgiv ccan. Ur d terziv ma d azedgan. Ma d amsuter id iusan, s wudem ikukran, keçç, degs, d win istehzan. Xaîi! Ihi wagi d asmekti. Ismekti t id win ib$an. Di tewôeqtin ikeysen, aâlayen, zeddigen, ger ifassen imqeddmin, leêôaô, izedganen. Tameppant i umdan! Ay d ajehli! S wacu it Ixleq? Si tiqqit, Ixelq it, Iwezn it. Sinna, abrid Isehhel as t. Nessuffe$ ed, segs, iâaqqayen, tiéuôin, akked wayen zegzawen, tizemrin, tizdayin, iqwiôen iveôsen, tikessawin akked izwayen. D l$it i kunwi, akked lmal nnwen. سُوۡرَةُ التَّكۡوِيۡرِ Ma iu$al itij d akennur. Ma $lin itran. Ma pwanehôen idurar. Ma pwasebblent tle$wmatin, s tdisin. Ma pwafessren lêayawan. Ma îwakenfen ilellen. Ma rran imanen d tiyugiwin. Ma tepwavleb teqcict ipwaneîlen, anwa abekkav i$ef te$wan$a. Ma pwafessrent tewôeqtin. Igenni ma cerrgen t. Times, ma smendgen p. Loennet, ma tuéa d. Ad yissin, yiman, ayen d ihegga. Ihi, Gulle$ s yitran iteffren, ippazalen, ppâidayen! S yiv, ma iôuê! S tûebêit, ma tecôuôeq! Wigi ard awalen Umazan ukyis. Bu tezmert s$uô Bab n usgeld iôesmen. Bab n wannuz, u Muman. I win, segwen, ib$an ad issewqem. Ur tbeqqum, siwa ma Ib$a Öebbi, Mass imavalen.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡاِنۡفِطَارِ Igenni, ma iqlaâ, itran, ma mebruzzâen, ilellen, ma falen, iéekwan, ma nneqlaben, ad iéeô yiman ayen d ibbwi, akked wayen iooa. A yamdan, d acu k i$uôôen, $ef Mass ik Ukyis ik Ixelqen, ik Imesslen, ik Iwezznen? Ifka yak udem i aS iwulmen. Xaîi! Teskiddibem ddin. Ni$ $urwen imêaraben. D imura ukyisen. èôan ayen txeddmem. Ih, di ssaâd, ara ilin iâaôdiyen. Ih, di tmessi, ara ilin ucmiten. A p kecmen, ass iqeîîiyen. Tuff$a segs, ur zmiren. Anwa ara k imlen, d acu t wass iqeîîiyen? Ih! Anwa ara k imlen, d acu t wass iqeîîiyen? D ass ideg yiwen ur izmir ad ifukk yiwen, s wacemma. Assen, lameô i Öebbi.
سُوۡرَةُ المُطَفِّفِيۡنَ Imed$al, a nnegr nnsen! Wid, mara d ktilen ar medden, pêeppimen taceôt. Wanag, nitni, mara ktilen ne$ wezznen, ssenqasen. D tazmamt ipwanesxen. Assen, a nnegr inekkaôen! Wid iskiddiben ass iqeîîiyen. I t inekkôen, siwa amâaûi amednub. Isekniyen nne£, ma $ôan as ten, yini: "d tiêkayin imezwura". Xaîi! S tidep, ar di Âiliyun, ayen ippujerden i iâaôviyen. Âiliyun, anwa ara k t imlen? D tazmamt ipwanesxen. Inagan is d iqôiben. Di ssaâd ara ilin, war ccekk, iâaôviyen! F imîeôêen, ssikiden. A pwaliv deg udmawen nnsen, ticci isaâdiyen. Tissit nnsen d lfayeq ipwacemâen; cmaâ ines d lmesk, f ayagi ad mêizwiren wid ippemêizwiren. Aman n Tasmin, ad as xelîen. D tala ideg tessen iqôiben. Ur d pwaznen ara $uôsen, a ten âassen! Assa, d wid iumnen i ippavûan deg ijehliyen. £ef imîeôêen, ssikiden ma $elten ijehliyen, tirect igiten nnsen.
سُوۡرَةُ الاِنۡشقَاقِ Ma icerreg igenni, issemêess i Mass is, ippuêeppem. Ma temsawi tmurt, tveggeô i illan degs, texla; têess i Mass is, teppuêeppem, a yamdan iôe$ben aîas Mass ik, yideS a ppemlilev! War ccekk, a ppeddum si lêala ar tayev! Acu iten iu$en, ur uminen? Mara sen $ôen Leqwôan, ur kennun. Xaîi! Wid ijehlen skiddiben. Öebbi Issen, sennig akw, ayen teffren. Becceô iten s uâaqeb aqeôêan! سُوۡرَةُ الۡبُرُوۡجِ S igenni bu itran! S wass ippuwaââden! S unagi akked ccada s! At uxenduq pwan$an. Times m iseô$an; mi nitni qqimen $uôes. D nitni ay d inagan n lmumnin f wayen i sen xedmen. Ur illi ay sen stebâan, siwa imi umnen s Öebbi, Uzmir, Amaâzuz. IneS tagelda n tmurt akked igenwan. Öebbi d Anagi n yal cci. Ih, wid ihewwlen lmumnin, argaz tameîîut, ur steôoâen, ad ppuâaqben s Loahennama, ad ppuâaqben s tmeô$iwt. Wanag, i wid iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan, leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen. D wagi ay d rrbeê ameqwôan. Tiyta n Mass ik, s tidep, tewâaô. Neppa, s tidep, Ibeddu, Ippales. Neppa, Ipsemmiê, Iêemmel. Bab n usgeld, Amaâzuz. Ixeddem ayen i S ihwan.
