سُوۡرَةُ الطَّارِقِ S igenni, akked yitri n yiv! W ara k imlen d acu t itri n yiv? Ipôeôiq itri n yiv. Yal iman fellas amêareb. Ad iwali umdan seg wacu ipwaxleq. Ipwaxleq s waman id ifin. Ff$en ed ger tgeééal akked tgwejda. Ih, Izmer a t id Issker, Neppa. Ass ideg lesrar ur drigen ara. Ur isâi kra n tezmert ne$ n tallalt. S igenni bab n tririt! S tmurt ipceqqiqen! Ar neppa d awal ifeûûlen. Ur illi d urar waya. Atnan, ih, ppandin ticeôkep. Ad Andi$ ticeôkep. I ijehliyen eoo lmudda, eoo asen cwiî lmudda.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡاَعۡلٰي Sbuccaâ ism n Mass ik, Aâlayan, Ixelqen, Issemsaway, Iwezznen, Inhan, I d Issuff$en takessawt, sinna, Ippara p d asa$uô aberkan. A k Ness$eô, ur teppu, siwa ayen Irad Öebbi. Ih, Neppa, Issen ayen ibanen, akked wayen iffren. A k Nawi ar liser. Smmekti mi infaâ usmekti. A d ismmekti win iugaden. Ageswaê ijuneb it. Di tmes tabarart mavi ara iô$. Degs, ur ipmeppat, ur ippidir. Amarezg n win zeddigen! I ismektayen ism n Mass is, d$a ipéalla. Maca, tesmenyafem tameddurt n ddunit. Tif ip laxeôt, a pdum kteô. Ayagi, illa di tewôeqtin timezwura, Tiwôeqtin n Ibôahim akked Musa.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡغَاشِيَةِ Ma tebbweb ik id teqsiî n te$wlalt? Ad anzen wudmawen, assen. Ad xedmen, ad merten. Ad ô$en di tmes izehren. Ad asen sswen aman ippayzagen. Ur asen illi wuççi, siwa timeôéuga. Ur ssufayent, ur sseôwayent. Udmawen, assen nnecôaêen. öÔ Öuvan laâtab nnsen, di Loennet aâlayen. Yir awal, ur din sellen. Degs, tala ippazalen. Degs, imîeôêen aâlayen. Iqbucen wejden. Tisumtiwin iderrsen. Tiôakniwin issan. Acimi ur pmuqulen ara al$wem, amek ipwaxleq, u igenni, amek iuli, u idurar, amek âaoôen, u tamurt, amek temsuwa? Ihi, mmekti! Keçç d win kan ismektayen. Ur telliv d amôay nnsen. Kkes ed win iwexxôen, ijehlen. Ad as Iheggi Öebbi aâaqeb abarar mavi. Ni$ $uône£ tu$alin nnsen! Sinna, s tidep, fella£ aqeîîi nnsen.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡفَجۡرِ S tafrara! S mraw wavan! S wayugan akked waryugan! S yiv, ma ilêa! Day maççi dagi d tagallit i lfahem? Day ur twalav ara amek Ixdem Mass ik, i Âad? Iôam m tgejda; ur tepwaxleq temtilt is, di tmura. U Tamud, di te$zut, i i$zan tiéôa. Ferâun, bu ibudiden. Wid ijuôen di tmurt. Degs ssugten lefsad Iwwet iten Mass ik, s ujekwav uâaqeb. Ih, Mass ik d Amâassi. Amdan ma Ijeôôeb it Mass is, I$at it, Iga yas ccan, ad yini: "d Mass iw iyi Iâuzzen". Wanag, ma Ijeôôeb it, I$at it kan s lmizan, ad yini: "d Mass iw iyi Igelzen". Xaîi! Agujil, ur t tepâuzzum! Ur teppemtebbatem ar ume$bun, a t tecceççem! Teppeppem lweôt, têellqem! Têemlem ayla, tayri war tilas. Xaîi! Ma temsawi tmurt, yal amsawi, u Iusa d Mass ik, akked lmalayek, d idurra, assen, a d ters Loahennama. Assen, a d ismekti umdan. Acu ar as d iawi usmekti? Ad yini: "a ssexv iw! A lemmer hegga$ i tmeddurt iw"! Aâaqeb is, assen, ur t isâadda yiwen. Yiwen ur ipwaqqen akken ipwaqqen. A yiman illan di laman, u$al ar Mass ik, d amôavi ôuvan! Ekcem ger imdanen iW! Ekcem di Loennet iW!
سُوۡرَةُ الۡبَلَدِ Xaîi! Gulle$ s temdint a! U keçç d ilelli, di temdint a. S ubabat akked wayen id iurew! Ar Nxelq ed amdan d ûûam. Day inwa ur as izmir yiwen? Iqqaô: "sgullze$ lerbaê, werrken". Day inwa ur t iéôi yiwen? Day ur as Nefka ara snat wallen, iles, sin icenfiren? Nenha t di sin iberdan meqqwôen. Ur idhim deg win iulin. Abrid iulin, anwa ara k t imlen? Aserreê i wakli, ne$ acceççi, di tallit n cceôô, ugujil aqôib, igellil izellîen. Akked tilin seg wid iumnen, i ppemyenhun ar ûûbeô, u ppemyenhun ar lmaênana. Widak d at yeffus. Wid iugin issekniyen nne£, nitni d at zelmev. Times a ppezzi fellasen.
سُوۡرَةُ الشَّمۡسِ S tafugt akked tafat is! S waggur, mara p ivfeô! S wass, mi p ifet! S yiv, mi s isburr! S igenni, akked Win i t ibnan! S tmurt, akked Win ip issewsâan! S teôwiêt, akked Win ip imeslen! Iwehheb as laâwayeô is, aêezzeb is. Ni$ irbeê win ip izzazdgen. Ni$ ixseô win ip itelfen. Tamud nekkôen, di lbe$wv nnsen. Mi d ikker umcum mavi nnsen. Amazan n Öebbi inna yasen: "tal$wemt n Öebbi, ssewwet ep"! Skaddben t; i tel$wemt, gezmen ivaôen. Izâaf fellasen Mass nnsen, ilmend ubekkav nnsen; d$a Isemsawi p. Ur T icqi w ara iûaôen.
سُوۡرَةُ الَّيۡلِ S yiv, mara idell! S wass, mara iôeqq! S wayen Ixleq: ddkeô, nnta! Igiten nnwen, s tidep, mefruzit. Wanag win ipseddiqen, ipêezziben, di tezdeg iumen, ad as Nefk afus ad istiser. Wanag win icuêêen, i isme$wôen iman is, u iskaddeb ayen zeddigen, ad as Negg abrid ar laâûeô. Iwumi yas wayla s, imi ad i$li? Nnhaya, s tidep, fellane£. Ih, taneggarut akked tmezwarut, d ayla nne£. Âaggne$ awen: times d taqesêant. Ara p ikecmen, siwa imceôôi mavi, i iskaddben, u iwexxôen. A p swexxôen i win ipêezziben mavi, i ipseddiqen seg wayla s i tezdeg. Ur ippawi êedd, a$iti s$uôes, siwa ma iô$eb udem n Mass is Aâlayan. War ccekk, deqqal ad Iôavi.
سُوۡرَةُ الضُّحٰي S tafat n tûebêit! S yiv, ma irked! Ur k Iooi Mass ik, ur k Ikrih. Tudert taneggarut ik, a ppif tamezwarut ik. A k tôavi tikci, deqqal, n Mass ik. Day ur k id Iufa ara d agujil, Isduri k? Iufa k id d utlif, Inha k. Iufa k id d igellil, I$at ik. Ihi, ur qehheô agujil. Ur ppara amappar. Wanag, $ef l$it n Mass ik, xas eêku.
سُوۡرَةُ الشَّرۡحِ Day ur ak Ncelleê ara idmaren ik? Nekkes ak taâkkwemt ik, ihban aârur ik. Nefka azal i ism ik. Ih, cedda s talwit. S tidep, cedda s talwit. Ma ur tce$wlev, elhi d laxeôt ik. Eô$eb $ef Mass ik.
سُوۡرَةُ التِّيۡنِ S tme$ôust akked tzemmurt! S udrar n Sina! Akked temdint agi n laman! Ni$ Nxelq ed amdan d ûûam. Sinna, Nerra t d aneggaru ineggura. Kkes ed wid iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan, i nitni arraz imezgi. Ihi, d acu, deffir waya, ara k iskiddben f uqeîîi? Day Öebbi maççi d Imxeyyeô n yimêaddan?
سُوۡرَةُ الۡعَلَقِ £eô, s yisem n Mass ik Ixelqen. Ixleq amdan seg urgen. £eô! Mass ik, Imxeyyeô n wukyisen, i Islemden s umru. Isselmed i umdan, ayen ur issin. Xaîi! War ccekk, ijuô umdan, mi iwala isâa. Ih, ar Mass ik, tu$alin. Twalav win ikksen taéallit i uxdim? Twalav ma illa di nnhaya? Ne$ ma iumeô $eô uêezzeb? Twalav ma iskaddeb, ma iwexxeô? Day ur iéôi ara, ar Öebbi Ipwali? Xaîi! Ma ur iffuk ara, si tgwenza, war ccekk, ara t Neîîef, tagwenza n ubekkav, tuccva. Anef ad isiwel i im²eddukwal. A Nenced iâssasen. Ur s ssemêas, eknu, qeôôeb.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡقَدۡرِ Ni$ Nessader it id deg iv useyyi. Anwa ara k imlen, d acu ay d iv useyyi? Iv useyyi yif agim wagguren. Lmalayek akked ôôuê, ppadren d degs, s wannuf n Mass nnsen, i yal lameô. Di tifrat i illa alamma d tafrara.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡبَيِّنَةِ Ijehliyen seg At Tezmamt, akked imcurak, ur steôoiâen alamma irs ed, $uôsen, ubeggen: Amazan s$uô Öebbi, i immalen tiwôeqtin zeddigen; degsent tira tumâint. Ur myefrazen wid iwumi teppunefk Tezmamt, armi ten id iusa ubeggen. Ppwamôen, kan, ad âabden Öebbi s ddin iûfan, ad malen ar tidep, ad bedden i téallit, ad zzekkin. D wagi ay d ddin umâin. Ih, wid ijehlen, seg At Tezmamt akked imcurak, di tmes n Loahennama ad wekkôen. Widak, d aâar n yimdanen. Ma d wid ippamnen, i xeddmen ayen ilhan, widak d lxetyaô n yimdanen. Arraz nnsen, ar Mass nnsen, d leonanat n Âaden, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen, degsen ad wekkôen, i lebda. Öebbi Iôuva ten, nitni ôuvan T. Akka i win i ippagwaden Mass is.
سُوۡرَةُ الزِّلۡزَالِ Mara tezlez tmurt zzelzla s, U tessuffe$ ed d tmurt, tiâakkwemin is, amdan ad yini: "d acu p iu$en"? A d teêku tidyanin is, assen; akken i s Iweêêa Mass ik. Assen, a d asen imdanen, d igrawen, ar usnaâti igiten nnsen. Win ixedmen taéeyt ubelkim n lxiô, a t iéeô. Win ixedmen taéeyt ubelkim n cceôô, a t iéeô.
سُوۡرَةُ العٰدِيٰتِ S tid id ippazalen neffôent! Ifeîîiwjen, ssafagent. Di tûebêit ara d dehment. A$ebbaô, sskarent. Ar tlemmast n ugraw, kecment. Ih, amdan, i Mass is, d lkaraâ. U neppa, ard anagi n waya. Neppa, s tidep, aîas i iêemmel sâaya! Day ur iéôi ara ar mara d iffe$ i illan deg iéekwan, i illan deg idmaren, a d ivheô meôôa. S tidep, assen, Mass nnsen, ippuxebbeô fellasen.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡقَارِعَةِ Taheûûakt. D acu p theûûakt? Anwa ara k imlen d acu p theûûakt? Ass ideg ara ilin imdanen am iferîeîîa ibruzzâen, u ara ilin idurar, am taduî iqerdcen, d$a, wanag bu lwezn ééayen, ad yili di tmeddurt igerzen. Wanag bu lwezn fessusen, di maylellif ara d igwri. Anwa ara k imlen d acu t? D times ipzehhiren.
سُوۡرَةُ التَّكَاثُرِ Tem$weô tessedha kwen, armi trezfem ar iéekwan. Xaîi! Deqqal a ppissinem. Da$en, xaîi! Deqqal a ppissinem. Xaîi! Lemmer, s tussna itebbten, ara tissinem, war ccekk, times, a p twalim. D$a, s tiî utebbet, ara p twalim. D$a, assen, war ccekk, fellawen asteqsi $ef lhawiyyat.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡعَصۡرِ S wakud! Ih, amdan, war ccekk, ar di lexsaôa. Kkes ed wid iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan, ippemyenhun ar tidep, ippemyenhun ar ûûbeô.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡهُمَزَةِ A ssxev n yal aqeôôav alemmam! I ijemmlen ayla, iêeppeb it. Inwa, s wayla, ad iwekkeô. Xaîi! Ad ippuveggeô ar Tuêvimt. Anwa ara k yinin d acu p Tuêvimt? D times n Öebbi i smendagen, i ippalin $ef ulawen. Neppat, ih, t$umm iten s tgwejda $wezzifen.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡفِيۡلِ Day ur twalav ara amek Ixdem, Mass ik, i At Lfil? Day ur Issexôeb ara tixidas nnsen? Iuzen asen d ifôax ikkaten. ï Ïîeggiôen d fellasen id$a$en iweccmen. Irra ten am alim ipwaféen.
سُوۡرَةُ قُرَيۡشٍ Ilmend n lemwafqa n Qurayc. Lemwafqa nnsen $ef inig unebdu akked win n tegrist. Awufan ad âabden Mass n Uxxam a, iten Iceççen, ur plaéen, iten Ivemnen, ur ppagwaden.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡمَاعُوۡنِ Twalav win inekôen ddin? Winna ipparan agujil akin. Ur t icqi uççi ume$bun. Iméulla, a tawa$it nnsen! Wid istehzayen di téilla nnsen, wid ib$an a ten id walin, u gedlen talalin.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡكَوۡثَرِ Ni$ Nefka yak lufa. èéal i Mass ik, zzlu îêegga. Ih, axûim ik, amengur d neppa.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡكَافِرُوۡنَ Ini: "a yijehliyen! Ur âabde$ ayen tâabdem. Ayen âabde$, kunwi ur t tâabdem. Nek, ur d âabad n ayen tâabdem, Ayen âabde$, kunwi ur t tâabdem. Nekkini, s ddin inu, kunwi s ddin nnwen".
سُوۡرَةُ النَّصۡرِ Ma iusa d l$elb n Öebbi, akked rrbeê. D$a twalav imdanen keççmen ddin n Öebbi, d igrawen. Sbuccaâ s ccekôan Mass ik, ssuter aS ssmaê. Neppa Izga Issuruf.
سُوۡرَةُ اللَهَبِ A nnger ifassen n Abulahab, u a nnegr is! Iwumi yas wayla s, akked wayen ikseb? Ad iôe$ di tmessi m ujajiê, akked tmeîîut is, i ipbibbin as$aô, tamrart inzizen, $ef umgaôv is.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡاِخۡلَاصِ Ini: "Neppa, Öebbi Yiwen. Öebbi, ur T ippissin yiwen. Ur Iuriw, ur T uriwen. Ur illi, d nned iS, yiwen.
سُوۡرَةُ الۡفَلَقِ Ini: "ad iyi Iûûeô, Mass n wanqaô! Si lhemm n wayen Ixelq, si lhemm n tillas ma ssant, si lhemm n tid ipûuvun di tyersiwin, si lhemm um$ecci, ma iusem.
سُوۡرَةُ النَّاسِ Ini: "ad iyi Iûûeô, Mass n yimdanen! Agellid n yimdanen, Öebbi n yimdanen, si lhemm u$way n win ipfezwin, i i$ewwun idmaren n yimdanen, si leonun u seg yimdanen.
